GAMES PEOPLE PLAY

人们玩的游戏

Dr Eric Berne, like his father, graduated from the Faculty of Medicine, McGill University, Montreal, Canada, and later moved to the United States, where he had his internship in psychiatry at the New Haven Hospital and the Yale Institute of Human Relations. He also studied at the New York and San Francisco Psychoanalytic Institutes. During the Second World War he served in the U.S. Army Medical Corps and was discharged with the rank of major. Afterwards he became a consultant in psychiatry and neurology to the Surgeon General of the U.S. Army. He was a practising psychiatrist in Carmel and San Francisco, California, a lecturer at the University of California Medical School, and Consultant in Group Therapy at McAuley Clinic in San Francisco. He was a corresponding member of the Indian Psychiatric Society, chairman of the board of trustees of the International Transactional Analysis Association and editor of the Transactional Analysis Bulletin. He also wrote The Mind in Action, Transactional Analysis in Psychotherapy, The Structure and Dynamics of Organizations and Groups and Principles of Group Treatment. A Layman’s Guide to Psychiatry and Psychoanalysis and Sex in Human Loving are also available in Penguins. While at college he wrote for the Canadian magazine Forum, the London Adelphi, and other periodicals. He died in 1970.

埃里克·伯恩博士和他的父亲一样，毕业于加拿大蒙特利尔麦吉尔大学医学院，之后移居美国，在纽黑文医院和耶鲁大学人际关系研究所完成了精神病学实习。他还曾在纽约和旧金山精神分析研究所进修。二战期间，他曾在美国陆军医疗队服役，并以少校军衔退役。战后，他成为美国陆军军医总监的精神病学和神经病学顾问。他曾在加利福尼亚州卡梅尔和旧金山担任执业精神科医生，并在加州大学医学院担任讲师，同时在旧金山麦考利诊所担任团体治疗顾问。他还是印度精神病学会的通讯会员、国际人际沟通分析协会理事会主席以及《人际沟通分析公报》的编辑。他还著有《行动中的心智》（The Mind in Action）、《心理治疗中的交互分析》（Transactional Analysis in Psychotherapy）、《组织与团体的结构与动力》（The Structure and Dynamics of Organizations and Groups）以及《团体治疗原则》（Principles of Group Treatment）。《精神病学与精神分析入门》（A Layman’s Guide to Psychiatry and Psychoanalysis）和《人类之爱中的性》（Sex in Human Loving）也由企鹅出版社出版。大学期间，他曾为加拿大杂志《论坛》（Forum）、伦敦《阿德尔菲》（Adelphi）及其他期刊撰稿。他于1970年去世。

Preface

前言

T HIS book is primarily designed to be a sequel to my book Transactional Analysis in Psychotherapy , 1 but has been planned so that it can be read and understood independently. The theory necessary for the analysis and clear understanding of games has been summarized in Part I . Part II contains descriptions of the individual games. Part III contains new clinical and theoretical material which, added to the old, makes it possible to understand to some extent what it means to be game-free. Those desiring further background are referred to the earlier volume. The reader of both will note that in addition to the theoretical advances, there have been some minor changes in terminology and viewpoint based on further thinking and reading and new clinical material.

本书主要旨在作为我著作《心理治疗中的交互分析》的续篇，但其结构设计使其可以独立阅读和理解。第一部分总结了分析和清晰理解游戏所需的理论。第二部分描述了各种游戏。第三部分包含新的临床和理论材料，这些材料与原有内容相结合，使读者能够在一定程度上理解“无游戏”的含义。希望了解更多背景知识的读者可以参考前作。两本书的读者都会注意到，除了理论方面的进步之外，基于进一步的思考、阅读和新的临床材料，本书在术语和观点方面也进行了一些细微的调整。

The need for this book was indicated by interested requests from students and lecture audiences for lists of games, or for further elaboration of games mentioned briefly as examples in a general exposition of the principles of transactional analysis. Thanks are due in general to these students and audiences, and especially to the many patients who exposed to view, spotted or named new games; and in particular to Miss Barbara Rosenfeld for her many ideas about the art and meaning of listening; and to Mr Melvin Boyce, Mr Joseph Concannon, Dr Franklin Ernst, Dr Kenneth Everts, Dr Gordon Gritter, Mrs Frances Matson, and Dr Ray Poindexter, among others, for their independent discovery or confirmation of the significance of many games.

本书的出版源于学生和听众的强烈要求，他们希望获得游戏清单，或希望对在人际沟通分析原理概述中简要提及的游戏进行更详细的阐述。在此，我们衷心感谢这些学生和听众，尤其要感谢众多接触过本书、发现或命名新游戏的患者；特别感谢芭芭拉·罗森菲尔德女士，她对倾听的艺术和意义提出了诸多真知灼见；还要感谢梅尔文·博伊斯先生、约瑟夫·康卡农先生、富兰克林·恩斯特博士、肯尼斯·埃弗茨博士、戈登·格里特博士、弗朗西丝·马特森女士和雷·波因德克斯特博士等人，他们独立地发现或证实了许多游戏的意义。

Mr Claude Steiner, formerly Research Director of the San Francisco Social Psychiatry Seminars and presently in the Department of Psychology at the University of Michigan deserves special mention on two counts. He conducted the first experiments which confirmed many of the theoretical points at issue here, and as a result of these experiments he helped considerably in clarifying the nature of autonomy and of intimacy. Thanks are also due to Miss Viola Litt, the Secretary-Treasurer of the Seminars, and to Mrs Mary N. Williams, my personal secretary, for their continued help, and to Anne Garrett for her assistance in reading the proof.

克劳德·施泰纳先生，曾任旧金山社会精神病学研讨会研究主任，现任职于密歇根大学心理学系，在两方面值得特别提及。他开展了首批实验，证实了本文探讨的许多理论观点；这些实验极大地帮助我们阐明了自主性和亲密关系的本质。此外，还要感谢研讨会秘书兼财务主管维奥拉·利特小姐、我的私人秘书玛丽·N·威廉姆斯女士的持续帮助，以及安妮·加勒特女士在校对过程中提供的帮助。

SEMANTICS

语义学

For conciseness, the games are described primarily from the male point of view unless they are clearly feminine. Thus the chief player is usually designated as ‘he’, but without prejudice, since the same situation, unless otherwise indicated, could as easily be outlined with ‘she’, mutatis mutandis. If the woman’s role differs significantly from the man’s, it is treated separately. The therapist is similarly without prejudice designated as ‘he’. The vocabulary and viewpoint are primarily oriented toward the practising clinician, but members of other professions may find this book interesting or useful.

为简洁起见，除非游戏明显具有女性特征，否则游戏描述主要以男性视角为主。因此，主要玩家通常被指代为“他”，但这并不带有偏见，因为除非另有说明，同样的情况也可以用“她”来描述，只需稍作调整即可。如果女性的角色与男性有显著差异，则会单独处理。治疗师同样被指代为“他”，这并不带有偏见。本书的词汇和视角主要面向临床医生，但其他专业人士也可能觉得本书有趣或有用。

Transactional game analysis should be clearly distinguished from its growing sister science of mathematical game analysis, although a few of the terms used in the text, such as ‘payoff’, are now respectably mathematical. For a detailed review of the mathematical theory of games see Games & Decisions, by R. D. Luce and H. Raiffa. 2

交易博弈分析应与日益发展的姊妹学科——数学博弈分析——明确区分开来，尽管文中使用的一些术语，例如“收益”，现在已具有相当的数学意义。有关博弈数学理论的详细回顾，请参阅 R. D. Luce 和 H. Raiffa 合著的《博弈与决策》。

Carmel, California, May 1962

加利福尼亚州卡梅尔，1962年5月

REFERENCES

参考

1. Berne, E.，《心理治疗中的交互分析》，Evergreen出版社，1961年。

#↩

Introduction

介绍

1 · SOCIAL INTERCOURSE

1. 社交互动

T HE theory of social intercourse, which has been outlined at some length in Transactional Analysis, 1 may be summarized as follows.

社会交往理论在《人际沟通分析》中已有详尽阐述， 1 可概括如下。

Spitz has found 2 that infants deprived of handling over a long period will tend at length to sink into an irreversible decline and are prone to succumb eventually to intercurrent disease. In effect, this means that what he calls emotional deprivation can have a fatal outcome. These observations give rise to the idea of stimulus-hunger, and indicate that the most favoured forms of stimuli are those provided by physical intimacy, a conclusion not hard to accept on the basis of everyday experience.

斯皮茨发现，长期缺乏抚触的婴儿最终会陷入不可逆转的衰退，并容易并发其他疾病。实际上，这意味着他所谓的“情感剥夺”可能导致致命后果。这些观察结果引出了“刺激饥渴”的概念，并表明最受欢迎的刺激形式是身体亲密接触所提供的刺激，这一结论基于日常经验并不难理解。

An allied phenomenon is seen in grown-ups subjected to sensory deprivation. Experimentally, such deprivation may call forth a transient psychosis, or at least give rise to temporary mental disturbances; In the past, social and sensory deprivation is noted to have had similar effects in individuals condemned to long periods of solitary imprisonment. Indeed, solitary confinement is one of the punishments most dreaded even by prisoners hardened to physical brutality, 3 , 4 and is now a notorious procedure for inducing political compliance. (Conversely, the best of the known weapons against political compliance is social organization.) 5

在遭受感官剥夺的成年人身上也观察到了类似的现象。实验表明，这种剥夺可能会引发短暂性精神病，或者至少会导致暂时的精神障碍；过去，人们注意到，社交和感官剥夺对被判处长期单独监禁的人会产生类似的影响。事实上，单独监禁是即使是那些对肉体暴行习以为常的囚犯也最为恐惧的刑罚之一，如今已成为一种臭名昭著的诱导政治顺从的手段。（反之，目前已知的对抗政治顺从的最佳武器是社会组织。）

On the biological side, it is probable that emotional and sensory deprivation tends to bring about or encourage organic changes. If the reticular activating system 6 of the brain stem is not sufficiently stimulated, degenerative changes in the nerve cells may follow, at least indirectly. This may be a secondary effect due to poor nutrition, but the poor nutrition itself may be a product of apathy, as in infants suffering from marasmus. Hence a biological chain may be postulated leading from emotional and sensory deprivation through apathy to degenerative changes and death. In this sense, stimulus-hunger has the same relationship to survival of the human organism as food-hunger.

从生物学角度来看，情感和感官剥夺很可能导致或促进机体发生改变。如果脑干网状激活系统（RAS）得不到充分刺激，神经细胞可能会发生退行性改变，至少是间接的。这可能是营养不良的继发效应，但营养不良本身也可能是冷漠的表现，例如患有消瘦症的婴儿。因此，可以推测存在一条生物学链，从情感和感官剥夺经由冷漠最终导致退行性改变和死亡。从这个意义上讲，对刺激的渴望与对食物的渴望一样，都与人类的生存息息相关。

Indeed, not only biologically but also psychologically and socially, stimulus-hunger in many ways parallels the hunger for food. Such terms as malnutrition, satiation, gourmet, gourmand, faddist, ascetic, culinary arts, and good cook are easily transferred from the field of nutrition to the field of sensation. Overstuffing has its parallel in overstimulation. In both spheres, under ordinary conditions where ample supplies are available and a diversified menu is possible, choices will be heavily influenced by an individual’s idiosyncrasies. It is possible that some or many of these idiosyncrasies are constitutionally determined, but this is irrelevant to the problems at issue here.

事实上，不仅在生物学层面，而且在心理学和社会学层面，对刺激的渴望在很多方面都与对食物的渴望相似。诸如营养不良、饱腹感、美食家、饕餮者、时尚达人、苦行僧、烹饪艺术和优秀厨师等术语，很容易从营养学领域转移到感官领域。过度饱腹与过度刺激也有相似之处。在这两个领域，在通常情况下，如果物资充足且菜单多样化，人们的选择将很大程度上受到个人特质的影响。这些特质中的一些或许多可能是由体质决定的，但这与本文讨论的问题无关。

The social psychiatrist’s concern in the matter is with what happens after the infant is separated from his mother in the normal course of growth. What has been said so far may be summarized by the ‘colloquialism’: 7 ‘If you are not stroked, your spinal cord will shrivel up.’ Hence, after the period of close intimacy with the mother is over, the individual for the rest of his life is confronted with a dilemma upon whose horns his destiny and survival are continually being tossed. One horn is the social, psychological and biological forces which stand in the way of continued physical intimacy in the infant style; the other is his perpetual striving for its attainment. Under most conditions he will compromise. He learns to do with more subtle, even symbolic, forms of handling, until the merest nod of recognition may serve the purpose to some extent, although his original craving for physical contact may remain unabated.

社会精神病学家关注的是婴儿在正常成长过程中与母亲分离后会发生什么。以上所述可以用一句俗语概括：“如果你不被抚摸，你的脊髓就会萎缩。” 因此，在与母亲亲密相处的时期结束后，个体终其一生都将面临一个两难困境，其命运和生存都取决于这两个困境。一方面是阻碍婴儿时期身体亲密接触的社会、心理和生物因素；另一方面是他自身对这种亲密接触的持续渴望。在大多数情况下，他会做出妥协。他学会接受更微妙、甚至是象征性的抚触方式，直到一个简单的点头就能在某种程度上起到作用，尽管他最初对身体接触的渴望可能依然存在。

This process of compromise may be called by various terms, such as sublimation; but whatever it is called, the result is a partial transformation of the infantile stimulus-hunger into something which may be termed recognition-hunger. As the complexities of compromise increase, each person becomes more and more individual in his quest for recognition, and it is these differentia which lend variety to social intercourse and which determine the individual’s destiny. A movie actor may require hundreds of strokes each week from anonymous and undifferentiated admirers to keep his spinal cord from shrivelling, while a scientist may keep physically and mentally healthy on one stroke a year from a respected master.

这种妥协过程可以用各种术语来称呼，例如升华；但无论它被称为什么，其结果都是将婴儿时期对刺激的渴望部分地转化为某种可以称之为对认可的渴望。随着妥协的复杂性增加，每个人在寻求认可的过程中变得越来越个性化，正是这些差异赋予了社会交往以多样性，并决定了个人的命运。一个电影演员可能需要每周数百次来自匿名且不加区分的仰慕者的抚摸，以防止脊髓萎缩，而一个科学家可能每年只需一位受人尊敬的导师的一次抚摸就能保持身心健康。

‘Stroking’ may be used as a general term for intimate physical contact; in practice it may take various forms. Some people literally stroke an infant; others hug or pat it, while some people pinch it playfully or flip it with a fingertip. These all have their analogues in conversation, so that it seems one might predict how an individual would handle a baby by listening to him talk. By an extension of meaning, ‘stroking’ may be employed colloquially to denote any act implying recognition of another’s presence. Hence a stroke may be used as the fundamental unit of social action. An exchange of strokes constitutes a transaction, which is the unit of social intercourse.

“抚摸”一词可泛指亲密的身体接触；在实践中，它可以采取多种形式。有些人会真的抚摸婴儿；有些人会拥抱或轻拍婴儿；还有些人会轻轻捏捏婴儿或用指尖翻动婴儿。这些行为在日常对话中都有相应的表现，因此似乎可以通过听一个人说话来预测他会如何对待婴儿。引申而言，“抚摸”一词在口语中也可以用来指代任何表示认可他人存在的行为。因此，抚摸可以作为社会行为的基本单位。抚摸的交换构成了一次互动，而互动则是社会交往的基本单位。

As far as the theory of games is concerned, the principle which emerges here is that any social intercourse whatever has a biological advantage over no intercourse at all. This has been experimentally demonstrated in the case of rats through some remarkable experiments by S. Levine 8 in which not only physical, mental and emotional development but also the biochemistry of the brain and even resistance to leukemia were favourably affected by handling. The significant feature of these experiments was that gentle handling and painful electric shocks were equally effective in promoting the health of the animals.

就博弈论而言，这里引出的原则是，任何形式的社会交往都比完全没有交往具有生物学优势。S. Levine 8 通过对大鼠进行的一系列卓越实验证实了这一点。在这些实验中，人为的抚摸不仅对大鼠的生理、心理和情感发育产生积极影响，而且对大脑的生物化学以及对白血病的抵抗力也产生了积极影响。这些实验的显著特点是，轻柔的抚摸和痛苦的电击在促进动物健康方面同样有效。

This validation of what has been said above encourages us to proceed with increased confidence to the next section.

上述内容的验证鼓励我们更有信心进入下一节。

2 · THE STRUCTURING OF TIME

2. 时间结构

Granted that handling of infants, and its symbolic equivalent in grown-ups, recognition, have a survival value. The question is. What next ? In everyday terms, what can people do after they have exchanged greetings, whether the greeting consists of a collegiate ‘Hi!’ or an Oriental ritual lasting several hours ? After stimulus-hunger and recognition hunger comes structure-hunger. The perennial problem of adolescents is : ‘What do you say to her (him) then ? And to many people besides adolescents, nothing is more uncomfortable than a social hiatus, a period of silent, unstructured time when no one present can think of anything more interesting to say than: ‘Don’t you think the walls are perpendicular tonight ?’ The eternal problem of the human being is how to structure his waking hours. In this existential sense, the function of all social living is to lend mutual assistance for this project.

诚然，抚摸婴儿，以及在成人身上与之对应的象征性认可，都具有生存价值。问题是：接下来呢？在日常生活中，人们在互致问候之后还能做什么？无论这问候是一句简单的“嗨！”，还是持续数小时的东方礼仪？在对刺激和认可的渴望之后，便是对结构的渴望。青少年永恒的难题是：“那你该对她（他）说什么呢？”而对许多人来说，除了青少年之外，没有什么比社交空档期更令人难受的了。在一段沉默、无序的时光里，在场的每个人都想不到比“你不觉得今晚的墙是垂直的吗？”更有趣的话题。人类永恒的难题是如何安排自己的清醒时间。从这个存在主义的意义上讲，所有社会生活的功能都是为了实现这一目标而相互帮助。

The operational aspect of time-structuring may be called programming. It has three aspects: material, social and individual. The most common, convenient, comfortable, and utilitarian method of structuring time is by a project designed to deal with the material of external reality: what is commonly known as work. Such a project is technically called an activity ; the term ‘work’ is unsuitable because a general theory of social psychiatry must recognize that social intercourse is also a form of work.

时间结构的操作层面可以称为规划。它包含三个方面：物质层面、社会层面和个体层面。最常见、最便捷、最舒适、最实用的时间结构方法是通过一个旨在处理外部现实物质的项目来实现的，也就是我们通常所说的工作。这类项目在技术上被称为活动；“工作”一词并不恰当，因为社会精神病学的一般理论必须承认，社会交往也是一种工作形式。

Material programming arises from the vicissitudes encountered in dealing with external reality; it is of interest here only insofar as activities offer a matrix for ‘stroking’, recognition, and other more complex forms of social intercourse. Material programming is not primarily a social problem; in essence it is based on data processing. The activity of building a boat relies on a long series of measurements and probability estimates, and any social exchange which occurs must be subordinated to these in order for the building to proceed.

物质规划源于应对外部现实过程中遇到的种种变故；在此，它之所以重要，仅仅是因为各种活动为“抚慰”、认可和其他更复杂的社会交往形式提供了一个框架。物质规划并非主要是一个社会问题；本质上，它基于数据处理。造船活动依赖于一系列漫长的测量和概率估计，任何发生的社会交流都必须服从于这些，造船才能顺利进行。

Social programming results in traditional ritualistic or semi-ritualistic interchanges. The chief criterion for it is local acceptability, popularly called ‘good manners’. Parents in all parts of the world teach their children manners, which means that they know the proper greeting, eating, emunctory, courting and mourning rituals, and also how to carry on topical conversations with appropriate strictures and reinforcements. The strictures and reinforcements constitute tact or diplomacy, some of which is universal and some local. Belching at meals or asking after another man’s wife are each encouraged or forbidden by local ancestral tradition, and indeed there is a high degree of inverse correlation between these particular transactions. Usually in localities where people belch at meals, it is unwise to ask after the womenfolk; and in localities where people are asking after the womenfolk, it is unwise to belch at meals. Usually formal rituals precede semi-ritualistic topical conversations, and the latter may be distinguished by calling them pastimes.

社会教化造就了传统的仪式性或半仪式性的交流。其主要标准是当地的接受度，俗称“礼仪”。世界各地的父母都会教导孩子礼仪，这意味着他们懂得恰当的问候、用餐、排泄、求爱和哀悼礼节，以及如何以适当的规则和强化方式进行话题对话。这些规则和强化方式构成了社交技巧或外交手腕，其中一些是普遍适用的，一些则具有地域性。在餐桌上打嗝或询问他人妻子的近况，都受到当地传统习俗的鼓励或禁止，事实上，这两种行为之间存在着高度的反比关系。通常在人们会在餐桌上打嗝的地方，询问女性的近况是不明智的；而在人们会询问女性近况的地方，在餐桌上打嗝也是不明智的。通常，正式的仪式先于半仪式性的话题对话，后者可以通过称之为消遣来加以区分。

As people become better acquainted, more and more individual programming creeps in, so that ‘incidents’ begin to occur. These incidents superficially appear to be adventitious, and may be so described by the parties concerned, but careful scrutiny reveals that they tend to follow definite patterns which are amenable to sorting and classification, and that the sequence is circumscribed by unspoken rules and regulations. These regulations remain latent as long as the amities or hostilities proceed according to Hoyle, but they become manifest if an illegal move is made, giving rise to a symbolic, verbal or legal cry of ‘Foul!’ Such sequences, which in contrast to pastimes are based more on individual than on social programming, may be called games. Family life and married life, as well as life in organizations of various kinds, may year after year be based on variations of the same game.

随着人们彼此更加熟悉，越来越多的个人行为模式悄然渗入，于是“事件”开始发生。这些事件表面上看似偶然，相关人员也可能如此描述，但仔细审视便会发现，它们往往遵循着明确的模式，可以进行分类整理，而且其发展过程受到不成文规则的制约。只要友好或敌对关系按照霍伊尔的理论发展，这些规则就保持潜伏状态；但一旦出现违规行为，这些规则就会显露出来，引发象征性的、口头的或法律上的“犯规！”的叫喊。与消遣娱乐不同，这类基于个人而非社会行为模式的事件序列可以被称为游戏。家庭生活、婚姻生活以及各种组织中的生活，可能年复一年地基于同一场游戏的不同变体。

To say that the bulk of social activity consists of playing games does not necessarily mean that it is mostly ‘fun’ or that the parties are not seriously engaged in the relationship. On the one hand, ‘playing’ football and other athletic ‘games’ may not be fun at all, and the players may be intensely grim; and such games share with gambling and other forms of ‘play’ the potentiality for being very serious indeed, sometimes fatal. On the other hand, some authors for instance Huizinga, 9 include under ‘play’ such serious things as cannibal feasts. Hence calling such tragic behaviour as suicide, alcohol and drug addiction, criminality or schizophrenia ‘playing games’ is not irresponsible, facetious or barbaric. The essential characteristic of human play is not that the emotions are spurious, but that they are regulated. This is revealed when sanctions are imposed on an illegitimate emotional display. Play may be grimly serious, or even fatally serious, but the social sanctions are serious only if the rules are broken.

说大部分社交活动都由玩游戏构成，并不一定意味着这些游戏大多是“娱乐”，或者参与者对彼此关系不够认真。一方面，“玩”足球和其他体育“游戏”可能一点也不好玩，参与者也可能非常严肃；这类游戏与赌博和其他形式的“游戏”一样，都可能变得非常严重，有时甚至致命。另一方面，一些作者，例如胡伊津加（Huizinga），将诸如食人盛宴之类的严肃行为也归类为“游戏”。因此，将自杀、酗酒吸毒、犯罪或精神分裂症等悲剧行为称为“玩游戏”并非不负责任、轻佻或野蛮。人类游戏的本质特征不在于情感的虚假，而在于情感的调节。这一点在对不正当的情感表达施加制裁时便得以体现。游戏可能非常严肃，甚至非常危险，但只有违反规则才会受到严重的社会制裁。

Pastimes and games are substitutes for the real living of real intimacy. Because of this they may be regarded as preliminary engagements rather than as unions, which is why they are characterized as poignant forms of play. Intimacy begins when individual (usually instinctual) programming becomes more intense, and both social patterning and ulterior restrictions and motives begin to give way. It is the only completely satisfying answer to stimulus-hunger, recognition-hunger and structure-hunger. Its prototype is the act of loving impregnation.

消遣和游戏是真实亲密关系的替代品。正因如此，它们可以被视为初步的交往而非真正的结合，这也是为什么它们被认为是令人心酸的游戏形式。亲密关系始于个体（通常是本能的）行为模式变得更加强烈之时，此时社会模式以及潜在的限制和动机都开始瓦解。它是对刺激渴望、认可渴望和结构渴望的唯一完全满足的答案。它的原型是充满爱意的孕育行为。

Structure-hunger has the same survival value as stimulus-hunger. Stimulus-hunger and recognition-hunger express the need to avoid sensory and emotional starvation, both of which lead to biological deterioration. Structure-hunger expresses the need to avoid boredom, and Kierkegaard 10 has pointed out the evils which result from unstructured time. If it persists for any length of time, boredom becomes synonymous with emotional starvation and can have the same consequences.

结构渴望与刺激渴望具有相同的生存价值。刺激渴望和认同渴望表达了避免感官和情感匮乏的需求，而这两者都会导致生理机能的衰退。结构渴望表达了避免无聊的需求，克尔凯郭尔曾指出缺乏结构的时间会带来诸多弊端。如果无聊持续一段时间，它就会等同于情感匮乏，并可能导致相同的后果。

The solitary individual can structure time in two ways: activity and fantasy. An individual can remain solitary even in the presence of others, as every schoolteacher knows. When one is a member of a social aggregation of two or more people, there are several options for structuring time. In order of complexity, these are: (1) Rituals; (2) Pastimes; (3) Games; (4) Intimacy; and (5) Activity, which may form a matrix for any of the others. The goal of each member of the aggregation is to obtain as many satisfactions as possible from his transactions with other members. The more accessible he is, the more satisfactions he can obtain. Most of the programming of his social operations is automatic. Since some of the ‘satisfactions’ obtained under this programming, such as self-destructive ones, are difficult to recognize in the usual sense of the word ‘satisfactions’, it would be better to substitute some more non-committal term, such as ‘gains’ or ‘advantages’.

独处者可以通过两种方式安排时间：活动和幻想。正如每位教师都知道的那样，即使身处他人之中，一个人仍然可以保持独处。当一个人成为由两人或多人组成的社会群体的一员时，他/她就有了多种安排时间的选择。按复杂程度排序，这些选择包括：（1）仪式；（2）消遣；（3）游戏；（4）亲密关系；以及（5）活动，这些活动可以构成其他任何一种活动的基础。群体中每个成员的目标都是从与其他成员的互动中获得尽可能多的满足感。他/她越容易被他人接触，就能获得越多的满足感。他/她的大部分社交活动都是自动进行的。由于在这种自动模式下获得的某些“满足感”（例如自我毁灭性的满足感）难以用通常意义上的“满足感”来定义，因此最好使用一些更宽泛的词语来代替，例如“收益”或“好处”。

The advantages of social contact revolve around somatic and psychic equilibrium. They are related to the following factors: (1) the relief of tension; (2) the avoidance of noxious situations; (3) the procurement of stroking; and (4) the maintenance of an established equilibrium. All these items have been investigated and discussed in great detail by physiologists, psychologists, and psychoanalysts. Translated into terms of social psychiatry, they may be stated as (1) the primary internal advantages; (2) the primary external advantages; (3) the secondary advantages; and (4) the existential advantages. The first three parallel the ‘gains from illness’ described by Freud: the internal paranosic gain, the external paranosic gain, and the epinosic gain, respectively. 11 Experience has shown that it is more useful and enlightening to investigate social transactions from the point of view of the advantages gained than to treat them as defensive operations. In the first place, the best defence is to engage in no transactions at all; in the second place, the concept of ‘defences’ covers only part of the first two classes of advantages, and the rest of them, together with the third and fourth classes, are lost to this point of view.

社交接触的益处围绕着身心平衡展开。这些益处与以下因素相关：(1) 缓解紧张；(2) 避免有害情境；(3) 获得抚慰；(4) 维持已建立的平衡。生理学家、心理学家和精神分析学家已对所有这些方面进行了深入研究和探讨。从社会精神病学的角度来看，这些益处可概括为：(1) 主要内在益处；(2) 主要外在益处；(3) 次要益处；(4) 存在性益处。前三者分别与弗洛伊德描述的“疾病获益”相对应：内在偏执获益、外在偏执获益和外在偏执获益。经验表明，从获益的角度研究社交互动比将其视为防御行为更有用，也更有启发性。首先，最好的防御就是根本不进行任何交易；其次，“防御”的概念只涵盖了前两类优势的一部分，其余的优势，连同第三类和第四类优势，在这种观点下都被忽略了。

The most gratifying forms of social contact, whether or not they are embedded in a matrix of activity, are games and intimacy. Prolonged intimacy is rare, and even then it is primarily a private matter; significant social intercourse most commonly takes the form of games, and that is the subject which principally concerns us here. For further information about time-structuring, the author’s book on group dynamics should be consulted. 12

无论是否融入某种活动体系，最令人愉悦的社交形式是游戏和亲密关系。持久的亲密关系并不常见，即便存在，也主要是一种私人行为；重要的社交互动通常以游戏的形式出现，而这正是我们在此主要关注的主题。关于时间结构的更多信息，请参阅作者关于群体动力学的著作。

Freud, S., ‘Analysis of a Case of Hysteria’, ibid., VI , 1953.

弗洛伊德，S.，《癔症病例分析》，同上，第六卷，1953年。

12. Berne, E., The Structure and Dynamics of Organizations and Groups , Pitman Medical, 1963.

12. Berne, E.，《组织和群体的结构与动力》，Pitman Medical，1963 年。

#↩

PART ONE

第一部分

#↩

ANALYSIS OF GAMES

游戏分析

#↩

1 · Structural Analysis

1. 结构分析

O BESERVATION of spontaneous social activity, most productively carried out in certain kinds of psychotherapy groups, reveals that from time to time people show noticeable changes in posture, view-point, voice, vocabulary, and other aspects of behaviour. These behavioural changes are often accompanied by shifts in feeling. In a given individual, a certain set of behaviour patterns corresponds to one state of mind, while another set is related to a different psychic attitude, often inconsistent with the first. These changes and differences give rise to the idea of ego states.

对自发性社会活动的观察，尤其是在某些心理治疗小组中进行的观察，揭示了人们的姿势、观点、语调、词汇和其他行为方面会不时发生显著变化。这些行为变化通常伴随着情绪的转变。对于特定个体而言，某些行为模式对应着一种心理状态，而另一组行为模式则与另一种心理状态相关，后者往往与前者不一致。这些变化和差异催生了自我状态的概念。

In technical language, an ego state may be described phenome-nologically as a coherent system of feelings, and operationally as a set of coherent behaviour patterns. In more practical terms, it is a system of feelings accompanied by a related set of behaviour patterns. Each individual seems to have available a limited repertoire of such ego states, which are not roles but psychological realities. This repertoire can be sorted into the following categories: (1) ego states which resemble those of parental figures; (2) ego states which are autonomously directed towards objective appraisal of reality and (3) those which represent archaic relics, still-active ego states which were fixated in early childhood. Technically these are called, respectively, exteropsychic, neopsychic, and archaeopsychic ego states. Colloquially their exhibitions are called Parent, Adult and Child, and these simple terms serve for all but the most formal discussions.

从技术角度来说，自我状态可以从现象学上描述为一个连贯的情感系统，也可以从操作层面描述为一套连贯的行为模式。更实际地说，它是一个伴随一系列相关行为模式的情感系统。每个人似乎都拥有有限的自我状态库，这些状态并非角色，而是心理现实。这些状态库可以分为以下几类：（1）类似于父母形象的自我状态；（2）自主地指向对现实进行客观评价的自我状态；（3）代表古老遗迹的自我状态，即在童年早期固着的、至今仍然活跃的自我状态。从技术角度来说，这些状态分别被称为外在心理自我状态、新心理自我状态和古心理自我状态。在日常用语中，它们的表现形式分别被称为父母、成人和儿童，这些简单的术语适用于除最正式的讨论之外的所有情况。

The position is, then, that at any given moment each individual in a social aggregation will exhibit a Parental, Adult or Child ego state, and that individuals can shift with varying degrees of readiness from one ego state to another. These observations give rise to certain diagnostic statements. ‘That is your Parent’ means: ‘You are now in the same state of mind as one of your parents (or a parental substitute) used to be, and you are responding as he would, with the same posture, gestures, vocabulary, feelings, etc’ ‘That is your Adult’ means: ‘You have just made an autonomous, objective appraisal of the situation and are stating these thought-processes, or the problems you perceive, or the conclusions you have come to, in a non-prejudicial manner.’ ‘That is your Child’ means: ‘The manner and intent of your reaction is the same as it would have been when you were a very little boy or girl.’

因此，这种观点认为，在任何特定时刻，社会群体中的每个个体都会展现出父母、成人或儿童三种自我状态，并且个体可以从一种自我状态转换到另一种自我状态，转换的准备程度各不相同。这些观察结果引出了一些诊断性陈述。“那是你的父母状态”意味着：“你现在的心理状态与你的父母（或父母的替代者）曾经的心理状态相同，你的反应也与他/她相同，包括相同的姿势、手势、词汇、感受等等。”“那是你的成人状态”意味着：“你刚刚对当前情况进行了自主、客观的评估，并且正在以不带偏见的方式陈述这些思考过程、你感知到的问题或你得出的结论。”“那是你的儿童状态”意味着：“你的反应方式和意图与你还是个小男孩或小女孩时的反应方式相同。”

The implications are:

其含义是：

1. That every individual has had parents (or substitute parents) and that he carries within him a set of ego states that reproduce the ego states of those parents (as he perceived them), and that these parental ego states can be activated under certain circumstances (exteropsychic functioning). Colloquially: ‘Everyone carries his parents around inside of him.’

1. 每个人都曾有过父母（或替代父母），并且他内心都蕴藏着一套自我状态，这些自我状态再现了父母的自我状态（以他所感知到的方式），而且这些父母的自我状态可以在特定情况下被激活（外在心理功能）。通俗地说：“每个人内心都带着父母。”

2. That every individual (including children, the mentally retarded and schizophrenics) is capable of objective data processing if the appropriate ego state can be activated (neopsychic functioning) Colloquially: ‘Everyone has an Adult.’

2. 每个人（包括儿童、智力低下者和精神分裂症患者）如果能够激活适当的自我状态（新心理功能），就能够进行客观数据处理。通俗地说：“每个人都有一个成年人。”

3. That every individual was once younger than he is now, and that he carries within him fixated relics from earlier years which will be activated under certain circumstances (archaeopsychic functioning). Colloquially: ‘Everyone carries a little boy or girl around inside of him.’

3. 每个人都曾比现在更年轻，并且体内都保留着早年岁月的痕迹，这些痕迹会在特定情况下被激活（古心理功能）。通俗地说：“每个人心中都住着一个小男孩或小女孩。”

At this point it is appropriate to draw Figure 1A, which is called a structural diagram. This represents, from the present viewpoint, a diagram of the complete personality of any individual. It includes his Parental, Adult, and Child ego states. They are carefully segregated from each other, because they are so different and because they are so often quite inconsistent with each other. The distinctions may not be clear at first to an inexperienced observer, but soon become impressive and interesting to anyone who takes the trouble to learn structural diagnosis. It will be convenient henceforth to call actual people parents, adults or children, with no capital letters; Parent, Adult and Child, capitalized, will be used when ego states are referred to. Figure 1B represents a convenient, simplified form of the structural diagram.

此时，绘制图1A（结构图）是合适的。从目前的视角来看，它代表了任何个体的完整人格图，包括其父母、成人和儿童三种自我状态。这些状态被仔细区分，因为它们截然不同，而且常常彼此矛盾。对于缺乏经验的观察者来说，这些区别起初可能并不清晰，但对于任何愿意花时间学习结构诊断的人来说，很快就会变得令人印象深刻且饶有趣味。为了方便起见，今后在称呼实际人物时，我们将使用首字母小写的“父母”、“成人”或“儿童”；而“父母”、“成人”和“儿童”则在提及自我状态时使用首字母大写。图1B展示了结构图的简化版本。

Before we leave the subject of structural analysis, certain complications should be mentioned.

在结束结构分析这一主题之前，应该提及一些复杂情况。

1. The word ‘childish’ is never used in structural analysis, since it has come to have strong connotations of undesirability, and of something to be stopped forthwith or got rid of. The term ‘childlike’ is used in describing the Child (an archaic ego state), since it is more biological and not prejudicial. Actually the Child is in many ways the most valuable part of the personality, and can contribute to the individual’s life exactly what an actual child can contribute to family life: charm, pleasure and creativity. If the Child in the individual is confused and unhealthy, then the consequences may be unfortunate, but something can and should be done about it.

1. 在结构分析中，我们从不使用“幼稚”一词，因为它带有强烈的贬义，仿佛某种东西需要立即制止或消除。描述“孩童般”则用“孩子气”来指代孩童（一种古老的自我状态），因为它更贴近生物学，也更不带偏见。事实上，孩童在很多方面都是人格中最宝贵的部分，它能为个体的生活带来如同真实孩童为家庭生活带来的那种魅力、快乐和创造力。如果个体的孩童状态混乱且不健康，那么后果可能不堪设想，但我们可以也应该采取措施来改善这种情况。

2. The same applies to the words ‘mature’ and ‘immature’. In this system there is no such thing as an ‘immature person’. There are only people in whom the Child takes over inappropriately or unproductively, but all such people have a complete, well-structured Adult which only needs to be uncovered or activated. Conversely, so-called ‘mature people’ are people who are able to keep the Adult in control most of the time, but their Child will take over on occasion like anyone else’s, often with disconcerting results.

2. 同样适用于“成熟”和“不成熟”这两个词。在这个体系中，并不存在“不成熟的人”这种说法。只有一些人，他们的“孩子”本能会不恰当或无益地占据主导地位，但所有这些人内心都拥有一个完整、结构良好的“成人”本能，只需要将其发掘或激活即可。相反，所谓的“成熟的人”是指那些大部分时间都能让“成人”本能保持控制的人，但他们的“孩子”本能偶尔也会像其他人一样占据主导地位，而且往往会带来令人不安的后果。

Figure 1. A Structure Diagram

图 1. 结构图

3. It should be noted that the Parent is exhibited in two forms, direct and indirect: as an active ego state, and as an influence. When it is directly active, the person responds as his own father (or mother) actually responded (‘Do as I do’). When it is an indirect influence, he responds the way they wanted him to respond (‘Don’t do as I do, do as I say’). In the first case he becomes one of them; in the second, he adapts himself to their requirements.

3. 需要注意的是，“父母”特质以两种形式展现：直接的和间接的；一种是主动的自我状态，另一种是间接的影响。当“父母”特质直接主动时，个体的回应方式如同其亲生父亲（或母亲）的实际回应方式（“照我做的做”）。当“父母”特质以间接影响的方式出现时，个体的回应方式则取决于“父母”希望他如何回应（“不要照我做的做，要照我说的做”）。在前一种情况下，个体融入了“父母”的圈子；在后一种情况下，个体则适应了“父母”的要求。

4. Thus the Child is also exhibited in two forms: the adapted Child and the natural Child. The adapted Child is the one who modifies his behaviour under the Parental influence. He behaves as father (or mother) wanted him to behave: compliantly or precociously, for example. Or he adapts himself by withdrawing or whining. Thus the Parental influence is a cause, and the adapted Child an effect. The natural Child is a spontaneous expression: rebellion or creativity, for example. A confirmation of structural analysis is seen in the results of alcohol intoxication. Usually this decommissions the Parent first, so that the adapted Child is freed of the Parental influence, and is transformed by release into the natural Child.

4. 因此，儿童也以两种形式展现：适应型儿童和自然型儿童。适应型儿童是指在父母影响下改变自身行为的儿童。他/她会按照父亲（或母亲）的期望行事：例如，顺从或早熟。或者，他/她会通过退缩或抱怨来适应。因此，父母的影响是原因，而适应型儿童是结果。自然型儿童则是一种自发的表达：例如，反叛或创造力。酒精中毒的结果印证了结构分析。通常，酒精首先会削弱父母的影响，从而使适应型儿童摆脱父母的影响，并通过释放转化为自然型儿童。

It is seldom necessary, for effective game analysis, to go beyond what has been outlined above as far as personality structure is concerned.

对于有效的比赛分析而言，就人格结构而言，很少需要超出上述概述的范围。

Ego states are normal physiological phenomena. The human brain is the organ or organizer of psychic life, and its products are organized and stored in the form of ego states. There is already concrete evidence for this in some findings of Penfield and his associates. 1 , 2 There are other sorting systems at various levels, such as factual memory, but the natural form of experience itself is in shifting states of mind. Each type of ego state has its own vital value for the human organism.

自我状态是正常的生理现象。人脑是心理生活的器官或组织者，其产物以自我状态的形式组织和存储。彭菲尔德及其同事的一些研究成果已为此提供了确凿的证据。 1 , 2 在不同层面上还存在其他分类系统，例如事实记忆，但体验本身的自然形式是不断变化的心理状态。每一种自我状态对人体都具有其独特的生命价值。

In the Child reside intuition, 3 creativity and spontaneous drive and enjoyment.

儿童身上蕴藏着直觉、创造力、自发的动力和乐趣。

The Adult is necessary for survival. It processes data and computes the probabilities which are essential for dealing effectively with the outside world. It also experiences its own kinds of setbacks and gratifications. Crossing a busy highway, for example, requires the processing of a complex series of velocity data; action is suspended until the computations indicate a high degree of probability for reaching the other side safely. The gratifications offered by successful computations of this type afford some of the joys of skiing, flying, sailing, and other mobile sports. Another task of the Adult is to regulate the activities of the Parent and the Child, and to mediate objectively between them.

成人是生存的必要条件。它处理数据并计算概率，这对于有效应对外部世界至关重要。它自身也会经历各种挫折和满足。例如，穿越繁忙的公路需要处理一系列复杂的速度数据；只有当计算结果表明安全到达对面的概率很高时，行动才会停止。成功计算带来的满足感，类似于滑雪、飞行、帆船和其他移动运动的乐趣。成人的另一项任务是调节父母和孩子的活动，并在两者之间进行客观的调解。

The Parent has two main functions. First, it enables the individual to act effectively as the parent of actual children, thus promoting the survival of the human race. Its value in this respect is shown by the fact that in raising children, people orphaned in infancy seem to have a harder time than those from homes unbroken into adolescence. Secondly, it makes many responses automatic, which conserves a great deal of time and energy. Many things are done because ‘That’s the way it’s done.’ This frees the Adult from the necessity of making innumerable trivial decisions, so that it can devote itself to more important issues, leaving routine matters to the Parent.

“父母”这一概念具有两大主要功能。首先，它使个体能够有效地扮演父母的角色，养育子女，从而促进人类的延续。其价值体现在这样一个事实：在养育子女方面，幼年丧亲者似乎比那些在完整家庭中成长至青春期的人更加艰难。其次，它使许多反应自动化，从而节省了大量的时间和精力。许多事情之所以能够完成，是因为“理所当然”。这使得成年人无需再为无数琐碎的决定而烦恼，从而能够专注于更重要的事情，将日常事务留给“父母”这一概念。

Thus all three aspects of the personality have a high survival and living value, and it is only when one or the other of them disturbs the healthy balance that analysis and reorganization are indicated. Otherwise each of them, Parent, Adult, and Child, is entitled to equal respect and has its legitimate place in a full and productive life.

因此，人格的这三个方面都具有很高的生存和生活价值，只有当其中任何一个方面打破了健康的平衡时，才需要进行分析和重组。否则，父母、成人和儿童这三个方面都应受到同等的尊重，并在充实而富有成效的生活中占据其应有的位置。

REFERENCES

参考

1. Penfield, W., ‘记忆机制’,《神经病学与精神病学文献》, 67: 178–198,1952。

2. Penfield, W., and Jasper, H., Epilepsy and the Functional Anatomy of the Human Brain, Churchill, 1954, Chapter 11.

2. Penfield, W. 和 Jasper, H.，《癫痫与人脑的功能解剖》，丘吉尔出版社，1954 年，第 11 章。
