#↩

2 · Transactional Analysis

2. 交易分析

T HE unit of social intercourse is called a transaction. If two or more people encounter each other in a social aggregation, sooner or later one of them will speak, or give some other indication of acknowledging the presence of the others. This is called the transactional stimulus. Another person will then say or do something which is in some way related to this stimulus, and that is called the trans actional response. Simple transactional analysis is concerned with diagnosing which ego state implemented the transactional stimulus, and which one executed the transactional response. The simplest transactions are those in which both stimulus and response arise from the Adults of the parties concerned. The agent, estimating from the data before him that a scalpel is now the instrument of choice, holds out his hand. The respondent appraises this gesture correctly, estimates the forces and distances involved, and places the handle of the scalpel exactly where the surgeon expects it. Next in simplicity are Child-Parent transactions. The fevered child asks for a glass of water, and the nurturing mother brings it.

社会交往的基本单位称为“交易”。如果两个人或多人在社交场合相遇，迟早其中一人会开口说话，或以其他方式表示对其他人存在的认可。这被称为交易刺激。随后，另一人会说或做一些与此刺激相关的事情，这被称为交易反应。简单的交易分析旨在诊断是哪种自我状态触发了交易刺激，又是哪种自我状态执行了交易反应。最简单的交易是那些刺激和反应都源于相关各方成年人状态的交易。例如，行动者根据眼前的信息判断手术刀是最佳工具，于是伸出手。被行动者正确地评估了这一动作，估计了其中涉及的力和距离，并将手术刀的刀柄准确地放在了外科医生预期的位置。其次是亲子交易。例如，发烧的孩子要了一杯水，慈爱的母亲便递给了他。

Both these transactions are complementary; that is, the response is appropriate and expected and follows the natural order of healthy human relationships. The first, which is classified as Complementary Transaction Type I, is represented in Figure 2A. The second, Complementary Transaction Type II, is shown in Figure 2B. It is evident, however, that transactions tend to proceed in chains, so that each response is in turn a stimulus. The first rule of communication is that communication will proceed smoothly as long as transactions are complementary; and its corollary is that as long as transactions are complementary, communication can, in principle, proceed indefinitely. These rules are independent of the nature and content of the transactions; they are based entirely on the direction of the vectors involved. As long as the transactions are complementary, it is irrelevant to the rule whether two people are engaging in critical gossip (Parent-Parent), solving a problem (Adult-Adult), or playing together (Child-Child or Parent-Child).

这两种互动都是互补的；也就是说，回应是恰当且符合预期的，并且遵循健康的人际关系的自然顺序。第一种互动被归类为互补互动类型 I，如图 2A 所示。第二种互动，即互补互动类型 II，如图 2B 所示。然而，显而易见的是，互动往往呈链式进行，因此每个回应反过来又会成为一种刺激。沟通的第一条规则是，只要互动是互补的，沟通就能顺利进行；其推论是，只要互动是互补的，原则上沟通就可以无限进行下去。这些规则与互动的性质和内容无关；它们完全基于所涉及的向量的方向。只要互动是互补的，那么两个人是在进行批评性的八卦（父母之间）、解决问题（成人之间）还是一起玩耍（儿童之间或父母之间）都与这条规则无关。

The converse rule is that communication is broken off when a crossed transaction occurs. The most common crossed transaction, and the one which causes and always has caused most of the social difficulties in the world, whether in marriage, love, friendship, or work, is represented in Figure 3A as Crossed Transaction Type I. This type of transaction is the principal concern of psychotherapists and is typified by the classical transference reaction of psychoanalysis. The stimulus is Adult-Adult: e.g., ‘Maybe we should find out why you’ve been drinking more lately,’ or, ‘Do you know where my cuff links are?’ The appropriate Adult-Adult response in each case would be: ‘Maybe we should. I’d certainly like to know!’ or, ‘On the desk.’ If the respondent flares up, however, the responses will be something like ‘You’re always criticizing me, just like my father did,’ or, ‘You always blame me for everything.’ These are both Child-Parent responses, and as the transactional diagram shows, the vectors cross. In such cases the Adult problems about drinking or cuff links must be suspended until the vectors can be realigned. This may take anywhere from several months in the drinking example to a few seconds in the case of the cuff links. Either the agent must become Parental as a complement to the respondent’s suddenly activated Child, or the respondent’s Adult must be reactivated as a complement to the agent’s Adult. If the maid rebels during a discussion of dishwashing, the Adult-Adult conversation about dishes is finished; there can only ensue either a Child-Parent discourse, or a discussion of a different Adult subject, namely her continued employment.

反之，当发生交叉互动时，沟通就会中断。最常见的交叉互动，也是造成（并且一直以来都是造成）世界上大多数社会问题的原因，无论是在婚姻、爱情、友谊还是工作中，如图3A所示的交叉互动类型I。这种类型的互动是心理治疗师主要关注的问题，其典型特征是精神分析中的经典移情反应。刺激是成人对成人的互动，例如，“也许我们应该弄清楚你最近为什么喝得这么多”，或者，“你知道我的袖扣在哪儿吗？”在每种情况下，恰当的成人对成人的回应是：“也许我们应该。我当然想知道！”或者，“在桌子上。”然而，如果被回应者情绪激动，回应就会变成“你总是批评我，就像我父亲一样”，或者，“你总是把一切都怪罪到我头上。”这些都是儿童对父母的回应，正如互动图所示，向量发生了交叉。在这种情况下，关于饮酒或袖扣等成人层面的问题必须暂时搁置，直到双方的诉求方向重新调整。饮酒的例子可能需要几个月，而袖扣的例子可能只需要几秒钟。要么施事者必须转变为父母角色，以补充被诉者突然激活的儿童角色；要么被诉者的成人角色必须重新激活，以补充施事者的成人角色。如果女佣在讨论洗碗时反抗，那么关于洗碗的成人对话就结束了；接下来只能有两种对话：要么是儿童角色与父母角色的对话，要么是讨论另一个成人话题，即她是否继续工作。

Figure 2. Complementary Transactions

图 2. 互补交易

The converse of Crossed Transaction Type I is illustrated in Figure 3B. This is the counter-transference reaction familiar to psychotherapists, in which the patient makes an objective, Adult observation, and the therapist crosses the vectors by responding like a parent talking to a child. This is Crossed Transaction Type II. In everyday life, ‘Do you know where my cuff links are?’ may elicit: ‘Why don’t you keep track of your own things? You’re not a child any more.’

图 3B 展示了交叉交易类型 I 的逆向情况。这是心理治疗师熟悉的逆移情反应：患者做出客观的、成人式的观察，而治疗师则像父母对待孩子一样回应，从而打破了角色间的平衡。这就是交叉交易类型 II。在日常生活中，“你知道我的袖扣在哪儿吗？”可能会引发这样的反应：“你为什么不自己保管好东西？你又不是小孩子了。”

Figure 3. Crossed Transactions

图 3. 交叉交易

The relationship diagram in Figure 4 , showing the nine possible vectors of social action between an agent and a respondent, has some interesting geometrical (topological) qualities. Complementary transactions between ‘psychological equals’ are represented by (1–1) 2 , (5–5) 2 and (9–9) 2 . There are three other complementary transactions: (2–4) (4–2), (3–7) (7–3) and (6–8) (8–6). All other combinations form crossed transactions, and in most cases these show up as crossings in the diagram: e.g., (3–7) (3–7), which results in two speechless people glaring at each other. If neither of them gives way, communication is finished and they must part. The most common solutions are for one to yield and take (7–3), which results in a game of ‘Uproar’; or better, (5–5) 2 , in which case they both burst out laughing or shake hands.

图 4 中的关系图展示了主体和回应者之间九种可能的社会行为向量，它具有一些有趣的几何（拓扑）特征。“心理平等者”之间的互补互动由 (1–1) 2 、(5–5) 2 和 (9–9) 2 表示。还有三种其他互补互动：(2–4) (4–2)、(3–7) (7–3) 和 (6–8) (8–6)。所有其他组合都构成交叉互动，在大多数情况下，这些交叉互动在图中表现为交叉点，例如 (3–7) (3–7)，这会导致两个人怒目而视，一言不发。如果双方都不让步，沟通就此结束，他们必须分开。最常见的解决方案是一方让步并接受 (7–3)，这会导致一场“喧闹”游戏；或者更好，(5–5) 2 ，在这种情况下，他们都会大笑或握手。

Simple complementary transactions most commonly occur in superficial working and social relationships, and these are easily disturbed by simple crossed transactions. In fact a superficial relationship may be defined as one which is confined to simple complementary transactions. Such relationships occur in activities, rituals and pastimes. More complex are ulterior transactions – those involving the activity of more than two ego states simultaneously – and this category is the basis for games. Salesmen are particularly adept at angular transactions, those involving three ego states. A crude but dramatic example of a sales game is illustrated in the following exchange:

简单的互补交易最常发生在肤浅的工作和社交关系中，而这种关系很容易被简单的交叉交易所扰乱。事实上，肤浅的关系可以定义为仅限于简单互补交易的关系。这类关系存在于各种活动、仪式和消遣中。更复杂的是隐秘交易——涉及两种以上自我状态同时运作的交易——而这类交易正是博弈的基础。销售人员尤其擅长多角度交易，即涉及三种自我状态的交易。以下对话就是一个粗略但生动的销售博弈示例：

Figure 4. A Relationship Diagram

图 4. 关系图

Salesman: ‘This one is better, but you can’t afford it.’

销售员：“这款更好，但是你买不起。”

Housewife: ‘That’s the one I’ll take.’

家庭主妇：“我就选这个。”

The analysis of this transaction is shown in Figure 5A. The salesman, as Adult, states two objective facts: ‘This one is better’ and ‘You can’t afford it’. At the ostensible, or social, level these are directed to the Adult of the housewife, whose Adult reply would be: ‘You are correct on both counts.’ However, the ulterior, or psychological, vector is directed by the well-trained and experienced Adult of the salesman to the housewife’s Child. The correctness of his judgement is demonstrated by the Child’s reply, which says in effect: ‘Regardless of the financial consequences, I’ll show that arrogant fellow I’m as good as any of his customers.’ At both levels the transaction is complementary, since her reply is accepted at face value as an Adult purchasing contract.

图 5A 展示了对这笔交易的分析。销售员作为“成人”，陈述了两个客观事实：“这个更好”和“你买不起”。在表面上，或者说社会层面，这些陈述是针对家庭主妇的“成人”层面，而家庭主妇的“成人”层面的回应是：“你说的都对。”然而，销售员作为训练有素、经验丰富的“成人”，其更深层的“心理”层面则指向家庭主妇的“孩子”层面。“孩子”的回应证明了他判断的正确性，这实际上是在说：“不管经济后果如何，我都要让那个傲慢的家伙知道，我跟他的任何一个顾客一样好。”在两个层面上，这笔交易都是互补的，因为她的回应被当作一份“成人”层面的购买合同而接受。

Figure 5. Ulterior Transactions

图 5. 幕后交易

A duplex ulterior transaction involves four ego states, and is commonly seen in flirtation games.

双重隐瞒交易涉及四个自我状态，常见于调情游戏中。

Cowboy: ‘Come and see the barn.’

牛仔：“快来看看谷仓。”

Visitor: ‘I’ve loved barns ever since I was a little girl.’

游客：“我从小就喜欢谷仓。”

As shown in Figure 5B, at the social level this is an Adult conversation about barns, and at the psychological level it is a Child conversation about sex play. On the surface the Adult seems to have the initiative, but as in most games, the outcome is determined by the Child, and the participants may be in for a surprise.

如图 5B 所示，从社会层面来看，这是一场成人关于谷仓的对话；而从心理层面来看，这是一场儿童关于性游戏的对话。表面上看，成人似乎掌握了主动权，但如同大多数游戏一样，最终结果由儿童决定，参与者可能会感到意外。

Transactions may be classified, then, as complementary or crossed, simple or ulterior, and ulterior transactions may be subdivided into angular and duplex types.

因此，交易可以分为互补交易或交叉交易、简单交易或间接交易，而间接交易又可以细分为角度交易和双重交易。

#↩

3 · Procedures and Rituals

3. 程序和仪式

T RANSACTIONS usually proceed in series. These series are not random, but are programmed. Programming may come from one of three sources: Parent, Adult or Child, or more generally, from society, material or idiosyncrasy. Since the needs of adaptation require that the Child be shielded by the Parent or Adult until each social situation has been tested, Child programming is most apt to occur in situations of privacy and intimacy, where preliminary testing has already been done.

互动通常以序列的形式进行。这些序列并非随机，而是预先设定的。这种设定可能来自三个方面：父母、成人或儿童，或者更广泛地说，来自社会、物质或个人特质。由于适应的需要要求儿童在每次社交情境测试之前都受到父母或成人的保护，因此儿童的“设定”最容易发生在私密和亲密的场合，因为在这些场合中，初步的测试已经完成。

The simplest forms of social activity are procedures and rituals. Some of these are universal and some local, but all of them have to be learned. A procedure is a series of simple complementary Adult transactions directed towards the manipulation of reality. Reality is defined as having two aspects: static and dynamic. Static reality comprises all the possible arrangements of matter in the universe. Arithmetic, for example, consists of statements about static reality. Dynamic reality may be defined as the potentialities for interaction of all the energy systems in the universe. Chemistry, for example, consists of statements about dynamic reality. Procedures are based on data processing and probability estimates concerning the material of reality, and reach their highest development in professional techniques. Piloting an airplane and removing an appendix are procedures. Psychotherapy is a procedure insofar as it is under the control of the therapist’s Adult, and it is not a procedure insofar as his Parent or Child takes over the executive. The programming of a procedure is determined by the material, on the basis of estimates made by the agent’s Adult.

社会活动最简单的形式是程序和仪式。其中一些是普遍的，一些是地方性的，但所有这些都需要学习。程序是一系列简单的、互补的成人行为，旨在操纵现实。现实被定义为具有两个方面：静态和动态。静态现实包含宇宙中物质所有可能的排列方式。例如，算术就是关于静态现实的陈述。动态现实可以定义为宇宙中所有能量系统相互作用的潜能。例如，化学就是关于动态现实的陈述。程序基于对现实物质的数据处理和概率估计，并在专业技术中得到最高发展。驾驶飞机和切除阑尾都是程序。心理治疗之所以是一种程序，是因为它在治疗师的成人控制之下；而如果治疗师的父母或子女接管了执行，则它就不是一种程序。程序的程序化取决于物质，并基于行为者的成人所做的估计。

Two variables are used in evaluating procedures. A procedure is said to be efficient when the agent makes the best possible use of the data and experience available to him, regardless of any deficiencies that may exist in his knowledge. If the Parent or the Child interferes with the Adult’s data processing, the procedure becomes contaminated and will be less efficient. The effectiveness of a procedure is judged by the actual results. Thus efficiency is a psychological criterion and effectiveness is a material one. A native assistant medical officer on a tropical island became very adept at removing cataracts. He used what knowledge he had with a very high degree of efficiency, but since he knew less than the European medical officer, he was not quite as effective. The European began to drink heavily so that his efficiency dropped, but at first his effectiveness was not diminished. But when his hands became tremulous as the years went by, his assistant began to surpass him not only in efficiency, but also in effectiveness. It can be seen from this example that both of these variables are best evaluated by an expert in the procedures involved – efficiency by personal acquaintance with the agent, and effectiveness by surveying the actual results.

评估程序时会用到两个变量。当执行者能够充分利用现有数据和经验，而忽略自身知识的不足时，该程序就被认为是有效的。如果家长或儿童干预成人的数据处理，程序就会受到污染，效率降低。程序的有效性则取决于实际结果。因此，效率是一个心理标准，而有效性是一个物质标准。一位热带岛屿上的土著助理医务官非常擅长白内障摘除术。他能高效地运用已有的知识，但由于他掌握的知识不如欧洲医务官丰富，所以他的有效性略逊一筹。后来，这位欧洲医务官开始酗酒，导致效率下降，但起初他的有效性并未降低。然而，随着岁月的流逝，他的双手开始颤抖，他的助手不仅在效率上超越了他，在有效性上也更胜一筹。从这个例子可以看出，这两个变量最好由相关程序的专家来评估——效率通过与代理人的私人了解来评估，而效果则通过调查实际结果来评估。

From the present viewpoint, a ritual is a stereotyped series of simple complementary transactions programmed by external social forces. An informal ritual, such as social leave-taking, may be subject to considerable local variations in details, although the basic form remains the same. A formal ritual, such as a Roman Catholic Mass, offers much less option. The form of a ritual is Parentally determined by tradition, but more recent ‘parental’ influences may have similar but less stable effects in trivial instances. Some formal rituals of special historical or anthropological interest have two phases: (1) a phase in which transactions are carried on under rigid Parental strictures (2) a phase of Parental licence, in which the Child is allowed more or less complete transactional freedom, resulting in an orgy.

从目前的角度来看，仪式是由外部社会力量所安排的一系列固定的、简单的互补行为。非正式仪式，例如社交告别，虽然基本形式保持不变，但在细节上可能存在相当大的地域差异。正式仪式，例如罗马天主教弥撒，则选择余地要少得多。仪式的形式由父母的传统决定，但近期“父母”的影响在某些琐事中可能产生类似但不太稳定的影响。一些具有特殊历史或人类学意义的正式仪式包含两个阶段：（1）在父母严格的约束下进行行为的阶段；（2）父母放任的阶段，在此阶段，子女被允许或多或少地拥有行为自由，最终导致狂欢。

Many formal rituals started off as heavily contaminated though fairly efficient procedures, but as time passed and circumstances changed, they lost all procedural validity while still retaining their usefulness as acts of faith. Transactionally they represent guilt-relieving or reward-seeking compliances with traditional Parental demands. They offer a safe, reassuring (apotropaic), and often enjoyable method of structuring time.

许多正式的仪式最初都是一些虽有效但已被严重污染的程序，但随着时间的推移和环境的改变，它们失去了所有程序上的有效性，却仍然保留了其作为信仰行为的意义。从交易的角度来看，它们代表着人们为了减轻内疚或寻求回报而顺从父母的传统要求。它们提供了一种安全、令人安心（具有辟邪作用）且通常令人愉悦的时间来安排时间。

Of more significance as an introduction to game analysis are informal rituals, and among the most instructive are the American greeting rituals.

对于游戏分析而言，非正式仪式更为重要，其中最具指导意义的当属美国的问候仪式。

1A: ‘Hi!’ (Hello, good morning.)

1A：‘嗨！’（你好，早上好。）

1B: ‘Hi!’ (Hello, good morning.)

1B：‘嗨！’（你好，早上好。）

2A: ‘Warm enough forya?’ (How are you?)

2A：‘你好吗？’

2B: ‘Sure is. Looks like rain, though.’ (Fine. How are you?)

2B：‘确实如此。不过看起来要下雨了。’（我很好。你呢？）

3A: ‘Well, take cara yourself.’ (Okay.)

3A：‘好吧，你自己照顾好自己。’（好的。）

3B: ‘I’ll be seeing you.’

3B：“我会再见到你的。”

4A: ‘So long.’

4A：‘再见。’

4B: ‘So long.’

4B：‘再见。’

It is apparent that this exchange is not intended to convey information. Indeed, if there is any information, it is wisely withheld. It might take Mr A fifteen minutes to say how he is, and Mr B, who is only the most casual acquaintance, has no intention of devoting that much time to listening to him. This series of transactions is quite adequately characterized by calling it an ‘eight-stroke ritual’. If A and B were in a hurry, they might both be contented with a two-stroke exchange, Hi-Hi. If they were old-fashioned Oriental potentates, they might go through a two-hundred stroke ritual before settling down to business. Meanwhile, in the jargon of transactional analysis, A and B have improved each other’s health slightly; for the moment, at least, ‘their spinal cords won’t shrivel up’, and each is accordingly grateful.

显然，这种交流并非旨在传递信息。事实上，即便真有信息，也被明智地隐瞒了。A先生可能需要十五分钟才能说完自己的近况，而B先生只是与他略有交情，自然无意花费那么多时间倾听。用“八笔礼”来形容这一系列的交流再贴切不过了。如果A和B赶时间，他们或许会满足于两笔的寒暄，比如打个招呼。如果他们是古雅的东方君主，或许会先进行一番两百笔的礼节，才开始谈正事。与此同时，用人际沟通分析的术语来说，A和B的健康状况略有改善；至少目前来看，“他们的脊髓不会萎缩”，两人都心存感激。

This ritual is based on careful intuitive computations by both parties. At this stage of their acquaintance they figure that they owe each other exactly four strokes at each meeting, and not oftener than once a day. If they run into each other again shortly, say within the next half-hour, and have no new business to transact, they will pass by without any sign, or with only the slightest nod of recognition, or at most with a very perfunctory Hi-Hi. These computations hold not only for short intervals but over periods of several months. Let us now consider Mr C and Mr D, who pass each other about once a day, trade one stroke each – Hi-Hi – and go their ways. Mr C goes on a month’s vacation. The day after he returns, he encounters Mr D as usual. If on this occasion Mr D merely says ‘Hi!’ and no more, Mr C will be offended, ‘his spinal cord will shrivel slightly’. By his calculations, Mr D and he owe each other about thirty strokes. These can be compressed into a few transactions, if those transactions are emphatic enough. Mr D’s side properly runs something like this (where each unit of ‘intensity’ or ‘interest’ is equivalent to a stroke):

这种礼节建立在双方仔细的直觉计算之上。在他们相识的这个阶段，他们估算每次见面都该互相打四下，而且一天最多一次。如果他们很快再次相遇，比如半小时内，而且没有什么新的事情要谈，他们就会默默地擦肩而过，或者只是轻轻点头致意，最多也就是敷衍地打个招呼。这种计算不仅适用于短时间，也适用于几个月的时间。现在我们来看C先生和D先生，他们大约每天相遇一次，互相打一下招呼——打个招呼——然后各自离开。C先生去度假一个月。他回来后的第二天，像往常一样遇到了D先生。如果这次D先生只是说了声“嗨！”就没了下文，C先生就会感到不快，“他的脊椎会微微萎缩”。根据他的计算，他和D先生大约应该互相打三十下。如果这些交易足够有力，就可以将它们压缩成几笔交易。D先生那边通常采用类似这样的方式（其中每个“强度”或“兴趣”单位都相当于一笔交易）：

1D: ‘Hi!’ (1 unit)

1D：‘嗨！’（1 个单位）

2D: ‘Haven’t seen you around lately.’(2 units)

2D：‘最近没见到你。’（2个单位）

3D: ‘Oh, have you! Where did you go?’ (5 units)

3D：‘哦，你竟然去了哪里？’（5个单元）

4D: ‘Say, that’s interesting. How was it?’ (7 units)

4D：‘嗯，这很有意思。感觉怎么样？’（7个单位）

5D: ‘Well, you’re sure looking fine.’ (4 units) ‘Did your family go along?’ (4 units)

5D：‘嗯，你看起来气色真不错。’（4个单位）‘你的家人也一起去了吗？’（4个单位）

6D: ‘Well, glad to see you back.’ (4 units)

6D：‘很高兴看到你回来。’（4个单位）

7D: ‘So long.’ (1 unit)

7D：‘再见。’（1个单位）

This gives Mr D a total of 28 units. Both he and Mr C know that he will make up the missing units the following day, so the account is now, for all practical purposes, squared. Two days later they will be back at their two-stroke exchange, Hi-Hi. But now they ‘know each other better’, i.e., each knows the other is reliable, and this may be useful if they should meet ‘socially’.

这样一来，D先生总共就有了28个单位。他和C先生都知道，他会在第二天补足缺失的单位，所以实际上账目已经结清了。两天后，他们会回到他们常去的二手车交易店Hi-Hi。但现在他们“更了解彼此了”，也就是说，他们都知道对方可靠，如果他们以后有机会“社交”见面，这可能会很有帮助。

The inverse case is also worth considering, Mr E and Mr F have set up a two-stroke ritual, Hi-Hi. One day instead of passing on, Mr E stops and asks: ‘How are you?’ The conversation proceeds as follows:

反过来也值得考虑。E先生和F先生约定了一个两步碰头的仪式，叫“嗨嗨”。有一天，E先生没有像往常那样继续打招呼，而是停下来问：“你好吗？” 对话如下：

1E: ‘Hi!’

1E：‘嗨！’

1F: ‘Hi!’

1F：‘嗨！’

2E: ‘How are you?’

2E：‘你好吗？’

2F ( puzzled ): ‘Fine. How are you?’

2F（疑惑地）：“我很好。你呢？”

3E: ‘Everything’s great Warm enough for you?’

3E：“一切都很好，够暖和吗？”

3F: ‘Yeah.’ ( Cautiously. ) ‘Looks like rain, though.’

3F：“嗯。”（谨慎地）“不过，看起来要下雨了。”

4E: ‘Nice to see you again.’

4E：‘很高兴再次见到你。’

4F: ‘Same here. Sorry, I’ve got to get to the library before it closes. So long.’

4F：‘我也是。抱歉，我得在图书馆关门前赶过去。再见。’

5E: ‘So long.’

5E：‘再见。’

As Mr F hurries away, he thinks to himself: ‘What’s come over him all of a sudden? Is he selling insurance or something?’ In transactional terms this reads: ‘All he owes me is one stroke, why is he giving me five?’

F先生匆匆离开时，心里想着：“他怎么突然变成这样了？他是在推销保险吗？” 从交易的角度来看，这可以理解为：“他只欠我一次机会，为什么给我五次机会？”

An even simpler demonstration of the truly transactional, business-like nature of these simple rituals is the occasion when Mr G says ‘Hi!’ and Mr H passes on without replying. Mr G’s reaction is ‘What’s the matter with him?’ meaning: ‘I gave him a stroke and he didn’t give me one in return.’ If Mr H keeps this up and extends it to other acquaintances, he is going to cause some talk in his community.

更简单的例子就能说明这些简单礼仪背后隐藏着多么功利、多么商业化的本质：G先生打招呼“嗨！”，H先生却不予回应便径直走开了。G先生的反应是：“他怎么了？”言下之意是：“我跟他打了个招呼，他居然没回我一个。”如果H先生继续这样下去，甚至对其他熟人也如此，那他肯定会在社区里引起议论。

In borderline cases it is sometimes difficult to distinguish between a procedure and a ritual. The tendency is for the laymen to call professional procedures rituals, while actually every transaction may be based on sound, even vital experience, but the layman does not have the background to appreciate that. Conversely, there is a tendency for professionals to rationalize ritualistic elements that still cling to their procedures, and to dismiss sceptical laymen on the ground that they are not equipped to understand. And one of the ways in which entrenched professionals may resist the introduction of sound new procedures is by laughing them off as rituals. Hence the fate of Semmelweis and other innovators.

在某些模糊不清的情况下，有时很难区分程序和仪式。外行人往往把专业程序称为仪式，而实际上，每项操作都可能基于可靠甚至至关重要的经验，只是外行人缺乏理解这些经验的背景知识。反之，专业人士也倾向于为程序中仍然存在的仪式性元素辩解，并以外行人缺乏理解能力为由，驳斥他们的质疑。根深蒂固的专业人士抵制引入合理的新程序的方式之一，就是将其斥为仪式而嗤之以鼻。塞麦尔维斯和其他创新者的遭遇正是如此。

The essential and similar feature of both procedures and rituals is that they are stereotyped. Once the first transaction has been initiated, the whole series is predictable and follows a predetermined course to a foreordained conclusion unless special conditions arise. The difference between them lies in the origin of the predetermination: procedures are programmed by the Adult and rituals are Parentally patterned.

程序和仪式的本质共同特征在于它们的模式化。一旦第一次互动开始，除非出现特殊情况，否则整个过程都是可预测的，并会按照预定的路线走向预定的结局。二者的区别在于预定性的来源：程序由成人设定，而仪式则由父母模式塑造。

Individuals who are not comfortable or adept with rituals sometimes evade them by substituting procedures. They can be found, for example, among people who like to help the hostess with preparing or serving food and drink at parties.

有些人不习惯或不擅长礼仪，有时会用其他方式来代替。例如，在聚会上喜欢帮女主人准备或上菜的人，往往就是这类人。

#↩

4 · Pastimes

4. 消遣

P ASTIMES occur in social and temporal matrices of varying degrees of complexity, and hence vary in complexity. However, if we use the transaction as the unit of social intercourse, we can dissect out of appropriate situations an entity which may be called a simple pastime. This may be defined as a series of semi-ritualistic, simple, complementary transactions arranged around a single field of material, whose primary object is to structure an interval of time. The beginning and end of the interval are typically signalled by procedures or rituals. The transactions are adaptively programmed so that each party will obtain the maximum gains or advantages during the interval. The better his adaptation, the more he will get out of it.

消遣活动发生在复杂程度各异的社会和时间矩阵中，因此其复杂程度也各不相同。然而，如果我们以交易作为社会交往的基本单位，就可以从适当的情境中提炼出一种可以称之为“简单消遣”的实体。这种简单消遣可以定义为一系列围绕单一物质领域展开的半仪式性的、简单的、互补的交易，其主要目的是构建一段时间段。这段时间段的开始和结束通常由特定的程序或仪式来标记。这些交易经过适应性编程，使得参与方在时间段内都能获得最大的收益或优势。参与方的适应性越强，从中获得的收益就越多。

Pastimes are typically played at parties (‘social gatherings’) or during the waiting period before a formal group meeting begins; such waiting periods before a meeting ‘begins’ have the same structure and dynamics as ‘parties’. Pastimes may take the form described as ‘chit-chat’ or they may become more serious, e.g., argumentative. A large cocktail party often functions as a kind of gallery for the exhibition of pastimes. In one corner of the room a few people are playing ‘PTA’, another corner is the forum for ‘Psychiatry’, a third is the theatre for ‘Ever Been’ or ‘What Became’, the fourth is engaged for ‘General Motors’, and the buffet is reserved for women who want to play ‘Kitchen’ or ‘Wardrobe’. The proceedings at such a gathering may be almost identical, with a change of names here and there, with the proceedings at a dozen similar parties taking place simultaneously in the area. At another dozen in a different social stratum, a different assortment of pastimes is underway.

消遣活动通常在聚会（“社交聚会”）上进行，或者在正式小组会议开始前的等待期间进行；这种会议“开始”前的等待期与“聚会”的结构和动态相同。消遣活动的形式可以是“闲聊”，也可以变得更加严肃，例如辩论。大型鸡尾酒会常常充当着消遣活动展览馆的角色。房间的一个角落里，几个人在玩“家长教师协会”游戏，另一个角落是“精神病学”论坛，第三个角落是“曾经是”或“后来怎么样”剧场，第四个角落是“通用汽车”游戏区，自助餐区则留给了想玩“厨房”或“衣橱”游戏的女士们。这样的聚会流程可能几乎完全相同，只是名称略有不同，而且在附近同时进行的十几个类似的聚会也是如此。在另外十几个不同社会阶层的聚会上，人们正在进行着各种各样的消遣活动。

Pastimes may be classified in different ways. The external determinants are sociological (sex, age, marital status, cultural, racial or economic). ‘General Motors’ (comparing cars) and ‘Who Won’ (sports) are both ‘Man Talk’. ‘Grocery’, ‘Kitchen’, and ‘Wardrobe’ are all ‘Lady Talk’ – or, as practised in the South Seas, ‘Mary Talk’. ‘Making Out’ is adolescent, while the onset of middle age is marked by a shift to ‘Balance Sheet’. Other species of this class, which are all variations of ‘Small Talk’, are: ‘How To’ (go about doing something), an easy filler for short airplane trips; ‘How Much’ (does it cost), a favourite in lower middle-class bars; ‘Ever Been’ (to some nostalgic place), a middle-class game for ‘oldhands’ such as salesmen ;‘Do You Know’ (so-and-so) for lonely ones; ‘What Became’ (of good old Joe), often played by economic successes and failures: ‘Morning After’ (what a hangover) and ‘Martini’ (I know a better way), typical of a certain kind of ambitious young person.

消遣方式可以有很多种。外部决定因素包括社会因素（性别、年龄、婚姻状况、文化、种族或经济状况）。“通用汽车”（比较汽车）和“谁赢了”（体育比赛）都属于“男人的谈话”。“杂货”、“厨房”和“衣橱”都是“女人的谈话”——或者，在南太平洋地区，被称为“玛丽的谈话”。“亲热”是青少年时期的谈话，而中年时期的标志是谈话内容转向“资产负债表”。其他一些属于此类的谈话，都是“闲聊”的变体，例如：“如何做某事”，是短途飞机旅行中轻松打发时间的话题；“多少钱”，是中下层阶级酒吧里的热门话题；“去过某个令人怀念的地方吗”，是中产阶级“老手”（例如销售员）的谈话游戏；“你知道某某吗”，是孤独者之间的谈话。 《老乔的结局》（What Became）经常被经济上的成功者和失败者演绎；《宿醉之后》（Morning After）（宿醉难受）和《马提尼》（Martini）（我知道更好的方法）则代表了某种雄心勃勃的年轻人。

The structural-transactional classification is a more personal one. Thus ‘PTA’ may be played at three levels. At the Child-Child level it takes the form of ‘How do You Deal with Recalcitrant Parents’; its Adult-Adult form, ‘PTA’ proper, is popular among well-read young mothers; with older people it tends to take the dogmatic Parent-Parent form of ‘Juvenile Delinquency’. Some married couples play ‘Tell Them Dear’, in which the wife is Parental and the husband comes through like a precocious child. ‘Look Ma No Hands’ is similarly a Child-Parent pastime suitable for people of any age, sometimes diffidently adapted into ‘Aw Shucks Fellows’.

结构-互动分类法更具个人色彩。因此，“家长教师游戏”（PTA）可以在三个层面上进行。在儿童-儿童层面，它的形式是“如何应对不听话的父母”；其成人-成人形式，即真正的“家长教师游戏”，在博览群书的年轻母亲中很流行；在老年人中，它往往采取教条式的父母-父母形式，例如“青少年犯罪”。一些已婚夫妇会玩“告诉他们，亲爱的”，其中妻子扮演父母的角色，而丈夫则扮演早熟的孩子。“看妈妈不用手”也是一种适合任何年龄段的儿童-父母游戏，有时会略带羞涩地改编成“哎呀，伙计们”。

Even more cogent is the psychological classification of pastimes. Both ‘PTA’ and ‘Psychiatry’, for example, may be played in either projective or introjective forms. The analysis of ‘PTA Projective Type, is represented in Figure 6A, based on the following Parent-Parent paradigm:

更具说服力的是消遣方式的心理学分类。例如，“PTA”（亲子游戏）和“精神病学”都可以以投射型或内摄型的方式进行。图 6A 展示了基于以下父母-父母范式的“PTA 投射型”分析：

A: ‘There wouldn’t be all this delinquency if it weren’t for broken homes.’

A：“如果不是因为家庭破碎，就不会有这么多青少年犯罪。”

B: ‘It’s not only that. Even in good homes nowadays the children aren’t taught manners the way they used to be.’

B：“不仅如此。如今即使在条件不错的家庭里，孩子们也没有像过去那样接受礼仪教育。”

‘PTA’, Introjective Type, runs along the following lines (Adult-Adult):

“PTA”（内摄型）遵循以下模式（成人-成人）：

C: ‘I just don’t seem to have what it takes to be a mother.’

C：“我好像就是不具备当母亲的条件。”

D: ‘No matter how hard you try, they never grow up the way you want them to, so you have to keep wondering if you’re doing the right thing and what mistakes you’ve made.’

D：“无论你多么努力，他们永远不会按照你想要的方式长大，所以你必须不断地思考你做的事情是否正确，以及你犯了哪些错误。”

‘Psychiatry’, Projective Type, takes the Adult-Adult form:

“精神病学”，投射类型，采用成人-成人形式：

E: ‘I think it’s some unconscious oral frustration that makes him act that way.’

E：“我认为这是一种无意识的口吃挫败感，才会让他那样做。”

F: ‘You seem to have your aggressions so well sublimated.’

F：“你似乎把你的攻击性压抑得很好。”

Figure 6 B represents ‘Psychiatry’, Introjective Type, another Adult-Adult pastime.

图 6B 代表“精神病学”，内摄型，这是成年人之间的另一种消遣方式。

G: ‘That painting symbolizes smearing to me.’

G：“对我来说，那幅画象征着涂抹。”

H: ‘In my case, painting is trying to please my father.’

H：“对我来说，画画是为了取悦我的父亲。”

Figure 6. Pastimes

图 6. 消遣活动

Besides structuring time and providing mutually acceptable stroking for the parties concerned, pastimes serve the additional function of being social-selection processes. While a pastime is in progress, the Child in each player is watchfully assessing the potentialities of the others involved. At the end of the party, each person will have selected certain players he would like to see more of, while others he will discard, regardless of how skilfully or pleasantly theyeach engaged in the pastime. The ones he selects are those who seem the most likely candidates for more complex relationships – that is, games. This sorting system, however well rationalized, is actually largely unconscious and intuitive.

除了安排时间、为参与者提供彼此都能接受的慰藉之外，消遣活动还具有社会选择的功能。在消遣进行的过程中，每个参与者内心深处的“孩子”都会仔细评估其他参与者的潜力。聚会结束后，每个人都会选择一些自己想继续交往的伙伴，而将另一些伙伴排除在外，无论他们在游戏中表现得多么娴熟或愉快。他选择的那些人，往往是那些看起来最有可能发展出更复杂关系——也就是参与游戏——的人。这种分类系统，无论其理论多么完善，实际上很大程度上是无意识的、直觉式的。

In special cases the Adult overrides the Child in the selection process. This is most clearly illustrated by an insurance salesman who carefully learns to play social pastimes. While he is playing, his Adult listens for possible prospects and selects them from the players as people he would like to see more of. Their adeptness at games or congeniality is quite irrelevant to his process of selection, which is based, as in most cases, on peripheral factors – in this instance, financial readiness.

在特殊情况下，成人会在选择过程中凌驾于儿童之上。一位保险推销员的例子最能说明这一点，他认真学习各种社交游戏。当他玩游戏时，他内心的成人会倾听潜在的潜在客户，并从中挑选出他希望进一步接触的人。他们的游戏技巧或亲和力与他的选择过程几乎无关，他的选择通常基于一些次要因素——在这个例子中，是经济能力。

Pastimes, however, have a quite specific aspect of exclusiveness. For example, ‘Man Talk’ and ‘Lady Talk’ do not mix. People playing a hard hand of ‘Ever Been’ (there) will be annoyed by an intruder who wants to play ‘How Much’ (for avocados) or ‘Morning After’. People playing Projective ‘PTA’ will resent the intrusion of Introjective ‘PTA’, athough usually not as intensely as the other way around.

然而，消遣方式本身就具有一种独特的排他性。例如，“男人的谈话”和“女人的谈话”就互不相容。正在玩“去过那里吗？”（Ever Been）的人，如果被打扰去玩“多少钱？”（How Much）或“宿醉”（Morning After）之类的游戏，肯定会感到恼火。玩投射型“PTA”（PTA）的人也会反感内摄型“PTA”的介入，尽管通常不会像反过来那样强烈。

Pastimes form the basis for the selection of acquaintances, and may lead to friendship. A party of women who drop in at each other’s houses every morning for coffee to play ‘Delinquent Husband’ are likely to give a cool reception to a new neighbour who wants to play ‘Sunny Side Up’. If they are saying how mean their husbands are, it is too disconcerting to have a newcomer declare that her husband is just marvellous, in fact perfect, and they will not keep her long. So at a cocktail party, if someone wants to move from one corner to another, he must either join in the pastime played in his new location or else successfully switch the whole proceeding into a new channel. A good hostess, of course, takes the situation in hand immediately and states the programme: ‘We were just playing Projective “PTA”. What do you think?’ Or: ‘Come now, you girls have been playing “Wardrobe” long enough Mr J here is a writer/politician/surgeon, and I’m sure he’d like to play “Look Ma No Hands”. Wouldn’t you, Mr J?’

消遣是结交朋友的基础，也可能发展成友谊。一群每天早上互相串门喝咖啡、玩“不负责任的丈夫”游戏的女士，如果新邻居想玩“阳光灿烂的早餐”，她们很可能会冷淡接待。如果她们正在吐槽自己的丈夫有多糟糕，那么新来的人突然宣称自己的丈夫简直完美无缺，这会让她们感到很不自在，她们也不会久留。所以在鸡尾酒会上，如果有人想从一个角落挪到另一个角落，他要么必须加入新位置正在进行的游戏，要么就得成功地把整个游戏转移到另一个频道。当然，一位好的女主人会立即掌控局面，并宣布游戏内容：“我们刚才在玩投射式‘家长教师协会’游戏。”你们觉得怎么样？或者：“好了好了，你们这些女孩玩‘衣橱’游戏都玩够了，J先生是一位作家/政治家/外科医生，我相信他肯定想玩‘看，妈妈不用手’。您不想玩吗，J先生？”

Another important advantage obtained from pastimes is the confirmation of role and the stabilizing of position. A role is something like what Jung calls persona, except that it is less opportunistic and more deeply rooted in the individual’s fantasies. Thus in Projective ‘PTA’ one player may take the role of tough Parent, another the role of righteous Parent, a third the role of indulgent Parent and a fourth the role of helpful Parent. All four experience and exhibit a Parental ego state, but each presents himself differently. The role of each one is confirmed if it prevails – that is, if it meets with no antagonism or is strengthened by any antagonism it meets or is approved by certain types of people with stroking.

从消遣中获得的另一个重要好处是角色确认和地位稳定。角色类似于荣格所说的“人格面具”，但它不那么具有机会主义色彩，而是更根植于个体的幻想之中。因此，在投射性“PTA”游戏中，一个玩家可能扮演严厉的父母角色，另一个扮演正义的父母角色，第三个扮演溺爱的父母角色，第四个扮演乐于助人的父母角色。这四个人都体验并展现出父母自我状态，但每个人呈现的方式都不同。如果某个角色占据主导地位——也就是说，如果它没有遇到任何对抗，或者在遇到任何对抗时得到加强，或者得到某些特定人群的认可和赞赏——那么该角色就得到了确认。

The confirmation of his role stabilizes the individual’s position, and this is called the existential advantage from the pastime. A position is a simple predicative statement which influences all of the individual’s transactions; in the long run it determines his destiny and often that of his descendants as well. A position may be more or less absolute. Typical positions from which Projective ‘PTA’ can be played are: ‘All children are bad!’ ‘All other children are bad!’ ‘All children are sad!’ ‘All children are persecuted!’ These positions might give rise to the role of the tough, the righteous, the indulgent and the helpful Parent, respectively. Actually a position is primarily manifested by the mental attitude to which it gives rise, and it is with this attitude that the individual undertakes the transactions which constitute his role.

对自身角色的确认巩固了个人的地位，这被称为从这种消遣中获得的生存优势。立场是一个简单的谓词性陈述，它影响着个人的所有行为；从长远来看，它决定着个人的命运，而且往往也决定着其后代的命运。立场可以是绝对的，也可以是绝对的。典型的投射性“PTA”（投射性亲子关系）立场包括：“所有孩子都是坏孩子！”“其他孩子都是坏孩子！”“所有孩子都很悲伤！”“所有孩子都遭受迫害！”这些立场可能分别导致严厉的父母、正义的父母、溺爱的父母和乐于助人的父母的角色。实际上，立场主要体现在它所引发的心理态度上，而正是基于这种态度，个人才会进行构成其角色的行为。

Positions are taken and become fixed surprisingly early, from the second or even the first year to the seventh year of life – in any case long before the individual is competent or experienced enough to make such a serious commitment. It is not difficult to deduce from an individual’s position the kind of childhood he must have had. Unless something or somebody intervenes, he spends the rest of his life stabilizing his position and dealing with situations that threaten it: by avoiding them, warding off certain elements or manipulating them provocatively so that they are transformed from threats into justifications. One reason pastimes are so stereotyped is that they serve such stereotyped purposes. But the gains they offer show why people play them so eagerly, and why they can be so pleasant if played with people who have constructive or benevolent positions to maintain.

人们的立场很早就被确立并固定下来，从两岁甚至一岁到七岁——总之，远在个人具备足够的能力或经验做出如此重大承诺之前。从一个人的立场不难推断出他/她童年的经历。除非有外力介入，否则他/她余生都在努力巩固自己的立场，并应对可能威胁到立场的情况：通过回避、抵御某些因素或巧妙地操纵，将威胁转化为正当理由。消遣活动之所以如此模式化，原因之一在于它们服务于模式化的目的。但这些活动带来的益处解释了为什么人们如此热衷于参与其中，以及为什么与那些拥有建设性或善意立场的人一起参与时，这些活动会如此令人愉悦。

A pastime is not always easy to distinguish from an activity, and combinations frequently occur. Many commonplace pastimes, such as ‘General Motors’, consist of what psychologists might call Multiple-Choice – Sentence-Completion exchanges.

消遣与活动并非总是容易区分，二者经常结合在一起。许多常见的消遣，例如“通用汽车”，实际上就包含心理学家所说的“多项选择-句子填空”互动。

A. ‘I like a Ford/Chevrolet/Plymouth better than a Ford/Chevrolet/Plymouth because …’

A.“我更喜欢福特/雪佛兰/普利茅斯，而不是福特/雪佛兰/普利茅斯，因为……”

B. ‘Oh. Well, I’d rather have a Ford/Chevrolet/Plymouth than a Ford/Chevrolet/Plymouth because …’

B：‘哦。嗯，我宁愿要一辆福特/雪佛兰/普利茅斯，而不是福特/雪佛兰/普利茅斯，因为……’

It is apparent that there may actually be some useful information conveyed in such stereotypes.

显然，这类刻板印象中可能确实包含一些有用的信息。

A few other common pastimes may be mentioned. ‘Me Too’ is often a variant of ‘Ain’t It Awful’. ‘Why Don’t They’ (do something about it) is a favourite among housewives who do not wish to be emancipated. ‘Then We’ll’ is a Child-Child pastime. ‘Let’s Find’ (something to do) is played by juvenile delinquents or mischievous grown-ups.

还有一些其他常见的消遣方式值得一提。“我也是”（Me Too）通常是“真糟糕”（Ain't It Awful）的变体。“他们为什么不采取行动”（Why Don't They，意为“他们为什么不采取行动”）是那些不愿摆脱家庭主妇束缚的家庭主妇们的最爱。“那我们就……”（Then We'll）是孩子们之间的消遣。“我们去找点事做”（Let's Find，意为“找点事做”）则是青少年罪犯或调皮捣蛋的成年人玩的游戏。

#↩

5 · Games

5 · 游戏

1 · DEFINITION

1. 定义

A GAME is an ongoing series of complementary ulterior transactions progressing to a well-defined, predictable outcome. Descriptively it is a recurring set of transactions, often repetitious, superficially plausible, with a concealed motivation; or, more colloquially, a series of moves with a snare, or ‘gimmick’. Games are clearly differentiated from procedures, rituals, and pastimes by two chief characteristics: (1) their ulterior quality and (2) the payoff. Procedures may be successful, rituals effective, and pastimes profitable, but all of them are by definition candid; they may involve contest, but not conflict, and the ending may be sensational, but it is not dramatic. Every game, on the other hand, is basically dishonest, and the outcome has a dramatic, as distinct from merely exciting, quality.

游戏是一系列持续进行的、互为补充的、别有用心的交易，最终导向一个明确且可预测的结果。从描述上看，它是一系列反复出现、看似合理实则暗藏动机的交易；或者更通俗地说，是一系列带有陷阱或“噱头”的行动。游戏与程序、仪式和消遣活动的主要区别在于两点：(1) 其别有用心的性质；(2) 其最终结果。程序或许成功，仪式或许有效，消遣活动或许有利可图，但它们本质上都是坦诚的；它们可能包含竞争，但不包含冲突，结局或许轰动，但并不戏剧化。而每场游戏本质上都是不诚实的，其结果具有戏剧性，而不仅仅是令人兴奋。

It remains to distinguish games from the one remaining type of social action which so far has not been discussed. An operation is a simple transaction or set of transactions undertaken for a specific, stated purpose. If someone frankly asks for reassurance and gets it, that is an operation. If someone asks for reassurance, and after it is given turns it in some way to the disadvantage of the giver, that is a game. Superficially, then, a game looks like a set of operations, but after the payoff it becomes apparent that these ‘operations’ were really manoeuvres ; not honest requests but moves in the game.

接下来需要区分博弈与一种尚未讨论的社会行为类型。操作是指为了特定目的而进行的简单交易或一系列交易。如果有人坦诚地寻求安慰并得到了安慰，那就是一次操作。如果有人寻求安慰，但在得到安慰后却以某种方式损害了给予者的利益，那就是一场博弈。因此，从表面上看，博弈似乎是一系列操作，但事后人们会发现，这些“操作”实际上是策略；并非真诚的请求，而是博弈中的一步步走棋。

In the ‘insurance game’, for example, no matter what the agent appears to be doing in conversation, if he is a hard player he is really looking for or working on a prospect. What he is after, if he is worth his salt, is to ‘make a killing’. The same applies to ‘the real estate game’, ‘the pajama game’ and similar occupations. Hence at a social gathering, while a salesman is engaged in pastimes, particularly variants of ‘Balance Sheet’, his congenial participation may conceal a series of skilful manoeuvres designed to elicit the kind of information he is professionally interested in. There are dozens of trade journals devoted to improving commercial manoeuvres, and which give accounts of outstanding players and games (interesting operators who make unusually big deals). Transactionally speaking, these are merely variants of Sports Illustrated, Chess World, and other sports magazines.

例如，在“保险交易”中，无论代理人在交谈中表面上做什么，如果他是个老练的玩家，实际上他是在寻找或争取潜在客户。如果他够格，他追求的就是“大赚一笔”。同样的道理也适用于“房地产交易”、“睡衣游戏”以及类似的职业。因此，在社交聚会上，当推销员忙于消遣，尤其是玩“资产负债表”之类的游戏时，他友好的参与可能掩盖了一系列旨在获取他专业所需信息的巧妙策略。有几十种行业期刊致力于提升商业技巧，并报道杰出的玩家和案例（那些达成巨额交易的有趣人物）。从交易的角度来看，这些期刊只不过是《体育画报》、《国际象棋世界》和其他体育杂志的变体而已。

As far as angular transactions are concerned – games which are consciously planned with professional precision under Adult control to yield the maximum gains – the big ‘con games’ which flourished in the early 1900s are hard to surpass for detailed practical planning and psychological virtuosity. 1

就角度交易而言——即在成年人控制下，经过精心策划、精准执行以获取最大利益的游戏——20世纪初盛行的那些大型“骗局”在详细的实际计划和心理技巧方面，几乎无可匹敌。

What we are concerned with here, however, are the unconscious games played by innocent people engaged in duplex transactions of which they are not fully aware, and which form the most important aspect of social life all over the world. Because of their dynamic qualities, games are easy to distinguish from mere static attitudes, which arise from taking a position.

然而，我们在此关注的是无意识中人们参与的双重交易，而他们对此却并不完全了解，这种交易构成了世界各地社会生活中最重要的方面。由于其动态特性，游戏很容易与仅仅源于立场选择的静态态度区分开来。

The use of the word ‘game’ should not be misleading. As explained in the introduction, it does not necessarily imply fun or even enjoyment. Many salesmen do not consider their work fun, as Arthur Miller made clear in his play, The Death of a Salesman. And there may be no lack of seriousness. Football games nowadays are taken very seriously, but no more so than such transactional games as ‘Alcoholic’ or “Third-Degree Rapo’.

使用“游戏”一词不应产生误导。正如引言中所述，它并不一定意味着乐趣或享受。许多销售员并不认为他们的工作有趣，正如阿瑟·米勒在他的戏剧《推销员之死》中所明确指出的那样。而且，严肃性也并非不存在。如今，人们对待足球比赛非常认真，但这并不比“酗酒者”或“三级强奸犯”这类交易性游戏更甚。

The same applies to the word ‘play’, as anyone who has ‘played’ hard poker or ‘played’ the stock market over a long period can testify. The possible seriousness of games and play, and the possibly serious results, are well known to anthropologists. The most complex game that ever existed, that of ‘Courtier’ as described so well by Stendhal in The Charterhouse of Parma, was deadly serious. The grimmest of all, of course, is ‘War’.

“玩”这个词也同样如此，任何长期玩过硬核扑克或股票市场的人都能证明这一点。游戏和玩乐的潜在严肃性，以及可能造成的严重后果，人类学家早已熟知。历史上最复杂的游戏，正如司汤达在《帕尔马修道院》中精彩描述的“廷臣游戏”，其后果极其严重。当然，最残酷的莫过于“战争”。

2 · A TYPICAL GAME

2. 一场典型的游戏

The most common game played between spouses is colloquially called ‘If It Weren’t For You’, and this will be used to illustrate the characteristics of games in general.

夫妻之间最常玩的游戏俗称“如果没有你”，我们将以此来说明游戏的一般特征。

Mrs White complained that her husband severely restricted her social activities, so that she had never learned to dance. Due to changes in her attitude brought about by psychiatric treatment, her husband became less sure of himself and more indulgent. Mrs White was then free to enlarge the scope of her activities. She signed up for dancing classes, and then discovered to her despair that she had a morbid fear of dance floors and had to abandon this project.

怀特太太抱怨说，她丈夫严加限制她的社交活动，以至于她从未学过跳舞。由于精神治疗改变了她的态度，她的丈夫变得不那么自信，也更加宽容了。怀特太太这才得以拓展自己的活动范围。她报名参加了舞蹈班，却绝望地发现自己对舞池有着病态的恐惧，不得不放弃。

This unfortunate adventure, along with similar ones, laid bare some important aspects of the structure of her marriage. Out of her many suitors she had picked a domineering man for a husband. She was then in a position to complain that she could do all sorts of things ‘if it weren’t for you’. Many of her women friends also had domineering husbands, and when they met for their morning coffee, they spent a good deal of time playing ‘If It Weren’t For Him’.

这段不幸的经历，以及其他类似的遭遇，暴露了她婚姻结构中的一些重要问题。在众多追求者中，她竟然选择了一个专横跋扈的男人作为丈夫。于是，她便有了抱怨的资本，说“要不是你”，她什么都能做。她的许多女性朋友也都有着专横跋扈的丈夫，她们早上一起喝咖啡时，常常会玩“要不是他”的游戏。

As it turned out, however, contrary to her complaints, her husband was performing a very real service for her by forbidding her to do something she was deeply afraid of, and by preventing her, in fact, from even becoming aware of her fears. This was one reason her Child had shrewdly chosen such a husband.

然而，事实证明，与她抱怨的相反，她的丈夫实际上是在帮她一个大忙：他禁止她去做她内心深处最害怕的事情，甚至阻止她意识到自己的恐惧。这正是她女儿当初精明地选择这样一位丈夫的原因之一。

But there was more to it than that. His prohibitions and her complaints frequently led to quarrels, so that their sex life was seriously impaired. And because of his feelings of guilt, he frequently brought her gifts which might not otherwise have been forthcoming; certainly when he gave her more freedom, his gifts diminished in lavishness and frequency. She and her husband had little in common besides their household worries and the children, so that their quarrels stood out as important events; it was mainly on these occasions that they had anything but the most casual conversations. At any rate, her married life had proved one thing to her that she had always maintained: that all men were mean and tyrannical. As it turned out, this attitude was related to some daydreams of being sexually abused which had plagued her in earlier years.

但事情远不止如此。他的禁令和她的抱怨常常导致争吵，严重影响了他们的性生活。由于内疚，他经常给她送礼物，而这些礼物原本可能不会送；当然，当他给予她更多自由时，他送的礼物也变得不再那么慷慨和频繁。除了家务和孩子，她和丈夫几乎没有什么共同话题，所以他们的争吵显得格外重要；也只有在这些争吵中，他们才会进行一些不那么随意的交谈。总之，她的婚姻生活证实了她一直以来坚信的一件事：所有男人都是卑鄙专横的。后来发现，这种想法与她早年一直困扰她的一些关于被性虐待的白日梦有关。

There are various ways of describing this game in general terms. It is apparent that it belongs in the large field of social dynamics. The basic fact is that by marrying, Mr and Mrs White have an opportunity to communicate with each other, and such an opportunity may be called social contact. The fact that they use this opportunity makes their household a social aggregation, as contrasted with a New York subway train, for example, where people are in spatial contact but rarely avail themselves of the opportunity and so form a dis-social aggregation. The influence the Whites exert on each other’s behaviour and responses constitutes social action . Various disciplines would investigate such social action from different points of view. Since we are here concerned with the personal histories and psychodynamics of the individuals involved, the present approach is one aspect of social psychiatry ; some implicit judgement is passed on the ‘healthiness’ of the games studied. This is somewhat different from the more neutral and less committed attitudes of sociology and social psychology. Psychiatry reserves the right to say ‘Just a moment!’, which the other disciplines do not. Transactional analysis is a branch of social psychiatry, and game analysis is a special aspect of transactional analysis.

可以用多种方式概括地描述这个游戏。显然，它属于社会动力学的范畴。基本事实是，怀特夫妇通过结婚获得了彼此交流的机会，这种机会可以称为社会接触。他们利用了这一机会，使他们的家庭成为一个社会聚集体，这与例如纽约地铁车厢形成鲜明对比——在地铁车厢里，人们虽然身处空间接触，却很少利用这种机会，因此形成了一个非社会聚集体。怀特夫妇彼此对对方行为和反应的影响构成了社会行动。不同的学科会从不同的角度研究这种社会行动。由于我们在此关注的是相关个体的个人经历和心理动力学，因此目前的研究方法是社会精神病学的一个方面；其中隐含着对所研究游戏的“健康性”的判断。这与社会学和社会心理学更为中立和客观的态度有所不同。精神病学保留着说“稍等片刻！”的权利，而其他学科则没有这种权利。人际沟通分析是社会精神病学的一个分支，而博弈分析是人际沟通分析的一个特殊方面。

Practical game analysis deals with special cases as they appear in specific situations. Theoretical game analysis attempts to abstract and generalize the characteristics of various games, so that they can be recognized independently of their momentary verbal content and their cultural matrix. The theoretical analysis of ‘If It Weren’t For You’, Marital Type, for example, should state the characteristics of that game in such a way that it can be recognized just as easily in a New Guinea jungle village as in a Manhattan penthouse, whether it is concerned with a nuptial party or with the financial problems of getting a fishing rod for the grandchildren; and regardless of how bluntly or subtly the moves are made, according to the permissible degrees of frankness between husband and wife. The prevalence of the game in a given society is a matter for sociology and anthropology. Game analysis, as a part of social psychiatry, is only interested in describing the game when it does occur, regardless of how often that may be. This distinction is not complete, but it is analogous to the distinction between public health and internal medicine; the first is interested in the prevalence of malaria, while the latter studies cases of malaria as they come up, in the jungle or in Manhattan.

实践博弈分析处理的是特定情境中出现的特殊案例。理论博弈分析则试图抽象和概括各种博弈的特征，使其能够独立于其瞬时语言内容和文化背景而被识别。例如，对“如果不是你”（If It Were’t For You）这种婚姻类型博弈的理论分析，应当阐明该博弈的特征，使其既能在新几内亚丛林村庄中被识别，也能在曼哈顿顶层公寓中被识别；无论其主题是婚礼派对还是为孙辈购置钓竿的经济问题；也无论夫妻之间坦诚程度如何，其行动方式是直白还是委婉。博弈在特定社会中的普遍程度属于社会学和人类学的研究范畴。作为社会精神病学的一部分，博弈分析只关注博弈发生时的描述，而不管其发生的频率如何。这种区分并不完全，但它类似于公共卫生和内科之间的区别。前者关注疟疾的流行情况，而后者研究在丛林或曼哈顿等地出现的疟疾病例。

At the present time the scheme given below has been found the most useful one for theoretical game analysis. No doubt it will be improved as further knowledge accumulates. The first requisite is to recognize that a certain sequence of manoeuvres meets the criteria of a game. As many samples as possible of the game are then collected. The significant features of the collection are isolated. Certain aspects emerge as essential. These are then classified under headings which are designed to be as meaningful and instructive as possible in the current state of knowledge. The analysis is undertaken from the point of view of the one who is ‘it’ – in this case, Mrs White.

目前，以下方案被认为是理论博弈分析中最有效的方法。毫无疑问，随着知识的积累，它将会得到改进。首先，需要认识到某些特定的操作序列符合博弈的标准。然后，尽可能多地收集博弈样本。从中提炼出显著特征，并找出某些关键方面。接下来，将这些关键方面归类到相应的标题下，这些标题旨在尽可能地贴近当前知识水平，并具有指导意义。分析是从“博弈者”——在本例中是怀特夫人——的角度进行的。

Thesis. This is a general description of the game, including the immediate sequence of events (the social level) and information about their psychological background, evolution and significance (the psychological level). In the case of ‘If It Weren’t For You’, Marital Type, the details already given will serve ( pages 45–7 ). For the sake of brevity, this game will henceforth be referred to as IWFY.

论文。本文对游戏进行了总体描述，包括事件的直接顺序（社会层面）以及有关其心理背景、演变和意义的信息（心理层面）。以“如果不是你”（If It Were’t For You）的婚姻类型为例，前文已提供的详细信息（第45-47页）将适用。为简洁起见，下文将此游戏简称为IWFY。

Antithesis. The presumption that a certain sequence constitutes a game is tentative until it has been existentially validated. This validation is carried out by a refusal to play or by undercutting the payoff. The one who is ‘it’ will then make more intense efforts to continue the game. In the face of adamant refusal to play or a successful undercutting he will then lapse into a state called ‘despair’, which in some respects resembles a depression, but is different in significant ways. It is more acute and contains elements of frustration and bewilderment. It may be manifested, for example, by the onset of perplexed weeping. In a successful therapeutic situation this may soon be replaced by humorous laughter, implying an Adult realization: ‘There I go again!’ Thus despair is a concern of the Adult, while in depression it is the Child who has the executive power. Hopefulness, enthusiasm or a lively interest in one’s surroundings is the opposite of depression; laughter is the opposite of despair. Hence the enjoyable quality of therapeutic game analysis. The antithesis to IWFY is permissiveness. As long as the husband is prohibitive, the game can proceed. If instead of saying ‘Don’t you dare!’ he says ‘Go ahead!’ the underlying phobias are unmasked, and the wife can no longer turn on him, as demonstrated in Mrs White’s case.

对立。某种序列构成游戏的假设只有在被实际验证后才成立。这种验证可以通过拒绝参与或降低回报来实现。扮演“鬼”的人会更加努力地继续游戏。面对对方坚决拒绝参与或成功降低回报，他会陷入一种被称为“绝望”的状态，这种状态在某些方面类似于抑郁症，但在重要方面却有所不同。它更加强烈，包含挫败感和困惑感。例如，它可能表现为困惑的哭泣。在成功的治疗情境中，这种哭泣可能很快就会被幽默的笑声所取代，这暗示着一种成人式的觉悟：“我又来了！”因此，绝望是成人的关注点，而抑郁症则是儿童的主导力量。希望、热情或对周围环境的浓厚兴趣是抑郁症的反面；笑声是绝望的反面。因此，治疗性游戏分析具有其趣味性。与“放任自流”（IWFY）相反的是放任自流。只要丈夫采取禁止的态度，游戏就能继续进行。如果他不说“你敢！”，而是说“去做吧！”，那么潜在的恐惧就会暴露出来，妻子就无法再反抗他，正如怀特太太的案例所示。

For clear understanding of a game, the antithesis should be known and its effectiveness demonstrated in practice.

要透彻理解一场游戏，就必须了解其对立面，并在实践中证明其有效性。

Aim. This states simply the general purpose of the game. Sometimes there are alternatives. The aim of IWFY may be stated as either reassurance (‘It’s not that I’m afraid, it’s that he won’t let me’) or vindication (‘It’s not that I’m not trying, it’s that he holds me back’). The reassuring function is easier to clarify and is more in accord with the security needs of the wife; therefore IWFY is most simply regarded as having the aim of reassurance.

目的。这简单地阐明了游戏的总体目标。有时也会有其他选择。IWFY 的目的可以表述为安抚（“不是我害怕，而是他不让我做”）或证明（“不是我不努力，而是他阻碍了我”）。安抚的功能更容易解释，也更符合妻子的安全需求；因此，IWFY 最简单来说就是以安抚为目的。

Roles. As previously noted, ego states are not roles but phenomena. Therefore ego states and roles have to be distinguished in a formal description. Games may be described as two-handed, three-handed, many-handed, etc., according to the number of roles offered. Sometimes the ego state of each player corresponds to his role, sometimes it does not.

角色。如前所述，自我状态并非角色，而是一种现象。因此，在正式描述中必须区分自我状态和角色。根据所提供的角色数量，游戏可以描述为两人游戏、三人游戏、多人游戏等等。有时，每个玩家的自我状态与其角色相符；有时则不然。

IWFY is a two-handed game and calls for a restricted wife and a domineering husband. The wife may play her role either as a prudent Adult (‘It’s best that I do as he says’) or as a petulant Child. The domineering husband may preserve an Adult ego state (‘It’s best that you do as I say’) or slip into a Parental one (‘You’d better do what I say’).

《IWFY》是一款双人游戏，需要一位受制于人的妻子和一位专横跋扈的丈夫。妻子可以扮演谨慎的成年人（“我最好听他的”），也可以扮演任性的孩子。专横的丈夫可以保持成年人的自我状态（“你最好听我的”），也可以切换到父母的自我状态（“你最好听我的”）。

Dynamics. There are alternatives in stating the psychodynamic driving forces behind each case of a game. It is usually possible, however, to pick out a single psychodynamic concept which usefully, aptly and meaningfully epitomizes the situation. Thus IWFY is best described as deriving from phobic sources.

动力学。对于每场博弈背后的心理动力学驱动力，都有多种表述方式。然而，通常可以挑选出一个能够有效、恰当且有意义地概括该情境的单一心理动力学概念。因此，IWFY 最恰当的描述是源于恐惧心理。

Examples. Since the childhood origins of a game, or its infantile prototypes, are instructive to study, it is worth-while to search for such cognates in making a formal description. It happens that IWFY is just as frequently played by little children as by grownups, so the childhood version is the same as the later one, with the actual parent substituted for the restricting husband.

例如，由于游戏的童年起源或其早期原型具有启发意义，因此在进行正式描述时，寻找此类同源物是值得的。碰巧的是，IWFY这款游戏在幼儿和成人中都经常玩，所以它的童年版本与成人版本相同，只是把限制性的丈夫换成了真正的父母。

Transactional Paradigm. The transactional analysis of a typical situation is presented, giving both the social and psychological levels of a revealing ulterior transaction. In its most dramatic form IWFY at the social level is a Parent-Child game.

交易范式。本文对一个典型情境进行了交易分析，揭示了其中隐藏交易的社会和心理层面。在最引人注目的社会层面，IWFY 表现为亲子博弈。

Mr White: ‘You stay home and take care of the house.’

怀特先生：“你待在家里照看房子。”

Mrs White: ‘If it weren’t for you, I could be out having fun.’

怀特太太：“要不是你，我现在可能正在外面玩呢。”

At the psychological level (the ulterior marriage contract) the relationship is Child-Child, and quite different.

在心理层面（婚后契约）上，这种关系是孩子与孩子之间的关系，截然不同。

Mr White: ‘You must always be here when I get home. I’m terrified of desertion.’

怀特先生：“我回家的时候，你必须一直在这里。我害怕被抛弃。”

Mrs White: ‘I will be if you help me avoid phobic situations.’

怀特太太：“如果你能帮我避免恐惧症发作的情况，我就会这么做。”

The two levels are illustrated in Figure 7 .

这两个层次如图 7 所示。

Moves. The moves of a game correspond roughly to the strokes in a ritual. As in any game, the players become increasingly adept with practice. Wasteful moves are eliminated, and more and more purpose is condensed into each move. ‘Beautiful friendships’ are often based on the fact that the players complement each other with great economy and satisfaction, so that there is a maximum yield with a minimum effort from the games they play with each other. Certain intermediate, precautionary or concessional moves can be elided, giving a high degree of elegance to the relationship.

招式。游戏中的招式大致对应着仪式中的击打动作。如同任何游戏一样，玩家会随着练习而日益熟练。无用招式会被剔除，而每一步都蕴含着越来越多的意义。“美好的友谊”往往建立在玩家之间高效且令人满意的互补之上，从而在彼此的游戏中以最小的努力获得最大的收益。某些中间的、预防性的或让步性的招式可以被省略，这使得彼此的关系更加优雅。

Figure 7. A Game

图 7. 一场游戏

The effort saved on defensive manoeuvres can be devoted to ornamental flourishes instead, to the delight of both parties and sometimes of the onlookers as well. The student observes that there is a minimum number of moves essential to the progress of the game, and these can be stated in the protocol. Individual players will embellish or multiply these basic moves according to their needs, talents or desires. The framework for IWFY is as follows

节省下来的防守精力可以用来进行华丽的装饰性动作，这不仅能让双方玩家赏心悦目，有时也能让旁观者感到愉悦。学生观察到，游戏进行到一定程度需要一些基本的走法，这些走法可以在规则中明确规定。玩家可以根据自身的需求、天赋或喜好，对这些基本走法进行润色或扩展。国际象棋联合会（IWFY）的框架如下。

(1) Instruction-Compliance (‘You stay home’ – ‘All right’).

（1）指令执行（“你待在家里”——“好的”）。

(2) Instruction-Protest (‘You stay home again’ – ‘If it weren’t for you’).

（2）指令-抗议（“你又待在家里了”——“要不是你”）。

Advantages. The general advantages of a game consist in its stabilizing (homeostatic) functions. Biological homeostasis is promoted by the stroking, and psychological stability is reinforced by the confirmation of position. As has already been noted, stroking may take various forms, so that the biological advantage of a game may be stated in tactile terms. Thus the husband’s role in IWFY is reminiscent of a backhanded slap (quite different in effect from a palmar slap, which is a direct humiliation), and the wife’s response is something like a petulant kick in the shins. Hence the biological gain from IWFY is derived from belligerence-petulance exchanges: a distressing but apparently effective way to maintain the health of nervous tissues.

优势。游戏的普遍优势在于其稳定（体内平衡）功能。抚摸促进生物体内平衡，而确认位置则增强心理稳定性。如前所述，抚摸可以采取多种形式，因此游戏的生物学优势可以用触觉术语来描述。例如，丈夫在“我爱我爱”游戏中扮演的角色类似于反手掌掴（与掌掴的效果截然不同，掌掴是一种直接的羞辱），而妻子的反应则类似于任性地踢小腿。因此，“我爱我爱”游戏的生物学收益来源于好斗与任性的互动：这是一种令人痛苦但显然有效的维持神经组织健康的方式。

Confirmation of the wife’s position – ‘All men are tyrants’ – is the existential advantage. This position is a reaction to the need to surrender that is inherent in the phobias, a demonstration of the coherent structure which underlies all games. The expanded statement would be: ‘If I went out alone in a crowd, I would be overcome by the temptation to surrender; at home I don’t surrender: he forces me, which proves that all men are tyrants.’ Hence this game is commonly played by women who suffer from feelings of unreality, which signifies their difficulty in keeping the Adult in charge in situations of strong temptation. The detailed elucidation of these mechanisms belongs to psychoanalysis rather than game analysis. In game analysis the end product is the chief concern.

妻子的立场——“所有男人都是暴君”——得到了确认，这本身就是一种存在主义优势。这种立场是对恐惧症中固有的屈服需求的反应，也是所有博弈背后内在逻辑结构的体现。更详细地说：“如果我独自一人身处人群，我会屈服于屈服的诱惑；在家我不会屈服：他强迫我，这证明所有男人都是暴君。”因此，这种博弈常被那些感到不真实感的女性所玩弄，这表明她们在面对强烈诱惑时难以保持“成年人”的主导地位。对这些机制的详细阐释属于精神分析的范畴，而非博弈分析。在博弈分析中，最终结果才是主要关注点。

Internal psychological advantage of a game is its direct effect on the psychic economy (libido). In IWFY the socially acceptable surrender to the husband’s authority keeps the woman from experiencing neurotic fears. At the same time it satisfies masochistic needs, if they exist, using masochism not in the sense of self-abnegation but with its classical meaning of sexual excitement in situations of deprivation, humiliation or pain. That is, it excites her to be deprived and dominated.

游戏的内在心理优势在于其对心理经济（力比多）的直接影响。在IWFY中，社会认可的对丈夫权威的顺从使女性免于产生神经质的恐惧。同时，它满足了女性的受虐需求（如果存在的话），这里的受虐并非指自我否定，而是指在被剥夺、羞辱或痛苦的情境下产生的性兴奋。也就是说，它激发了女性被剥夺和被支配的欲望。

External psychological advantage is the avoidance of the feared situation by playing the game. This is especially obvious in IWFY, where it is the outstanding motivation: by complying with the husband’s strictures, the wife avoids the public situations which she fears.

外部心理优势在于通过参与游戏来避免恐惧的情境。这一点在《IWFY》中尤为明显，它是该游戏中最突出的动机：妻子通过顺从丈夫的规矩来避免她所恐惧的公开场合。

Internal social advantage is designated by the name of the game as it is played in the individual’s intimate circle. By her compliance, the wife gains the privilege of saying ‘If it weren’t for you’. This helps to structure the time she must spend with her husband; in the case of Mrs White, this need for structure was especially strong because of the lack of other common interests, especially before the arrival of their offspring and after the children were grown. In between, the game was played less intensively and less frequently, because the children performed their usual function of structuring time for their parents, and also provided an even more widely accepted version of IWFY, the busy-housewife variation. The fact that young mothers in America often really are very busy does not change the analysis of this variation. Game analysis only attempts to answer this question without prejudice: given that a young woman is busy, how does she go about exploiting her busyness in order to get some compensation for it?

内部社会优势体现在游戏名称上，因为它是在个人的亲密圈子中进行的。妻子通过顺从，获得了说“要不是你”的特权。这有助于她安排与丈夫相处的时间；对于怀特太太来说，这种对结构的需求尤为强烈，因为缺乏其他共同兴趣，尤其是在孩子出生前和孩子长大后。在孩子出生前后，这种游戏进行的频率和强度都降低了，因为孩子们承担了为父母安排时间的日常功能，并且也提供了一种更广为接受的“要不是你”版本——忙碌主妇变体。美国年轻母亲通常确实非常忙碌这一事实，并不会改变对这种变体的分析。博弈论只是试图客观地回答这个问题：假设一位年轻女性很忙，她如何利用自己的忙碌来获得一些补偿？

External social advantage is designated by the use made of the situation in outside social contacts. In the case of the game ‘If It Weren’t For You’, which is what the wife says to her husband, there is a transformation into the pastime ‘If It Weren’t For Him’ when she meets with her friends over morning coffee. Again, the influence of games in the selection of social companions is shown. The new neighbour who is invited for morning coffee is being invited to play ‘If It Weren’t For Him’. If she plays, well and good, she will soon be a bosom friend of the old-timers, other things being equal. If she refuses to play and insists on taking a charitable view of her husband, she will not last long. Her situation will be the same as if she kept refusing to drink at cocktail parties – in most circles, she would gradually be dropped from the guest lists.

外部社会优势体现在人们如何利用自身处境进行外部社交互动。例如，妻子对丈夫说的那句“要不是你”，在她与朋友们喝早咖啡时，就变成了“要不是他”。这再次表明，游戏对社交伙伴的选择有着重要影响。新邻居被邀请来喝早咖啡，实际上是被邀请玩“要不是他”。如果她玩了，那当然很好，在其他条件相同的情况下，她很快就会成为老朋友们的知己。如果她拒绝玩，坚持对丈夫抱有同情心，那她也待不长久。她的处境就好比她在鸡尾酒会上一直拒绝喝酒——在大多数社交圈里，她最终都会被从宾客名单中剔除。

This completes the analysis of the formal features of IWFY. In order to clarify the procedure further, the analysis of ‘Why Don’t You – Yes But’, which is the most common game played at social gatherings, committee meetings and psychotherapy groups the world over, should be consulted ( page 101 ).

至此，IWFY 的形式特征分析完毕。为了进一步阐明该程序，应参考“Why Don’t You – Yes But”游戏的分析（第 101 页），该游戏是世界各地社交聚会、委员会会议和心理治疗小组中最常见的游戏。

3 · THE GENESIS OF GAMES

3. 游戏的起源

From the present point of view, child rearing may be regarded as an educational process in which the child is taught what games to play and how to play them. He is also taught procedures, rituals and pastimes appropriate to his position in the local social situation, but these are less significant. His knowledge of and skill in procedures, rituals and pastimes determine what opportunities will be available to him, other things being equal; but his games determine the use he will make of those opportunities, and the outcomes of situations for which he is eligible. As elements of his script, or unconscious life-plan, his favoured games also determine his ultimate destiny (again with other things being equal): the payoffs on his marriage and career, and the circumstances surrounding his death.

从目前的角度来看，育儿可以被视为一个教育过程，在这个过程中，孩子被教导玩什么游戏以及如何玩。他也被教导一些与其在当地社会环境中的地位相适应的程序、仪式和消遣活动，但这些相对次要。在其他条件相同的情况下，他对这些程序、仪式和消遣活动的了解和技能决定了他所能获得的机会；而他所玩的游戏则决定了他如何利用这些机会，以及他所处境况的最终结果。作为他人生剧本或无意识人生规划的一部分，他所喜爱的游戏也决定了他最终的命运（同样在其他条件相同的情况下）：婚姻和事业的回报，以及他死亡时的境况。

While conscientious parents devote a great deal of attention to teaching their children procedures, rituals and pastimes appropriate to their stations in life, and with equal care select schools, colleges and churches where their teachings will be reinforced, they tend to overlook the question of games, which form the basic structure for the emotional dynamics of each family, and which the children learn through significant experiences in everyday living from their earliest months. Related questions have been discussed for thousands of years in a rather general, unsystematic fashion, and there has been some attempt at a more methodical approach in the modern orthopsychiatric literature; but without the concept of games there is little possibility of a consistent investigation. Theories of internal individual psychodynamics have so far not been able to solve satisfactorily the problems of human relationships. These are transactional situations which call for a theory of social dynamics that cannot be derived solely from consideration of individual motivations.

尽职尽责的父母虽然花费大量精力教导孩子与其人生阶段相符的礼仪、习俗和消遣，并同样精心挑选能够巩固这些教诲的学校、学院和教会，但他们往往忽略了游戏的重要性。游戏构成了每个家庭情感动力的基础结构，孩子们从出生后的几个月起，便通过日常生活中的重要体验来学习游戏。数千年来，人们以一种相当笼统、缺乏系统的方式探讨了相关问题，现代正统精神病学文献中也曾尝试过一些更为系统的方法；但如果没有游戏的概念，就很难进行连贯的研究。迄今为止，关于个体内部心理动力学的理论还无法令人满意地解决人际关系的问题。人际关系是互动性的情境，需要一种社会动力学理论，而这种理论不能仅仅基于对个体动机的考量。

Since there are as yet few well-trained specialists in child psychology and child psychiatry who are also trained in game analysis, observations on the genesis of games are sparse. Fortunately, the following episode took place in the presence of a well-educated transactional analyst.

由于目前既精通儿童心理学和儿童精神病学，又接受过游戏分析训练的专家寥寥无几，因此关于游戏起源的观察资料十分匮乏。幸运的是，接下来的事件发生时，一位受过良好教育的交互分析师在场。

Tanjy, age seven, got a stomach-ache at the dinner table and asked to be excused for that reason. His parents suggested that he lie down for a while. His little brother Mike, age three, then said, ‘I have a stomach-ache too,’ evidently angling for the same consideration. The father looked at him for a few seconds and then replied, ‘You don’t want to play that game, do you?’ Whereupon Mike burst out laughing and said, ‘No!’

七岁的坦吉在餐桌上肚子疼，便请求父母让他先休息一会儿。父母建议他躺下休息一会儿。这时，三岁的弟弟迈克也说：“我也肚子疼。”显然，他是想博取同样的宽容。爸爸看了他几秒钟，然后说：“你不想玩这个游戏，对吧？”迈克听了哈哈大笑，说道：“不想！”

If this had been a household of food or bowel faddists, Mike would also have been packed off to bed by his alarmed parents. If he and they had repeated this performance several times, it might be anticipated that this game would have become part of Mike’s character, as it so often does if the parents cooperate. Whenever he was jealous of a privilege granted to a competitor, he would plead illness in order to get some privileges himself. The ulterior transaction would then consist of: (social level) ‘I don’t feel well’ + (psychological level) ‘You must grant me a privilege, too.’ Mike, however, was saved from such a hypochondriacal career. Perhaps he will end up with a worse fate, but that is not the issue. The issue is that a game in statu nascendi was broken up right there by the father’s question and by the boy’s frank acknowledgement that what he proposed was a game.

如果这是一个对食物或排便有特殊癖好的家庭，迈克也会被惊慌失措的父母赶回床上睡觉。如果他和父母反复上演这种戏码，那么这种游戏很可能会成为迈克性格的一部分，就像父母配合时经常发生的那样。每当他嫉妒竞争对手获得的特权时，他就会装病，以便自己也能获得一些特权。这背后的交易是：（社交层面）“我不舒服”+（心理层面）“你也必须给我一个特权”。然而，迈克却避免了走上这种疑病症的道路。也许他最终会遭遇更糟糕的命运，但这并非重点。重点在于，一场刚刚开始的游戏，就被父亲的提问和男孩坦诚地承认自己提出的只是一场游戏而打破了。

This demonstrates clearly enough that games are quite deliberately initiated by young children. After they become fixed patterns of stimulus and response, their origins become lost in the mists of time and their ulterior nature becomes obscured by social fogs. Both can be brought into awareness only by appropriate procedures : the origin by some form of analytic therapy and the ulterior aspect by antithesis. Repeated clinical experience along these lines makes it clear that games are imitative in nature, and that they are initially set up by the Adult (neopsychic) aspect of the child’s personality. If the Child ego state can be revived in the grown-up player, the psychological aptitude of this segment (the Adult aspect of the Child ego state) is so striking, and its skill in manipulating people so enviable, that it is colloquially called ‘The Professor’ (of Psychiatry). Hence in psychotherapy groups which concentrate on game analysis, one of the more sophisticated procedures is the search for the little ‘Professor’ in each patient, whose early adventures in setting up games between the ages of two and eight are listened to by everyone present with fascination and often, unless the games are tragic, with enjoyment and even hilarity, in which the patient himself may join with justifiable self-appreciation and smugness. Once he is able to do that, he is well on his way to relinquishing what may be an unfortunate behaviour pattern which he is much better off without.

这足以证明，游戏是由幼儿有意发起的。当游戏演变成固定的刺激与反应模式后，其起源便湮没在时间的迷雾中，其内在本质也被社会迷雾所掩盖。只有通过适当的方法才能使这两方面都变得清晰可见：起源可以通过某种形式的分析疗法来揭示，而内在本质则可以通过对比分析来阐明。反复的临床经验表明，游戏本质上是模仿性的，并且最初是由儿童人格中的成人（新心理）层面所设定的。如果成年玩家能够重新唤起儿童自我状态，那么这一部分（儿童自我状态中的成人层面）的心理能力将非常惊人，其操纵他人的技巧也令人艳羡，以至于人们将其俗称为“（精神病学的）教授”。因此，在以游戏分析为重点的心理治疗小组中，一项较为精妙的程序是寻找每位患者内心深处的“小教授”。在场的每个人都饶有兴致地聆听着他们在两岁到八岁之间创造游戏的早期冒险经历，除非游戏本身充满悲剧色彩，否则大家往往乐在其中，甚至捧腹大笑。患者本人也可能带着理所当然的自我欣赏和沾沾自喜加入其中。一旦他能够做到这一点，他就离摆脱某种不幸的行为模式不远了，而摆脱这种模式对他来说意义重大。

Those are the reasons why in the formal description of a game an attempt is always made to describe the infantile or childhood prototype.

这就是为什么在对一款游戏进行正式描述时，总是要尝试描述其婴儿期或童年时期的原型。

4 · THE FUNCTION OF GAMES

4. 游戏的功能

Because there is so little opportunity for intimacy in daily life, and because some forms of intimacy (especially if intense) are psychologically impossible for most people, the bulk of the time in serious social life is taken up with playing games. Hence games are both necessary and desirable, and the only problem at issue is whether the games played by an individual offer the best yield for him. In this connexion it should be remembered that the essential feature of a game is its culmination, or payoff. The principal function of the preliminary moves is to set up the situation for this payoff, but they are always designed to harvest the maximum permissible satisfaction at each step as a secondary product. Thus in ‘Schlemiel’ (making messes and then apologizing) the payoff, and the purpose of the game, is to obtain the forgiveness which is forced by the apology; the spillings and cigarette burns are only steps leading up to this, but each such trespass yields its own pleasure. The enjoyment derived from the spilling does not make spilling a game. The apology is the critical stimulus that leads to the denouement. Otherwise the spilling would simply be a destructive procedure, a delinquency perhaps enjoyable.

由于日常生活中亲密关系的机会寥寥无几，而且某些形式的亲密关系（尤其是强烈的亲密关系）对大多数人来说在心理上是难以实现的，因此，严肃的社交生活中，大部分时间都花在了玩游戏上。由此可见，游戏既是必要的，也是可取的，唯一的问题在于，个人所玩的游戏是否能给他带来最大的收益。在此，我们应该记住，游戏的本质特征在于其最终结果，或者说回报。前期步骤的主要功能是为最终的回报创造条件，但它们的设计目的始终在于在每个步骤中获取最大程度的满足感，而这本身就是一种次要结果。因此，在“Schlemiel”（弄脏东西然后道歉）游戏中，回报，以及游戏的目的，在于获得道歉所带来的宽恕；洒东西和烟头烫伤只是通往这一目标的步骤，但每一次这样的过错都能带来其自身的乐趣。从洒东西中获得的乐趣并不能使洒东西本身成为一种游戏。道歉是促成结局的关键因素。否则，泄露事件就只会变成一种破坏性的行为，一种或许令人愉悦的犯罪行为。

The game of ‘Alcoholic’ is similar; whatever the physiological origin, if any, of the need to drink, in terms of game analysis the imbibing is merely a move in a game which is carried on with the people in the environment. The drinking may bring its own kinds of pleasure, but it is not the essence of the game. This is demonstrated in the variant of ‘Dry Alcoholic’, which involves the same moves and leads to the same payoff as the regular game, but is played without any bottles ( page 66 ).

“酗酒者”游戏与之类似；无论饮酒的生理根源是什么（如果有的话），从游戏分析的角度来看，饮酒仅仅是与周围人进行的游戏中的一个步骤。饮酒或许会带来某种快感，但这并非游戏的本质。这一点在“无酒精酗酒者”的变体游戏中得到了体现，该变体游戏包含与常规游戏相同的步骤，并最终获得相同的回报，但游戏中不使用任何酒瓶（第66页）。

Beyond their social function in structuring time satisfactorily, some games are urgently necessary for the maintenance of health in certain individuals. These people’s psychic stability is so precarious, and their positions are so tenuously maintained, that to deprive them of their games may plunge them into irreversible despair and even psychosis. Such people will fight very hard against any antithetical moves. This is often observed in marital situations when the psychiatric improvement of one spouse (i.e., the abandonment of destructive games) leads to rapid deterioration in the other spouse, to whom the games were of paramount importance in maintaining equilibrium. Hence it is necessary to exercise prudence in game analysis.

除了在合理安排时间方面发挥社会功能外，某些游戏对于某些人的健康至关重要。这些人的心理稳定性极度脆弱，他们的处境也岌岌可危，剥夺他们的游戏可能会使他们陷入不可逆转的绝望，甚至精神错乱。这些人会极力抵制任何相反的举动。这种情况在婚姻关系中经常出现：一方的精神状况改善（即放弃破坏性游戏）会导致另一方迅速恶化，因为游戏对后者维持平衡至关重要。因此，在进行博弈分析时必须谨慎行事。

Fortunately, the rewards of game-free intimacy, which is or should be the most perfect form of human living, are so great that even precariously balanced personalities can safely and joyfully relinquish their games if an appropriate partner can be found for the better relationship.

幸运的是，不玩弄感情的亲密关系（这是或应该是人类生活最完美的形式）带来的回报是如此巨大，以至于即使是性格不稳定的人，如果能找到合适的伴侣来建立更好的关系，也能安全快乐地放弃他们的游戏。

On a larger scale, games are integral and dynamic components of the unconscious life-plan, or script, of each individual; they serve to fill in the time while he waits for the final fulfilment, simultaneously advancing the action. Since the last act of a script characteristically calls for either a miracle or a catastrophe, depending on whether the script is constructive or destructive, the corresponding games are accordingly either constructive or destructive. In colloquial terms, an individual whose script is oriented towards ‘waiting for Santa Claus’ is likely to be pleasant to deal with in such games as ‘Gee You’re Wonderful, Mr Murgatroyd’, while someone with a tragic script oriented towards ‘waiting for rigor mortis to set in’ may play such disagreeable games as ‘Now I’ve Got You, You Son of a Bitch’.

从更宏观的角度来看，游戏是每个人无意识人生计划或剧本中不可或缺且充满活力的组成部分；它们填补了等待最终结局到来的空虚时光，同时推动着剧情发展。由于剧本的最终结局通常需要奇迹或灾难的发生（取决于剧本是建设性的还是破坏性的），相应的游戏也相应地具有建设性或破坏性。通俗地说，一个剧本以“等待圣诞老人”为导向的人，在玩“哇，你真棒，默格特罗伊德先生”这类游戏时，可能会表现得比较友善；而一个剧本以“等待尸僵”为导向的悲剧人物，则可能会玩“现在我抓到你了，你这混蛋”这类令人不快的游戏。

It should be noted that colloquialisms such as those in the previous sentence are an integral part of game analysis, and are freely used in transactional psychotherapy groups and seminars. The expression ‘waiting for rigor mortis to set in’ originated in a dream of a patient, in which she decided to get certain things done ‘before rigor mortis set in’. A patient in a sophisticated group pointed out what the therapist had overlooked: that in practice, waiting for Santa Claus and waiting for death are synonymous. Since colloquialisms are of decisive importance in game analysis, they will be discussed at length later on.

值得注意的是，像上一句中那样的口语表达是游戏分析不可或缺的一部分，在互动式心理治疗小组和研讨会中被广泛使用。“等待尸僵”这一表达源于一位患者的梦境，梦中她决定在“尸僵”出现之前完成某些事情。一位参加高级小组的患者指出了治疗师忽略的一点：在现实生活中，等待圣诞老人和等待死亡是同义词。由于口语表达在游戏分析中至关重要，我们将在后文中详细讨论它们。

5 · THE CLASSIFICATION OF GAMES

5. 游戏分类

Most of the variables used in analysing games and pastimes have already been mentioned, and any of them can be used in classifying games and pastimes systematically. Some of the more obvious classifications are based on the following factors:

用于分析游戏和消遣活动的多数变量已在前面提及，其中任何一个变量都可用于对游戏和消遣活动进行系统分类。一些比较明显的分类基于以下因素：

1. Number of players: two-handed games (Frigid Woman), three-handed games (Let’s You and Him Fight), five-handed games (Alcoholic) and many-handed games (Why Don’t You – Yes But).

1. 玩家人数：两人游戏（冷漠的女人）、三人游戏（让你和他打一架）、五人游戏（酗酒者）和多人游戏（你为什么不——是的，但是）。

2. Currency used: words (Psychiatry), money (Debtor), parts of the body (Polysurgery).

2. 使用的货币：文字（精神病学），金钱（债务人），身体部位（综合外科）。

3. Clinical types: hysterical (Rapo), obsessive-compulsive (Schlemiel), paranoid (Why Does This Have to Happen to Me), depressive (There I Go Again).

3. 临床类型：歇斯底里型（拉波）、强迫型（施莱米尔）、偏执型（为什么这种事会发生在我身上）、抑郁型（我又来了）。

4. Zonal: oral (Alcoholic), anal (Schlemiel), phallic (Let’s You and Him Fight).

4. 区域：口部（酒精中毒），肛门（笨蛋），阴茎（让你和他打架）。

5. Psychodynamic: counterphobic (If It Weren’t for You), projective (PTA), introjective (Psychiatry).

5. 精神动力学：反恐惧（如果不是因为你），投射（PTA），内摄（精神病学）。

6. Instinctual: masochistic (If It Weren’t for You), sadistic (Schlemiel), fetishistic (Frigid Man).

6. 本能：受虐狂（如果不是因为你），施虐狂（笨蛋），恋物癖（冷漠的男人）。

In addition to the number of players, three other quantitative variables are often useful to consider:

除了玩家人数之外，通常还需要考虑其他三个定量变量：

1. Flexibility. Some games, such as Debtor and Polysurgery, can be played properly with only one kind of currency, while others, such as exhibitionistic games, are more flexible.

1. 灵活性。有些游戏，例如《债务人》和《多重手术》，只需要一种货币就能正常进行，而另一些游戏，例如表演类游戏，则更加灵活。

2. Tenacity. Some people give up their games easily, others are persistent.

2. 毅力。有些人很容易放弃游戏，而有些人则坚持不懈。

3. Intensity. Some people play their games in a relaxed way, others are more tense and aggressive. Games so played are known as easy and hard games, respectively.

3. 强度。有些人玩游戏时比较放松，有些人则比较紧张激烈。这两种玩法分别被称为简单游戏和困难游戏。

These three variables converge to make games gentle or violent. In mentally disturbed people, there is often a noticeable progression in this respect, so that one can speak of stages. A paranoid schizophrenic may initially play a flexible, loose, easy game of first-stage ‘Ain’t It Awful’ and progress to an inflexible, tenacious, hard third stage. The stages in a game are distinguished as follows:

这三个变量共同决定了游戏的温和程度或暴力程度。在精神障碍患者中，这方面通常存在明显的进展，因此可以称之为阶段性变化。例如，偏执型精神分裂症患者最初可能玩的是轻松随意的“Ain't It Awful”第一阶段游戏，然后逐渐过渡到僵硬顽固的第三阶段。游戏的各个阶段可区分如下：

(a) A First-Degree Game is one which is socially acceptable in the agent’s circle.

（a）一级博弈是指在行为者的社交圈中被社会接受的博弈。

(b) A Second-Degree Game is one from which no permanent irremediable damage arises, but which the players would rather conceal from the public.

（b）二级博弈是指不会造成永久性、不可弥补的损害，但参与者宁愿向公众隐瞒的博弈。

(c) A Third-Degree Game is one which is played for keeps, and which ends in the surgery, the courtroom or the morgue.

（c）三级游戏是指玩真的游戏，最终以手术、法庭或停尸房告终。

Games can also be classified according to any of the other specific factors discussed in the analysis of IWFY: the aims, the roles, the most obvious advantages. The most likely candidate for a systematic, scientific classification is probably one based on the existential position; but since knowledge of this factor is not yet sufficiently advanced, such a classification will have to be postponed. Failing that, the most practical classification at present is probably a sociological one. That is what will be used in the next section.

游戏还可以根据国际世界锦标赛分析中讨论的其他具体因素进行分类，例如目标、角色和最明显的优势。最有可能进行系统、科学分类的或许是基于存在主义立场的分类；但由于对这一因素的认识尚不充分，这种分类不得不推迟。如果无法进行系统分类，目前最实用的分类或许是社会学分类。下一节将采用这种分类方法。

NOTES

笔记

Due credit should be given to Stephen Potter for his perceptive, humorous discussions of manoeuvres, or ‘ploys’, in everyday social situations, 2 and to G. H. Mead for his pioneering study of the role of games in social living. 3 Those games that lead to psychiatric disabilities have been systematically studied at the San Francisco Social Psychiatry Seminars since 1958, and this sector of game analysis has recently been approached by T. Szasz. 4 For the role of games in the group process, the present writer’s book on group dynamics should be consulted. 5

斯蒂芬·波特对日常社交情境中的各种策略或“计谋”进行了敏锐而幽默的探讨，值得我们给予应有的赞扬。G·H·米德则开创性地研究了游戏在社会生活中的作用，也应得到肯定。自1958年以来，旧金山社会精神病学研讨会一直在系统地研究那些会导致精神障碍的游戏，而T·萨斯最近也开始关注游戏分析的这一领域。关于游戏在群体过程中的作用，请参阅笔者撰写的关于群体动力学的著作。
