#↩

PART TWO

第二部分

#↩

A THESAURUS OF GAMES

游戏词典

#↩

Introduction

介绍

T HIS collection is complete to date (1962), but new games are continually being discovered. Sometimes what appears to be another example of a known game turns out, on more careful study, to be an entirely new one, and a game which appears to be new often turns out to be a variation of a known one. The individual items of the analyses are also subject to change as new knowledge accumulates; for example, where there are several possible choices in describing dynamics, the statement given may turn out later not to have been the most cogent one. Both the list of games and the items given in the analyses, however, areadequate for clinical work.

本合集截至1962年已完整收录，但新的游戏仍在不断涌现。有时，看似已知游戏的又一例证，经仔细研究后却发现是全新的游戏；而看似全新的游戏，往往实际上是已知游戏的变体。随着新知识的积累，分析中的具体内容也会随之改变；例如，在描述游戏动态时，如果存在多种可能的表述，那么之前给出的表述可能并非最恰当的。然而，无论是游戏列表还是分析中的具体内容，都足以满足临床应用的需求。

Some of the games are discussed and analysed in extenso. Others, which require more investigation, or are uncommon, or whose significance is fairly obvious, are only briefly mentioned. The one who is ‘it’ is generally referred to as the ‘agent’, or is given the name of ‘White’, while the other party is called ‘Black’.

有些棋局会进行详尽的讨论和分析。而另一些棋局，例如需要更多研究、较为罕见或意义显而易见的棋局，则仅作简要提及。通常，扮演“鬼”的一方被称为“代理人”，或被称为“白方”，而另一方则被称为“黑方”。

The games are classified into families according to the situations in which they most commonly occur: Life Games, Marital Games, Party Games, Sexual Games and Underworld Games; then comes a section for professionals on Consulting Room Games, and finally, some examples of Good Games.

这些游戏根据它们最常发生的场景分为以下几类：生活游戏、婚姻游戏、派对游戏、性游戏和黑社会游戏；接下来是面向专业人士的咨询室游戏部分，最后是一些好游戏的例子。

1 · NOTATION

1 · 符号

The following notation will be used in the analytic protocols.

分析协议中将使用以下符号。

Title: if the game has a long name, a convenient abbreviation is used in the text. Where a game or its variations has more than one name, a cross reference will be found in the Index of Games. In oral reports it is preferable to use the full name of the game rather than its abbreviation or acronym.

标题：如果游戏名称较长，正文中会使用方便的缩写。如果某个游戏或其变体有多个名称，可在游戏索引中找到交叉引用。口头报告时，最好使用游戏的完整名称，而不是缩写或首字母缩略词。

Thesis: this is restated as cogently as possible.

论点：尽可能简洁明了地重述此论点。

Aim: this gives the most meaningful choice, based on the writer’s experience.

目的：根据作者的经验，做出最有意义的选择。

Roles: the role of the one who is ‘it’, and from whose point of view the game is discussed, is given first, in italics.

角色：首先用斜体字标出扮演“它”的人的角色，以及从其角度讨论游戏的角色。

Dynamics: as with aim.

动态：如同瞄准。

Examples: (1) this gives an illustration of the game as played in childhood, the most easily recognizable pertinent prototype. (2) an illustration from adult life.

例如：（1）这幅图展示了儿童时期玩这款游戏的场景，这是最容易识别的相关原型。（2）这幅图展示了成年生活中玩这款游戏的场景。

Paradigm: this illustrates as briefly as possible the critical transaction or transactions at the social and psychological levels.

范式：这尽可能简明扼要地说明了社会和心理层面上的关键交易或互动。

Moves: this gives the minimum number of transactional stimuli and transactional responses as found in practice. These may be expanded, diluted or ornamented to an unlimited extent in different situations.

行动方案：这给出了实践中实际存在的最少数量的交易刺激和交易反应。在不同的情况下，这些刺激和反应可以被无限扩展、稀释或修饰。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – this attempts to state how the game contributes to internal psychic stability. (2) External Psychological – this attempts to state what anxiety-arousing situations or intimacies are being avoided. (3) Internal Social – this gives the characteristic phrase used in the game as played with intimates. (4) External Social – this gives the key phrase used in the derivative game or pastime played in less intimate circles. (5) Biological – this attempts to characterize the kind of stroking which the game offers to the parties involved. (6) Existential – this states the position from which the game is typically played.

优势：（1）内在心理层面——试图阐明游戏如何促进内在心理稳定。（2）外在心理层面——试图阐明游戏旨在避免哪些引发焦虑的情境或亲密关系。（3）内在社交层面——阐述与亲密对象进行游戏时所使用的典型短语。（4）外在社交层面——阐述衍生游戏或在不太亲密的圈子中进行的消遣活动所使用的关键短语。（5）生理层面——试图描述游戏为参与者提供的抚慰方式。（6）存在层面——阐述游戏通常进行的立场。

Relatives: this gives the names of complementary, allied and antithetical games.

亲属关系：这给出了互补游戏、同盟游戏和对立游戏的名称。

An adequate understanding of a game can only be obtained in the psychotherapeutic situation. People who play destructive games will come to the therapist far more frequently than people who play constructive ones. Therefore most of the games which are well understood are basically destructive, but the reader should remember that there are constructive ones played by more fortunate people. And to prevent the idea of games from becoming vulgarized, as so many psychiatric terms are, it should be emphasized once more that it is a very precise idea: games should be clearly distinguished, by the criteria given previously, from procedures, rituals, pastimes, operations, manoeuvres and the attitudes which arise from various positions. A game is played from a position, but a position or its corresponding attitude is not a game.

只有在心理治疗情境中才能充分理解游戏。玩破坏性游戏的人比玩建设性游戏的人更频繁地寻求治疗师的帮助。因此，大多数被充分理解的游戏本质上都是破坏性的，但读者应该记住，也有一些幸运的人玩建设性游戏。为了防止“游戏”的概念像许多精神病学术语一样被庸俗化，需要再次强调，这是一个非常精确的概念：根据前面提到的标准，游戏应该与程序、仪式、消遣、操作、策略以及由各种立场产生的态度明确区分开来。游戏是从某种立场出发的，但立场或其相应的态度本身并不是游戏。

2 · COLLOQUIALISMS

2 · 口语化表达

Many colloquialisms used here were supplied by patients. All of them, if used with due regard to timing and sensibilities, are appreciated, understood and enjoyed by the players. If some of them seem disrespectful, the irony is directed against the games and not against the people who play them. The first requirement for colloquialisms is aptness, and if they often sound amusing, that is precisely because they hit the nail on the head. As I have tried to show elsewhere in discussing colloquial epithets, a whole page of learned polysyllables may not convey as much as the statement that a certain woman is a bitch, or that a certain man is a jerk. 1 Psychological truths may be stated for academic purposes in scientific language, but the effective recognition of emotional strivings in practice may require a different approach. So we prefer playing ‘Ain’t It Awful’ to ‘verbalizing projected anal aggression’. The former not only has a more dynamic meaning and impact, but it is actually more precise. And sometimes people get better faster in bright rooms than they do in drab ones.

这里使用的许多俚语都来自患者。所有这些俚语，只要使用得当，注意时机和语气，都能被玩家理解、欣赏和享受。如果有些俚语听起来不太尊重人，那讽刺的是游戏本身，而不是玩家。俚语的首要条件是贴切，如果它们听起来常常很有趣，那恰恰是因为它们一针见血。正如我在其他讨论俚语形容词时所指出的，一整页晦涩难懂的多音节词汇可能还不如直接说某个女人是“婊子”，或者某个男人是“混蛋”来得有力。心理学真理可以用科学语言进行学术阐述，但在实践中有效地识别情感诉求可能需要不同的方法。因此，我们更喜欢玩“Ain't It Awful”游戏，而不是“用言语表达投射出的肛门攻击”。前者不仅更具动态意义和影响力，而且实际上也更精准。有时，人们在明亮的房间里比在阴暗的房间里进步更快。

REFERENCE

参考

1. Berne, E., ‘Intution IV: Primal Images & Primal Judgments’, Psychiatric Quarterly , 29: 634-658, 1955.

1. Berne, E., ‘直觉 IV：原始意象和原始判断’，精神病学季刊，29: 634-658, 1955。

#↩

6 · Life Games

6 · 人生游戏

A LL games have an important and probably decisive influence on the destinies of the players under ordinary social conditions; but some offer more opportunities than others for life-long careers and are more likely to involve relatively innocent bystanders. This group may be conveniently called Life Games. It includes ‘Alcoholic’, ‘Debtor’, ‘Kick Me’, ‘Now I’ve Got You, You Son of a Bitch’, ‘See What You Made Me Do’ and their principal variants. They merge on the one side with marital games, and on the other with those of the underworld.

在普通的社会条件下，所有游戏都会对玩家的命运产生重要甚至决定性的影响；但有些游戏比其他游戏更能为玩家提供终身职业发展的机会，也更容易牵涉到相对无辜的旁观者。这类游戏可以方便地称为“人生游戏”。它包括“酗酒游戏”、“债务游戏”、“踢我游戏”、“现在我抓到你了，你这混蛋”、“看看你都做了些什么”以及它们的主要变体。它们一方面与婚姻游戏相融合，另一方面又与黑社会游戏有所关联。

1 · ALCOHOLIC

1. 含酒精的

Thesis. In game analysis there is no such thing as alcoholism or ‘an alcoholic’, but there is a role called the Alcoholic in a certain type of game. If a biochemical or physiological abnormality is the prime mover in excessive drinking – and that is still open to some question – then its study belongs in the field of internal medicine. Game analysis is interested in something quite different – the kinds of social transactions that are related to such excesses. Hence the game ‘Alcoholic’.

论文：在博弈分析中，并不存在酗酒或“酗酒者”这样的概念，但在某种类型的博弈中，存在一个名为“酗酒者”的角色。如果生化或生理异常是过度饮酒的主要原因——这一点仍有待商榷——那么对它的研究就属于内科的范畴。博弈分析关注的是截然不同的东西——与这种过度行为相关的各种社会互动。因此，就有了“酗酒者”这个博弈。

In its full flower this is a five-handed game, although the roles may be condensed so that it starts off and terminates as a two-handed one. The central role is that of the Alcoholic – the one who is ‘it’ – played by White. The chief supporting role is that of Persecutor, typically played by a member of the opposite sex, usually the spouse. The third role is that of Rescuer, usually played by someone of the same sex, often the good family doctor who is interested in the patient and also in drinking problems. In the classical situation the doctor successfully rescues the alcoholic from his habit. After White has not taken a drink for six months they congratulate each other. The following day White is found in the gutter.

完整的游戏规则是五人参与，但角色可以简化，使其以两人游戏开始和结束。核心角色是“酒鬼”——也就是“鬼”——由白人扮演。主要配角是“迫害者”，通常由异性扮演，一般是配偶。第三个角色是“拯救者”，通常由同性扮演，通常是关心病人及其酗酒问题的家庭医生。在经典的剧本中，医生成功地帮助酒鬼戒酒。白人戒酒六个月后，两人互相祝贺。第二天，人们发现白人倒在了街头。

The fourth role is that of the Patsy, or Dummy. In literature this is played by the delicatessen man who extends credit to White, gives him a sandwich on the cuff and perhaps a cup of coffee, without either persecuting him or trying to rescue him. In life this is more frequently played by White’s mother, who gives him money and often sympathizes with him about the wife who does not understand him. In this aspect of the game, White is required to account in some plausible way for his need for money – by some project in which both pretend to believe, although they know what he is really going to spend most of the money for. Sometimes the Patsy slides over into another role, which is a helpful but not essential one: the Agitator, the ‘good guy’ who offers supplies without even being asked for them: ‘Come have a drink with me (and you will go downhill faster).’

第四个角色是替罪羊，或者说傀儡。在文学作品中，这个角色通常由熟食店老板扮演，他会赊账给怀特，随手给他一个三明治，或许还会给他一杯咖啡，既不迫害他，也不试图拯救他。在现实生活中，这个角色更常由怀特的母亲扮演，她会给他钱，并且常常同情他那不理解他的妻子。在这个游戏中，怀特需要用某种看似合理的理由来解释他需要钱的原因——比如通过某个双方都假装相信的项目，尽管他们都知道他真正会把大部分钱花在什么地方。有时，替罪羊会转变为另一个角色，这个角色虽然有用但并非必不可少：煽动者，也就是那个“好人”，他会主动提供各种帮助，甚至在怀特开口之前就说：“来跟我喝一杯吧（这样你会走得更快）。”

The ancillary professional in all drinking games is the bartender or liquor clerk. In the game ‘Alcoholic’ he plays the fifth role, the Connexion, the direct source of supply who also understands alcoholic talk, and who in a way is the most meaningful person in the life of any addict. The difference between the Connexion and the other players is the difference between professionals and amateurs in any game: the professional knows when to stop. At a certain point a good bartender refuses to serve the Alcoholic, who is then left without any supplies unless he can locate a more indulgent Connexion.

在所有饮酒游戏中，辅助专业人士通常是调酒师或酒水售货员。在“酒鬼”游戏中，他扮演第五个角色——联络人，是酒水的直接来源，也了解酒鬼的谈话，某种程度上来说，他是任何酒鬼生命中最重要的人。联络人与其他玩家的区别，就像任何游戏中专业人士和业余玩家的区别一样：专业人士知道何时该停止。到了某个时候，一个好的调酒师会拒绝为酒鬼服务，除非他能找到一个更慷慨的联络人，否则酒鬼就会断货。

In the initial stages of ‘Alcoholic’, the wife may play all three supporting roles: at midnight the Patsy, undressing him, making him coffee and letting him beat up on her; in the morning the Persecutor, berating him for the evil of his ways; and in the evening the Rescuer, pleading with him to change them. In the later stages, due sometimes to organic deterioration, the Persecutor and the Rescuer can be dispensed with, but are tolerated if they are also willing to act as sources of supply. White will go to the Mission House and be rescued if he can get a free meal there; or he will stand for a scolding, amateur or professional, as long as he can get a handout afterwards.

在“酗酒”初期，妻子可能扮演所有三个辅助角色：午夜时分，她是替罪羊，脱掉丈夫的衣服，给他煮咖啡，任由他殴打自己；清晨，她是迫害者，斥责他行为的罪恶；夜晚，她是拯救者，恳求他改过自新。在后期，有时由于生理机能的衰退，迫害者和拯救者的角色可能会被舍弃，但如果她们也愿意提供物质支持，则可以容忍她们的存在。如果能得到一顿免费餐食，怀特就会去救济院寻求帮助；或者，只要事后能得到施舍，他就会忍受训斥，无论训斥者是业余的还是专业的。

Present experience indicates that the payoff in in ‘Alcoholic’ (as is characteristic of games in general) comes from the aspect to which most investigators pay least attention. In the analysis of this game, drinking itself is merely an incidental pleasure having added advantages, the procedure leading up to the real culmination, which is the hangover. It is the same in the game of Schlemiel: the mess-making, which attracts the most attention, is merely a pleasure-giving way for White to lead up to the crux, which is obtaining forgiveness from Black.

目前的经验表明，在“酗酒者”游戏中（这在大多数游戏中都很常见），真正的收益来自于大多数研究者最容易忽略的方面。在分析这款游戏时，饮酒本身仅仅是一种附带的乐趣，而真正的高潮——宿醉——则来自于饮酒的过程。这与“笨蛋游戏”的情况类似：最引人注目的混乱局面，仅仅是白方获得乐趣的一种方式，其最终目的是赢得黑方的原谅。

For the Alcoholic the hangover is not as much the physical pain as the psychological torment. The two favourite pastimes of drinking people are ‘Martini’ (how many drinks and how they were mixed) and ‘Morning After’ (Let me tell you about my hangover). ‘Martini’ is played, for the most part, by social drinkers; many alcoholics prefer a hard round of psychological ‘Morning After’, and organizations such as Alcoholics Anonymous offer him an unlimited opportunity for this.

对酗酒者来说，宿醉与其说是身体上的痛苦，不如说是精神上的折磨。饮酒者最爱的两件事是“马提尼”（数数喝了多少，怎么调的）和“宿醉之后”（跟你说说我的宿醉）。“马提尼”大多是社交饮酒者玩的游戏；许多酗酒者更喜欢经历一场痛苦的“宿醉之后”心理折磨，而像匿名戒酒会这样的组织则为他们提供了无限的机会。

Whenever one patient visited his psychiatrist after a binge, he would call himself all sorts of names; the psychiatrist said nothing. Later, recounting these visits in a therapy group, White said with smug satisfaction that it was the psychiatrist who had called him all those names. The main conversational interest of many alcoholics in the therapeutic situation is not their drinking, which they apparently mention mostly in deference to their persecutors, but their subsequent suffering. The transactional object of the drinking, aside from the personal pleasures it brings, is to set up a situation where the Child can be severely scolded not only by the internal Parent but by any parental figures in the environment who are interested enough to oblige. Hence the therapy of this game should be concentrated not on the drinking but on the morning after, the self-indulgence in self-castigation. There is a type of heavy drinker, however, who does not have hangovers, and such people do not belong in the present category.

每当一位病人在酗酒后去看精神科医生时，他都会对自己进行各种辱骂；而精神科医生却一言不发。后来，怀特在一次治疗小组中回忆起这些就诊经历时，沾沾自喜地说，是精神科医生骂了他那些难听的话。许多酗酒者在治疗情境中的主要谈话兴趣并非他们的饮酒行为（他们提及饮酒似乎大多是为了迎合那些指责他们的人），而是他们随后的痛苦。饮酒的交易目的，除了带来的个人快感之外，还在于营造一种情境，让“孩子”不仅能受到内在“父母”的严厉责骂，还能受到环境中任何愿意配合的“父母”的严厉责骂。因此，这种“游戏”的治疗重点不应放在饮酒本身，而应放在第二天早晨，放在自我惩罚的沉溺之中。然而，有一种酗酒者不会宿醉，这类人并不属于我们讨论的范畴。

There is also a game ‘Dry Alcoholic’, in which White goes through the process of financial or social degradation without a bottle, making the same sequence of moves and requiring the same supporting cast. Here again, the morning after is the crux of the matter. Indeed, it is the similarity between ‘Dry Alcoholic’ and regular ‘Alcoholic’ which emphasizes that both are games; for example, the procedure for getting discharged from a job is the same in both. ‘Addict’ is similar to ‘Alcoholic’, but more sinister, more dramatic, more sensational and faster. In our society, at least, it leans more heavily on the readily available Persecutor, with Patsies and Rescuers being few and far between and the Connexion playing a much more central role.

还有一种叫做“戒酒者”的游戏，在这种游戏中，白方在没有酒的情况下经历经济或社会地位的下降，其走法和所需的辅助角色与普通“酗酒者”相同。同样，宿醉后的第二天早上才是关键所在。事实上，“戒酒者”和普通“酗酒者”之间的相似之处恰恰强调了它们都是游戏；例如，两者的解雇程序完全相同。“瘾君子”与“酗酒者”类似，但更加阴险、更加戏剧化、更加耸人听闻，节奏也更快。至少在我们的社会中，它更依赖于现成的迫害者，替罪羊和救援者寥寥无几，而关系网则扮演着更为核心的角色。

There are a variety of organizations involved in ‘Alcoholic’, some of them national or even international in scope, others local. Many of them publish rules for the game. Nearly all of them explain how to play the role of Alcoholic: take a drink before breakfast, spend money allotted for other purposes, etc. They also explain the function of the Rescuer. Alcoholics Anonymous, for example, continues playing the actual game but concentrates on inducing the Alcoholic to take the role of Rescuer. Former Alcoholics are preferred because they know how the game goes, and hence are better qualified to play the supporting role than people who have never played before. Cases have been reported of a chapter of A.A. running out of Alcoholics to work on; whereupon the members resumed drinking, since there was no other way to continue the game in the absence of people to rescue. 1

参与“酗酒者”游戏的组织多种多样，有些是全国性的甚至国际性的，有些则是地方性的。许多组织都发布了游戏规则。几乎所有组织都会解释如何扮演酗酒者的角色：早餐前喝酒、挪用原本用于其他用途的钱等等。他们还会解释“拯救者”的职责。例如，匿名戒酒会（AA）会继续进行游戏，但重点在于引导酗酒者扮演拯救者的角色。他们更倾向于选择曾经酗酒的人，因为他们了解游戏规则，因此比从未玩过的人更适合扮演支持者的角色。曾有报道称，某个AA分会因为没有酗酒者可供拯救而停止了游戏；由于没有其他办法继续进行游戏，成员们便重新开始喝酒。

There are also organizations devoted to improving the lot of the other players. Some put pressure on the spouses to shift their roles from Persecutor to Rescuer. The one which seems to come closest to the theoretical ideal of treatment deals with teen-age offspring of alcoholics; these young people are encouraged to break away from the game itself, rather than merely shift their roles.

还有一些组织致力于改善其他参与者的境遇。有些组织会向配偶施压，要求他们从迫害者转变为拯救者。其中最接近理想治疗方案的，是针对酗酒者青少年子女的；这些年轻人被鼓励彻底摆脱酗酒的泥潭，而不仅仅是改变他们的角色。

The psychological cure of an alcoholic also lies in getting him to stop playing the game altogether, rather than simply change from one role to another. In some cases this has been feasible, although it is a difficult task to find something else as interesting to the Alcoholic as continuing his game. Since he is classically afraid of intimacy, the substitute may have to be another game rather than a game-free relationship. Often so-called cured alcoholics are not very stimulating company socially, and possibly they feel a lack of excitement in their lives and are continually tempted to go back to their old ways. The criterion of a true ‘game cure’ is that the former Alcoholic should be able to drink socially without putting himself in jeopardy. The usual ‘total abstinence’ cure will not satisfy the game analyst.

对酗酒者进行心理治疗的关键在于让他们彻底停止这种“游戏”，而不仅仅是改变他们扮演的角色。在某些情况下，这并非不可能，但要找到其他能像继续玩“游戏”一样吸引酗酒者的事情却并非易事。由于他们通常害怕亲密关系，因此替代品可能必须是另一种“游戏”，而不是一段没有“游戏”的亲密关系。很多所谓的“治愈”酗酒者在社交场合并不讨喜，他们可能感到生活缺乏激情，并不断受到诱惑重蹈覆辙。真正意义上的“游戏疗法”的标准是，曾经的酗酒者应该能够在社交场合饮酒而不会让自己陷入危险。通常的“完全戒酒”疗法并不能让游戏分析师满意。

It is apparent from the description of this game that there is a strong temptation for the Rescuer to play ‘I’m Only Trying to Help You’; for the Persecutor to play ‘Look What You’ve Done to Me’; and for the Patsy * to play ‘Good Joe’. With the rise of rescue organizations which publicize the idea that alcoholism is a disease, alcoholics have been taught to play ‘Wooden Leg’. The law, which takes a special interest in such people, tends to encourage this nowadays. The emphasis has shifted from the Persecutor to the Rescuer, from ‘I am a sinner’ to ‘What do you expect from a sick man?’ (part of the trend in modern thinking away from religion and towards science). From an existential point of view the shift is questionable, and from a practical point of view it seems to have done little to diminish the sale of liquor to heavy drinkers. Nevertheless, Alcoholics Anonymous is still for most people the best initiation into the therapy of over-indulgence.

从对这款游戏的描述中可以明显看出，拯救者很容易扮演“我只是想帮你”的角色；迫害者很容易扮演“看看你对我做了什么”的角色；而替罪羊则很容易扮演“好人乔”的角色。随着一些救助组织的兴起，这些组织开始宣传酗酒是一种疾病，酗酒者也被教导要扮演“木腿”的角色。法律对这类人群格外关注，如今也倾向于鼓励这种行为。重点已经从迫害者转移到了拯救者，从“我是个罪人”转移到了“你还能指望一个病人做什么？”（这是现代思想从宗教转向科学的趋势之一）。从存在主义的角度来看，这种转变值得商榷；而从实际角度来看，它似乎并没有减少向酗酒者出售酒类的量。然而，对于大多数人来说，匿名戒酒会仍然是开始接受过度放纵治疗的最佳途径。

Antithesis. As is well known, ‘Alcoholic’ is usually played hard and is difficult to give up. In one case a female alcoholic in a therapy group participated very little until she thought she knew enough about the other members to go ahead with her game. She then asked them to tell her what they thought of her. Since she had behaved pleasantly enough, various members said nice things about her, but she protested: ‘That’s not what I want. I want to know what you really think.’ She made it clear that she was seeking derogatory comments. The other women refused to persecute her, whereupon she went home and told her husband that if she took another drink, he must either divorce her or send her to a hospital. He promised to do this, and that evening she became intoxicated and he sent her to a sanitarium. Here the other members refused to play the persecutory roles White assigned to them; she was unable to tolerate this antithetical behaviour, in spite of everyone’s efforts to reinforce whatever insight she had already obtained. At home she found someone who was willing to play the role she demanded.

反面。众所周知，“酗酒者”这个角色通常扮演得很重，而且很难放弃。在一个案例中，一位女性酗酒者参加了一个治疗小组，起初她很少参与，直到她认为自己对其他成员足够了解，可以开始玩她的游戏。然后，她要求她们告诉她对她的看法。由于她表现得相当友好，一些成员说了些好话，但她抗议道：“这不是我想要的。我想知道你们的真实想法。”她明确表示，她想要的是贬损性的评价。其他女性拒绝迫害她，于是她回家告诉丈夫，如果她再喝酒，他要么必须和她离婚，要么必须把她送进医院。丈夫答应了，当晚她喝醉了，丈夫把她送进了疗养院。在这里，其他成员拒绝扮演怀特赋予她们的迫害角色；尽管每个人都努力强化她已经获得的认知，但她仍然无法容忍这种反面行为。回到家后，她找到了一个愿意扮演她所要求的角色的人。

In other cases, however, it appears possible to prepare the patient sufficiently so that the game can be given up, and to attempt a true social cure in which the therapist declines to play either Persecutor or Rescuer. It is equally untherapeutic for him to play the role of Patsy by allowing the patient to forgo his financial and punctuality obligations. The correct therapeutic procedure from a transactional point of view is, after careful preliminary groundwork, to take an Adult contractual position and refuse to play any of the roles, hoping that the patient will be able to tolerate not only abstinence from drinking but also from playing his game. If he cannot, he is best referred to a Rescuer.

然而，在其他情况下，似乎可以对患者进行充分的准备，使其放弃这种游戏，并尝试进行真正的社会治疗，治疗师在治疗过程中既不扮演迫害者，也不扮演拯救者。同样，如果治疗师扮演替罪羊的角色，允许患者放弃其经济和守时义务，也是无益的。从治疗的角度来看，正确的治疗方法是在仔细的初步准备工作之后，采取成年人的契约立场，拒绝扮演任何角色，希望患者不仅能够忍受戒酒，还能忍受放弃这种游戏。如果患者无法做到，最好将其转介给拯救者。

Antithesis is particularly difficult, because the heavy drinker is highly regarded in most Western countries as a desirable object for censure, concern or generosity, and someone who refuses to play any of these roles tends to arouse public indignation. A rational approach may be even more alarming to the Rescuers than to the Alcoholic, sometimes with unfortunate consequences to the therapy. In one clinical situation a group of workers were seriously interested in the game ‘Alcoholic’ and were attempting to effect real cures by breaking up the game rather than merely rescuing the patients. As soon as this became apparent, they were frozen out by the lay committee which was backing the clinic, and none of them was ever again called on to assist in treating these patients.

反面教材尤其难以驾驭，因为在大多数西方国家，酗酒者往往被视为值得谴责、关怀或慷慨对待的对象，而拒绝扮演这些角色的人则往往会激起公众的愤慨。理性的方法对“拯救者”而言可能比对酗酒者本身更令人不安，有时甚至会对治疗造成不利影响。在一次临床案例中，一群工作人员对“酗酒者”游戏非常感兴趣，他们试图通过打断游戏而非仅仅拯救病人来达到真正的治愈效果。一旦他们的意图暴露，支持诊所的非专业人士委员会就将他们排除在外，此后他们再也没有被邀请参与治疗这些病人。

Relatives. An interesting byplay in ‘Alcoholic’ is called ‘Have One’. This was discovered by a perceptive student of industrial psychiatry. White and his wife (a non-drinking Persecutor) go on a picnic with Black and his wife (both Patsies). White says to the Blacks, ‘Have one!’ If they have one, this gives White licence to have four or five. The game is unmasked if the Blacks refuse. White, by the rules of drinking, is then entitled to be insulted, and he will find more compliant companions for his next picnic. What appears at the social level to be Adult generosity, is at the psychological level an act of insolence, whereby White’s Child obtains Parental indulgence from Black by open bribery under the very nose of Mrs White, who is powerless to protest. Actually it is just because she will be ‘powerless’ to protest that Mrs White consents to the whole arrangement, since she is just as anxious for the game to continue, with herself in the role of Persecutor, as Mr White is with himself in the role of Alcoholic. Her recriminations against him in the morning after the picnic are easy to imagine. This variant can cause complications if White is Black’s boss.

亲戚。在《酒鬼》这部剧中，有一个有趣的插曲叫做“喝一杯”。这是由一位敏锐的工业精神病学学生发现的。怀特和他的妻子（一个不喝酒的迫害者）与布莱克和他的妻子（两人都是替罪羊）一起去野餐。怀特对布莱克夫妇说：“喝一杯！”如果他们喝了一杯，怀特就可以喝四五杯。如果布莱克夫妇拒绝，这个游戏就暴露了。按照饮酒的规则，怀特就有权受到侮辱，而且他会在下次野餐时找到更顺从的同伴。在社会层面上，这似乎是成年人的慷慨，但在心理层面上，这是一种傲慢的行为，怀特的孩子通过公开贿赂布莱克，在怀特太太眼皮底下获得了父母般的宽容，而怀特太太却无力反抗。事实上，怀特太太之所以同意整个安排，正是因为她“无力”抗议，因为她和怀特先生一样渴望游戏继续进行，自己扮演迫害者的角色，就像怀特先生渴望自己扮演酗酒者的角色一样。可以想象，野餐后的第二天早上，她会如何责备他。如果怀特是黑方的上司，这种安排可能会引发一些问题。

In general the Patsy is not as badly off as the name implies. Patsies are often lonely people who have a great deal to gain by being nice to Alcoholics. The delicatessen man who plays ‘Good Joe’ makes many acquaintances in this way, and he can get a good reputation in his own social circle not only as a generous person but also as a good storyteller.

一般来说，“替罪羊”的处境并不像名字暗示的那样糟糕。他们往往是孤独的人，通过善待酗酒者而获益良多。熟食店老板扮演的“好人乔”就是这样结识了很多人，不仅因为慷慨大方，还因为能讲故事而在自己的社交圈中赢得了良好的声誉。

One variant of ‘Good Joe’, incidentally, is to go around asking for advice about how best to help people. This is an example of a jolly and constructive game worth encouraging. Its inverse is Tough Guy, taking lessons in violence or asking for advice about how best to hurt people. Although the mayhem is never put into practice, the player has the privilege of associating with real tough guys who are playing for keeps, and can bask in their reflected glory. This is one species of what the French call un fanfaron de vice.

顺便一提，“好人乔”游戏的一个变体是四处征求如何更好地帮助他人的建议。这是一个既有趣又有建设性的游戏，值得鼓励。它的反面是“硬汉”游戏，玩家会学习暴力技巧或征求如何更好地伤害他人的建议。虽然这些暴力行为从未付诸实践，但玩家却有幸结识那些真正玩真的硬汉，并能沾沾他们的光。这正是法国人所说的“恶作剧之风”（un fanfaron de vice）的一种表现形式。

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: How bad I’ve been; see if you can stop me.

论文题目：我有多糟糕；看看你能不能阻止我。

Aim: Self-castigation.

目的：自我惩罚。

Roles: Alcoholic, Persecutor, Rescuer, Patsy, Connexion.

角色：酗酒者、迫害者、拯救者、替罪羊、联络人。

Dynamics: Oral deprivation.

动态：口腔剥夺。

Examples: (1) See if you can catch me. The prototypes of this game are difficult to correlate because of its complexity. Children, however, particularly children of alcoholics, often go through many of the manoeuvres characteristic of the Alcoholic. ‘See if you can stop me’, which involves lying, hiding things, seeking derogatory comments, looking for helpful people, finding a benevolent neighbour who will give free handouts, etc. Self-castigation is often postponed to later years. (2) The alcoholic and his circle.

例如：（1）“看你能不能抓住我”。由于其复杂性，很难找到与此游戏原型相对应的例子。然而，孩子们，尤其是酗酒者的子女，常常会经历许多酗酒者特有的应对方式。“看你能不能阻止我”，这包括撒谎、藏东西、寻求贬损、寻找可以帮忙的人、寻找愿意施舍的仁慈邻居等等。自我惩罚往往会推迟到成年以后。（2）酗酒者及其圈子。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult: ‘Tell me what you really think of me or help me stop drinking.’

成年人：“告诉我你对我的真实想法，或者帮我戒酒。”

Adult: ‘I’ll be frank with you.’

成年人：“我会坦诚地告诉你。”

Psychological Paradigm: Parent-Child.

心理学范式：亲子关系。

Child: ‘See if you can stop me.’

孩子：“看看你能不能阻止我。”

Parent: ‘You must stop drinking because …’

家长：“你必须停止饮酒，因为……”

Moves: (1) Provocation – accusation or forgiveness. (2) Indulgence – anger or disappointment.

策略：（1）挑衅——指责或宽恕。（2）纵容——愤怒或失望。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – (a) Drinking as a procedure – rebellion, reassurance and satisfaction of craving, (b) ‘Alcoholic’ as a game – self-castigation (probable). (2) External Psychological – avoidance of sexual and other forms of intimacy. (3) Internal Social – See if you can stop me. (4) External Social – ‘Morning After’, ‘Martini’, and other pastimes. (5) Biological – alternating loving and angry exchanges. (6) Existential – Everybody wants to deprive me.

优势：(1) 内在心理因素——(a) 饮酒作为一种行为方式——反叛、寻求安慰和满足渴望；(b) “酗酒者”作为一种游戏——自我惩罚（可能）。(2) 外在心理因素——逃避性行为和其他形式的亲密关系。(3) 内在社会因素——看看你能不能阻止我。(4) 外在社会因素——“宿醉”、“马提尼”和其他消遣。(5) 生理因素——爱与怒交替出现。(6) 存在主义因素——每个人都想剥夺我。

2 · DEBTOR

2 · 债务人

Thesis. ‘Debtor’ is more than a game. In America it tends to become a script, a plan for a whole lifetime, just as it does in some of the jungles of Africa and New Guinea. 2 There the relatives of a young man buy him a bride at an enormous price, putting him in their debt for years to come. Here the same custom prevails, at least in the more civilized sections of the country, except that the bride price becomes a house price, and if there is no stake from the relatives, this role is taken on by the bank.

论文。“债务人”不仅仅是一场游戏。在美国，它往往会变成一种剧本，一种贯穿一生的计划，就像在非洲和新几内亚的一些丛林地区一样。在那些地方，年轻人的亲戚会花重金为他买新娘，让他背负多年的债务。在美国，至少在较为文明的地区，同样的习俗依然存在，只不过彩礼变成了房款，如果亲戚没有出资，银行就会承担起这个角色。

Thus the young man in New Guinea with an old wrist watch dangling from his ear to ensure success, and the young man in America with a new wrist watch wrapped around his arm to ensure success, both feel that they have a ‘purpose’ in life. The big celebration, the wedding or housewarming, takes place not when the debt is discharged, but when it is undertaken. What is emphasized on TV, for example, is not the middle-aged man who has finally paid off his mortgage, but the young man who moves into his new home with his family, proudly waving the papers he has just signed and which will bind him for most of his productive years. After he has paid his debts – the mortgage, the college expenses for his children and his insurance – he is regarded as a problem, a ‘senior citizen’ for whom society must provide not only material comforts but a new ‘purpose’. As in New Guinea, if he is very shrewd, he may become a big creditor instead of a big debtor, but this happens relatively rarely.

因此，新几内亚的年轻人戴着一块旧手表，祈求成功；美国的年轻人戴着一块新手表，祈求成功，他们都觉得自己的人生有了“目标”。盛大的庆祝活动，比如婚礼或乔迁之喜，并非在还清债务之时举行，而是在承担债务之时举行。例如，电视上强调的不是终于还清房贷的中年人，而是带着家人搬进新家，骄傲地挥舞着刚刚签署的文件——这些文件将约束他大部分的劳动年限。还清债务——房贷、子女的大学学费和保险——之后，他被视为一个问题，一个“老年人”，社会不仅要为他提供物质上的舒适，还要为他赋予新的“目标”。就像在新几内亚一样，如果他非常精明，他可能会成为大债主而不是大债主，但这相对来说比较少见。

As this is written, a sow bug crawls across a desk. If he is turned over on his back, one can observe the tremendous struggle he goes through to get on his feet again. During this interval he has a ‘purpose’ in his life. When he succeeds, one can almost see the look of victory on his face. Off he goes, and one can imagine him telling his tale at the next meeting of sow bugs, looked up to by the younger generation as an insect who has made it. And yet mixed with his smugness is a little disappointment. Now that he has come out on top, life seems aimless. Maybe he will return in the hope of repeating his triumph. It might be worth marking his back with ink, so as to recognize him if he risks it. A courageous animal, the sow bug. No wonder he has survived for millions of years.

就在我写下这些文字的时候，一只鼠妇正爬过一张桌子。如果把它翻过来，你会看到它为了重新站起来而经历的艰辛挣扎。在这段时间里，它的生命仿佛有了“目标”。当它成功时，你几乎能看到它脸上洋溢着胜利的喜悦。它就此离去，你可以想象它在下一次鼠妇聚会上讲述自己的故事，被年轻一代视为成功昆虫的榜样。然而，在它的得意之中，却夹杂着一丝失望。如今它已占据上风，生命似乎失去了方向。也许它会再次回来，希望能重现胜利的辉煌。或许应该用墨水在它背上做个标记，以便在它冒险回来时能够认出它。鼠妇，真是勇敢的动物。难怪它能存活数百万年之久。

Most young Americans, however, take their mortgages very seriously only in times of stress. If they are depressed, or the economic situation is bad, their obligations keep them going and may prevent some of them from committing suicide. Most of the time they play a mild game of ‘If It Weren’t for the Debts’, but otherwise enjoy themselves. Only a few make a career out of playing a hard game of ‘Debtor’.

然而，大多数美国年轻人只有在压力巨大时才会认真对待房贷。如果他们情绪低落或经济状况不佳，房贷会成为他们生活的支柱，甚至可能阻止一些人自杀。大多数时候，他们只是玩玩“如果不是因为债务”这种轻松的游戏，其他时候则过得很开心。只有极少数人会把玩“债务人”这种高难度游戏作为职业。

‘Try and Collect’ (TAC) is commonly played by young married couples, and illustrates how a game is set up so that the player ‘wins’ whichever way it goes. The Whites obtain all sorts of goods and services on credit, petty or luxurious, depending on their backgrounds and how they were taught to play by their parents or grandparents. If the creditor gives up after a few soft efforts to collect, then the Whites can enjoy their gains without penalty, and in this sense they win. If the creditor makes more strenuous attempts, then they enjoy the pleasures of the chase as well as the use of their purchases. The hard form of the game occurs if the creditor is determined to collect. In order to get his money he will have to resort to extreme measures. These usually have a coercive element – going to White’s employers or driving up to his house in a noisy, garish truck labelled in big letters COLLECTION AGENCY.

“尝试催收”（Try and Collect，简称TAC）是年轻夫妇常玩的游戏，它巧妙地设计成无论结果如何，玩家都能“获胜”。怀特夫妇（Whites）会赊购各种各样的商品和服务，从小件物品到奢侈品，不一而足，这取决于他们的家庭背景以及父母或祖父母教给他们的游戏方式。如果债权人在几次温和的催收尝试后放弃，怀特夫妇就能毫无顾虑地享受他们的所得，从这个意义上讲，他们赢了。如果债权人更加努力地催收，他们不仅能享受购买物品的乐趣，还能体验追讨的快感。如果债权人决心要收回欠款，游戏就会进入硬核模式。为了拿到钱，他不得不采取极端手段。这些手段通常带有强制性质——比如去怀特夫妇的雇主那里，或者开着一辆醒目、噪音很大的卡车，车身上印着“催收公司”的大字，直接开到他家门口。

At this point there is a switch. White now knows that he will probably have to pay. But because of the coercive element, made clear in most cases by the ‘third letter’ from the collector (‘If you do not appear at our office within 48 hours …’), White feels peremptorily justified in getting angry; he now switches over to a variant of’ Now I’ve Got You, You Son of a Bitch’. In this case he wins by demonstrating that the creditor is greedy, ruthless and untrustworthy. The two most obvious advantages of this are (1) it strengthens White’s existential position, which is a disguised form of ‘All creditors are grasping’, and (2) it offers a large external social gain, since he is now in a position to abuse the creditor openly to his friends without losing his own status as a ‘Good Joe’. He may also exploit further internal social gain by confronting the creditor himself. In addition, it vindicates his taking advantage of the credit system: if that is the way creditors are, as he has now shown, why pay anybody?

此时，情况发生了转变。怀特现在知道自己可能不得不还钱。但由于催债人的“第三封信”（“如果您在48小时内不来我公司……”）中明显带有胁迫性，怀特觉得自己完全有理由生气；他开始用一种类似“现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋”的语气说话。在这种情况下，他通过证明债主贪婪、冷酷无情且不可信赖而获胜。这样做最明显的两个好处是：（1）它强化了怀特的生存状态，这其实是“所有债主都贪得无厌”的另一种伪装；（2）它带来了巨大的外部社会利益，因为他现在可以公开地在朋友面前辱骂债主，而不会失去自己“好人”的形象。他还可以通过亲自与债主对峙来获得进一步的内部社会利益。此外，这也证明了他利用信贷制度的做法是正确的：如果债权人真像他现在所表明的那样，那为什么还要付钱给任何人呢？

‘Creditor’, in the form ‘Try and Get Away With It’ (TAG-AWI), is sometimes played by small landlords. TAC and TAG-AWI players readily recognize each other, and because of the prospective transactional advantages and the promised sport, they are secretly pleased and readily become involved with each other. Regardless of who wins the money, each has improved the other’s position for playing ‘Why Does This Always Happen To Me?’ after it is all over.

“债主”游戏，有时以“侥幸逃脱”（TAG-AWI）的形式出现，由一些小房东玩。TAC和TAG-AWI的玩家彼此很容易认出对方，而且由于潜在的交易优势和游戏的趣味性，他们暗自高兴，并乐于参与其中。无论谁赢钱，游戏结束后，双方都为对方在玩“为什么这种事总是发生在我身上？”（Why Does This Always Happen To Me?）游戏时提供了便利。

Money games can have very serious consequences. If these descriptions sound facetious, as they do to some people, it is not because they relate to trivia but because of the exposure of trivial motivations behind matters people are taught to take seriously.

金钱游戏可能会造成非常严重的后果。如果这些描述听起来像是在开玩笑（有些人确实这么认为），那并非因为它们无关紧要，而是因为它们揭露了人们被教导要认真对待的事情背后那些微不足道的动机。

Antithesis. The obvious antithesis of TAC is to request immediate payment in cash. But a good TAC player has methods for getting around that, which will work on any but the most hard-boiled creditors. The antithesis of TAGAWI is promptness and honesty. Since hard TAC and TAGAWI players are both professionals in every sense of the word, an amateur stands as much chance playing against them as he does playing against professional gamblers. While the amateur seldom wins, he can at least enjoy himself if he becomes involved in one of these games. Since both are by tradition played grimly, nothing is more disconcerting to the professionals than to have an amateur victim laugh at the outcome. In financial circles this is considered strictly Out. In the cases reported to this writer, laughing at a debtor when one encounters him on the street is just as bewildering, frustrating and disconcerting to him as playing anti- ‘Schlemiel’ is to a Schlemiel.

反面。TAC 的明显反面是要求立即现金付款。但高手总有办法绕过这一点，这些方法对付除最顽固的债主之外的所有人都有效。TAGAWI 的反面是及时和诚实。由于 TAC 和 TAGAWI 的高手都是名副其实的专业人士，业余玩家与他们博弈的胜算与职业赌徒相当。虽然业余玩家很少赢，但如果参与其中，至少可以享受其中的乐趣。由于这两种游戏传统上都以严肃的方式进行，没有什么比业余玩家嘲笑游戏结果更让专业人士感到不安的了。在金融界，这种行为被视为绝对禁止。据笔者所了解，在街上遇到债务人时嘲笑他，对债务人来说，就像对一个倒霉蛋进行反“倒霉蛋”游戏一样，会让他感到困惑、沮丧和不安。

3 · KICK ME

3 · 踢我

Thesis. This is played by men whose social manner is equivalent to wearing a sign that reads ‘Please Don’t Kick Me’. The temptation is almost irresistible, and when the natural result follows, White cries piteously, ‘But the sign says “don’t kick me”.’ Then he adds incredulously, ‘Why does this always happen to me?’ (WAHM). Clinically, the WAHM may be introjected and disguised in the ‘Psychiatry’ cliché: ‘Whenever I’m under stress, I get all shook up.’ One game element in WAHM comes from inverse pride: ‘My misfortunes are better than yours.’ This factor is often found in paranoids.

论点：这种行为模式通常由那些社交举止如同举着“请勿踢我”标语的男人扮演。这种诱惑几乎无法抗拒，当自然而然的结果发生时，怀特会可怜兮兮地哭喊：“可是标语上写着‘请勿踢我’呢！”然后他难以置信地补充道：“为什么这种事总是发生在我身上？”（居家办公妈妈）。从临床角度来看，居家办公妈妈的行为可能被内化并伪装成“精神病学”的陈词滥调：“每当我感到压力时，我就会变得焦躁不安。”居家办公妈妈行为模式中的一个游戏元素源于反向的骄傲：“我的不幸比你的好。”这种因素在妄想症患者中很常见。

If the people in his environment are restrained from striking at him by kindheartedness, ‘I’m Only Trying to Help You’, social convention or organizational rules, his behaviour becomes more and more provocative until he transgresses the limits and forces them to oblige. These are men who are cast out, the jilted and the job losers.

如果周围的人出于好心、“我只是想帮你”之类的客套话、社会习俗或组织规则而克制住不去攻击他，他的行为就会越来越具有挑衅性，直到他越过底线，迫使他们屈服。这些人最终会被排斥、被抛弃，丢掉工作。

The corresponding game among women is ‘Threadbare’. Often genteel, they take pains to be shabby. They see to it that their earnings, for ‘good’ reasons, never rise much above the subsistence level. If they have a windfall, there are always enterprising young men who will help them get rid of it, giving them in return shares in a worthless business promotion or something equivalent. Colloquially, such a woman is called ‘Mother’s Friend’, always ready to give judicious Parental advice and living vicariously on the experience of others. Their WAHM is a silent one, and only their demeanour of brave struggle suggests ‘Why does this always happen to me?’

女性之间对应的游戏是“衣衫褴褛”。她们通常举止优雅，却刻意让自己看起来邋遢不堪。她们出于“正当”的理由，确保自己的收入始终维持在勉强糊口的水平。如果她们意外获得一笔横财，总会有一些精明的年轻男子帮她们挥霍掉，作为回报，她们会给她们一些毫无价值的商业推广股份或其他类似的东西。俗话说，这样的女人被称为“妈妈的朋友”，她们总是乐于提供明智的育儿建议，并过着与他人相似的生活。她们的“全职妈妈”角色沉默寡言，只有她们勇敢挣扎的姿态才会流露出“为什么这种事总是发生在我身上？”的疑问。

An interesting form of WAHM occurs in well-adapted people who reap increasing rewards and successes, often beyond their own expectations. Here the WAHM may lead to serious and constructive thinking, and to personal growth in the best sense, if it takes the form ‘What did I really do to deserve this?’

一种有趣的居家办公模式出现在那些适应能力强的人身上，他们获得了越来越多的回报和成功，往往超出了自身的预期。在这种情况下，如果居家办公能促使他们进行严肃而富有建设性的思考，并实现最佳意义上的个人成长，那就是思考“我究竟做了什么才配得上这一切？”

4 · NOW I’VE GOT YOU, YOU SON OF A BITCH

4 · 现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋

Thesis. This can be seen in classic form in poker games. White gets an unbeatable hand, such as four aces. At this point, if he is a NIGYSOB player, he is more interested in the fact that Black is completely at his mercy than he is in good poker or making money.

论点。这在扑克游戏中体现得淋漓尽致。白方拿到一手必胜牌，例如四张A。此时，如果他是个只会耍花招的玩家，他更关心的是黑方完全被他掌控，而不是牌技或赢钱。

White needed some plumbing fixtures installed, and he reviewed the costs very carefully with the plumber before giving him a go-ahead. The price was set, and it was agreed that there would be no extras. When the plumber submitted his bill, he included a few dollars extra for an unexpected valve that had to be installed – about four dollars on a four-hundred-dollar job. White became infuriated, called the plumber on the phone and demanded an explanation. The plumber would not back down. White wrote him a long letter criticizing his integrity and ethics and refused to pay the bill until the extra charge was withdrawn. The plumber finally gave in.

怀特先生需要安装一些水暖设备，在同意施工前，他与水管工仔细核对了价格。双方商定了价格，并约定不会有任何额外费用。然而，水管工提交账单时，却意外地加收了几美元，说是要安装一个阀门——在400美元的工程中，这笔费用大约是4美元。怀特先生勃然大怒，打电话给水管工，要求他解释。水管工拒不让步。怀特先生给他写了一封长信，批评他的诚信和职业道德，并拒绝支付账单，直到他取消这笔额外费用。最终，水管工妥协了。

It soon became obvious that both White and the plumber were playing games. In the course of their negotiations, they had recognized each other’s potentials. The plumber made his provocative move when he submitted his bill. Since White had the plumber’s word, the plumber was clearly in the wrong. White now felt justified in venting almost unlimited rage against him. Instead of merely negotiating in a dignified way that befitted the Adult standards he set for himself, perhaps with a little innocent annoyance, White took the opportunity to make extensive criticisms of the plumber’s whole way of living. On the surface their argument was Adult to Adult, a legitimate business dispute over a stated sum of money. At the psychological level it was Parent to Adult: White was exploiting his trivial but socially defensible objection (position) to vent the pent-up furies of many years on his cozening opponent, just as his mother might have done in a similar situation. He quickly recognized his underlying attitude (NIGYSOB) and realized how secretly delighted he had been at the plumber’s provocation. He then recalled that ever since early childhood he had looked for similar injustices, received them with delight and exploited them with the same vigour. In many of the cases he recounted, he had forgotten the actual provocation, but remembered in great detail the course of the ensuing battle. The plumber, apparently, was playing some variation of ‘Why Does This Always Happen to Me?’ (WAHM).

很快，怀特和水管工都意识到彼此都在玩弄权术。在谈判过程中，他们都看到了对方的潜力。水管工递上账单时，他挑衅的举动达到了顶峰。既然怀特得到了水管工的保证，那么水管工显然是错的。怀特现在觉得自己有理由对他发泄近乎无限的怒火。他没有像自己设定的成年人标准那样，以一种体面的方式进行谈判，或许可以略带一丝无伤大雅的恼怒，而是借此机会对水管工的生活方式进行了广泛的批判。表面上看，他们的争论是成年人之间的，是围绕一笔既定金额的合法商业纠纷。但在心理层面，这却是父母对成年人的较量：怀特利用他那看似微不足道但符合社会规范的反对意见（立场），将多年来积压的怒火发泄在了这位狡猾的对手身上，就像他的母亲在类似情况下可能会做的那样。他很快意识到自己内心深处的态度（NIGYSOB），并意识到自己对水管工的挑衅感到多么暗自得意。他随即回忆起，从孩提时代起，他就一直在寻找类似的冤屈，欣然接受，并以同样的劲头加以利用。在他讲述的许多案例中，他都忘记了最初的挑衅，却对随后的争斗过程记忆犹新。显然，那个水管工当时正沉浸在某种“为什么这种事总是发生在我身上？”的抱怨声中（WAHM）。

NIGYSOB is a two-handed game which must be distinguished from ‘Ain’t It Awful’ (AIA). In AIA the agent seeks injustices in order to complain about them to a third party, making a three-handed game: Aggressor, Victim, Confidant. AIA is played under the slogan ‘Misery Loves Company’. The confidant is usually someone who also plays AIA. WAHM is three-handed, too, but here the agent is trying to establish his pre-eminence in misfortune and resents competition from other unfortunates. NIGYSOB is commercialized in a three-handed professional form as the ‘badger game’. It may also be played as a two-handed marital game in more or less subtle forms.

NIGYSOB 是一种双人游戏，必须与“Ain’t It Awful”（AIA）区分开来。在 AIA 中，参与者会寻找不公，然后向第三方抱怨，从而构成一个三人游戏：施害者、受害者和知己。AIA 的口号是“同病相怜”。知己通常也是 AIA 的参与者。WAHM 也是一种三人游戏，但这里的参与者试图在不幸中确立自己的地位，并对其他不幸者的竞争感到不满。NIGYSOB 以“獾游戏”的形式商业化，成为一种三人参与的专业游戏。它也可以以或多或少隐晦的形式，作为一种夫妻间的双人游戏来玩。

Antithesis. The best antithesis is correct behaviour. The contractual structure of a relationship with a NIGYSOB player should be explicitly stated in detail at the first opportunity, and the rules strictly adhered to. In clinical practice, for example, the question of payment for missed appointments or cancellations must be settled clearly at once, and extra precautions must be taken to avoid mistakes in bookkeeping. If an unforeseen contretemps arises, the antithesis is to yield gracefully without dispute, until such time as the therapist is prepared to deal with the game. In everyday life, business dealings with NIGYSOB players are always calculated risks. The wife of such a person should be treated with polite correctness, and even the mildest flirtations, gallantries or slights should be avoided, especially if the husband himself seems to encourage them.

反面。最好的反面是得体的行为。与“非自愿性行为者”（NIGYSOB）建立关系的契约结构应在第一时间详细明确地阐明，并严格遵守规则。例如，在临床实践中，对于错过预约或取消预约的付款问题必须立即明确解决，并采取额外的预防措施以避免记账错误。如果出现意外冲突，反面是优雅地让步，避免争辩，直到治疗师准备好处理该行为为止。在日常生活中，与“非自愿性行为者”的商业往来始终存在风险。应以礼貌得体的态度对待此类人的妻子，即使是最轻微的调情、殷勤或轻蔑也应避免，尤其是在丈夫本人似乎鼓励这些行为的情况下。

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: Now I’ve got you, you son of a bitch.

论点：现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋。

Aim: Justification.

目的：论证。

Roles: Victim, Aggressor.

角色：受害者、施害者。

Dynamics: Jealous rage.

动态：嫉妒的愤怒。

Examples: (1) I caught you this time. (2) Jealous husband.

例如：（1）这次我抓到你了。（2）嫉妒的丈夫。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult: ‘See, you have done wrong.’

成年人：“你看，你做错了。”

Adult: ‘Now that you draw it to my attention, I guess I have.’

成人：“既然你提醒了我，我想我的确注意到了。”

Psychological Paradigm: Parent-Child.

心理学范式：亲子关系。

Parent: ‘I’ve been watching you, hoping you’d make a slip.’

家长：“我一直在观察你，希望你犯错。”

Child: ‘You caught me this time.’

孩子：“这次你抓到我了。”

Parent: ‘Yes, and I’m going to let you feel the full force of my fury.’

家长：“是的，我会让你感受到我全部的愤怒。”

Moves: (1) Provocation – Accusation. (2) Defence – Accusation. (3) Defence – Punishment.

行动：（1）挑衅——指控。（2）辩护——指控。（3）辩护——惩罚。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – justification for rage. (2) External Psychological – avoids confrontation of own deficiencies. (3) Internal Social – NIGYSOB. (4) External Social – they’re always out to get you. (5) Biological – belligerent exchanges, usually ipsisexual. (6) Existential – people can’t be trusted.

优势：（1）内在心理因素——为愤怒找到理由。（2）外在心理因素——避免面对自身的不足。（3）内在社会因素——NIGYSOB（意为“你就是混蛋”）。（4）外在社会因素——他们总是想害你。（5）生理因素——好斗的交流，通常是同性之间的交流。（6）存在主义因素——人不可信赖。

5 · SEE WHAT YOU MADE ME DO

5 · 看看你都让我做了些什么

Thesis. In its classical form this is a marital game, and in fact is a ‘three-star marriage buster’, but it may also be played between parents and children and in working life.

论点：从其经典形式来看，这是一种婚姻游戏，实际上是一种“三星级婚姻破坏游戏”，但它也可以在父母与子女之间以及工作生活中玩。

(1) First-Degree SWYMD: White, feeling unsociable, becomes engrossed in some activity which tends to insulate him against people. Perhaps all he wants at the moment is to be left alone. An intruder, such as his wife or one of his children, comes either for stroking or to ask him something like, ‘Where can I find the long-nosed pliers?’ This interruption ‘causes’ his chisel, paintbrush, typewriter or soldering iron to slip, whereupon he turns on the intruder in a rage and cries, ‘See what you made me do.’ As this is repeated through the years, his family tends more and more to leave him alone when he is engrossed. Of course it is not the intruder but his own irritation which ‘causes’ the slip, and he is only too happy when it occurs, since it gives him a lever for ejecting the visitor. Unfortunately this is a game which is only too easily learned by young children, so that it is easily passed on from generation to generation. The underlying satisfactions and advantages are more clearly demonstrated when it is played more seductively.

（1）一级SWYMD：怀特感到不愿与人交往，便沉浸于某种能让他与世隔绝的活动之中。或许他此刻只想独处。这时，一个闯入者，比如他的妻子或孩子，前来抚摸他，或者问他一些诸如“尖嘴钳在哪儿？”之类的问题。这种打断“导致”他的凿子、画笔、打字机或电烙铁滑落，于是他勃然大怒，冲着闯入者大喊：“看看你都把我逼成什么样了！”随着这种情况年复一年地重复发生，他的家人在他专注时也越来越倾向于让他一个人待着。当然，真正“导致”他手滑的并非闯入者，而是他自身的恼怒。而当这种情况发生时，他欣喜若狂，因为这给了他一个驱逐访客的契机。不幸的是，这种游戏很容易被幼童学会，因此很容易代代相传。当游戏玩法更具诱惑力时，其潜在的满足感和优势就更加明显地展现出来。

(2) Second-Degree SWYMD: If SWYMD is the basis for a way of life, rather than merely being used occasionally as a protective mechanism, White marries a woman who plays ‘I’m Only Trying to Help You’ or one of its relatives. It is then easy for him to defer decisions to her. Often this may be done in the guise of considerateness or gallantry. He may deferentially and courteously let her decide where to go for dinner or which movie to see. If things turn out well, he can enjoy them. If not, he can blame her by saying or implying: ‘You Got Me Into This’, a simple variation of SWYMD. Or he may throw the burden of decisions regarding the children’s upbringing on her, while he acts as executive officer; if the children get upset, he can play a straight game of SWYMD. This lays the groundwork through the years for blaming mother if the children turn out badly; then SWYMD is not an end in itself, but merely offers passing satisfaction on the way to ‘I Told You So’ or ‘See What You’ve Done Now’.

（2）二级“我只是想帮你”：如果“我只是想帮你”成为一种生活方式的基础，而不仅仅是偶尔作为一种保护机制，那么怀特娶的妻子就会扮演“我只是想帮你”或其类似角色。这样，他就能轻易地把决定权推给她。这种推卸往往伪装成体贴或绅士风度。他可能会恭敬有礼地让她决定去哪里吃饭或看哪部电影。如果一切顺利，他就能享受其中。如果不顺利，他可以通过说或暗示“都是你害的”来责怪她，这其实是“我只是想帮你”的简单变体。或者，他可能会把孩子抚养的重担推给她，而自己则扮演执行者的角色；如果孩子们不高兴，他就可以直接玩“我只是想帮你”的游戏。这为日后如果孩子出了问题就责怪母亲埋下了伏笔。那么，SWYMD 本身并不是目的，而只是在通往“我早就告诉过你”或“看看你现在做了什么”的路上提供短暂的满足感。

The professional player who pays his psychological way with SWYMD will use it also in his work. In occupational SWYMD the long-suffering look of resentment replaces words. The player ‘democratically’ or as part of ‘good management’ asks his assistants for suggestions. In this way he may attain an unassailable position for terrorizing his juniors. Any mistake he makes can be used against them by blaming them for it. Used against seniors (blaming them for one’s mistakes), it becomes self-destructive and may lead to termination of employment or, in the army, to transfer to another unit. In that case it is a component of ‘Why Does This Always Happen To Me?’ with resentful people, or of ‘There I Go Again’ with depressives – (both of the’ Kick Me’ family).

职业球员如果用“为什么总是这样？”这种心理战术来应对压力，也会将其运用到工作中。在职场中，怨恨的眼神取代了言语。球员会“民主地”或以“良好管理”的名义向助手征求建议。这样一来，他就能获得一个牢不可破的地位，从而恐吓下属。他犯的任何错误都可以反过来指责他们。如果这种做法被用来指责上级（将自己的错误归咎于他们），则会适得其反，甚至可能导致被解雇，或者在军队中被调往其他单位。在这种情况下，它就成了怨恨者的“为什么这种事总是发生在我身上？”的组成部分，或是抑郁症患者的“我又来了”的组成部分——（两者都属于“踢我”的范畴）。

(3) Third-Degree SWYMD: in a hard form SWYMD may be played by paranoids against people incautious enough to give them advice (see ‘I’m Only Trying to Help You’). There it may be dangerous, and in rare cases even fatal.

（3）三级SWYMD：在极端情况下，偏执狂可能会对那些不够谨慎、给他们建议的人使用SWYMD（参见“我只是想帮你”）。这种做法可能很危险，在极少数情况下甚至会致命。

‘See What You Made Me Do.’ (SWYMD) and ‘You Got Me into This’ (UGMIT) complement each other nicely, so that the SWYMD-UGMIT combination is a classical basis for the cover game contract in many marriages. This contract is illustrated by the following sequence.

“看看你都做了些什么”（SWYMD）和“你把我卷进来了”（UGMIT）相得益彰，因此SWYMD-UGMIT组合成为许多婚姻中“掩护游戏”契约的经典基础。以下序列说明了这种契约。

By mutual agreement Mrs White did the family bookkeeping and paid the bills out of the joint checking account because Mr White was ‘poor at figures’. Every few months they would be notified of an overdraft, and Mr White would have to square it with the bank. When they looked for the source of the difficulty, it would turn out that Mrs White had made an expensive purchase without telling her husband. When this came to light, Mr White would furiously play his UGMIT, and she would tearfully accept his rebuke and promise it would not happen again. Everything would go smoothly for a while, and then a creditor’s agent would suddenly appear to demand payment for a long-overdue bill. Mr White, not having heard of this bill, would question his wife about it. She would then play her SWYMD, saying that it was his fault. Since he had forbidden her to overdraw their account, the only way she could make ends meet was by leaving this large obligation unpaid and hiding the duns from him.

经双方同意，怀特太太负责家里的账目，并用联名支票账户支付账单，因为怀特先生“不擅长算数”。每隔几个月，他们就会收到透支通知，怀特先生不得不去银行结清欠款。当他们查找透支的原因时，发现原来是怀特太太瞒着丈夫买了一笔大件商品。事情败露后，怀特先生会勃然大怒，而她则会含泪接受他的责备，并保证不会再犯。一切似乎都风平浪静了一段时间，然后债权人的代理人突然出现，催缴一笔早已逾期的账单。怀特先生对此毫不知情，便质问妻子。这时，她又会故技重施，说都是他的错。因为他禁止她透支账户，所以她唯一能维持生计的办法就是故意拖欠这笔巨款，并瞒着他收到催款通知。

These games had been allowed to go on for ten years, on the basis that each occurrence would be the last, and that from then on it would be different – which it was, for a few months. In therapy Mr White very cleverly analysed this game without any assistance from the therapist, and also devised an effective remedy. By mutual agreement he and Mrs White put all charge accounts and their bank account in his name. Mrs White continued to do the bookkeeping and make out the checks, but Mr White saw the bills first and controlled the outgoing payments. In this way neither duns nor overdrafts could get by him, and they now shared the budgetary labour. Deprived of the satisfactions and advantages of SWYMD-UGMIT, the Whites were at first at a loss, and were then driven to find more open and constructive types of gratification from each other.

这些游戏持续了十年之久，每次都以“这是最后一次”为前提，并约定以后都会有所不同——而事实也的确如此，只是最初几个月如此。在治疗过程中，怀特先生非常巧妙地分析了这种游戏，无需治疗师的任何帮助，并制定了一个有效的补救措施。他和怀特太太达成一致，将所有赊账账户和银行账户都转到了他的名下。怀特太太继续负责记账和开支票，但怀特先生会先查看账单并控制支出。这样一来，催款和透支都逃不过他的眼睛，他们也共同承担了预算管理的工作。失去了“SWYMD-UGMIT”游戏带来的满足感和好处后，怀特夫妇起初感到迷茫，随后开始寻求彼此之间更加开放和建设性的满足方式。

Antithesis. The antithesis to First-Degree SWYMD is to leave the player alone, and to Second-Degree SWYMD to throw the decision back on White. The First-Degree player may react by feeling forlorn, but seldom angry; the Second-Degree player may become sulky if he is forced to take the initiative, so that systematic anti-SWYMD leads to disagreeable consequences. The antithesis to Third-Degree SWYMD should be put into competent professional hands.

反面。一级“你觉得我赢了”策略的反面是不要干预棋手，二级“你觉得我赢了”策略的反面是把决定权交还给白方。一级棋手可能会感到沮丧，但很少会生气；二级棋手如果被迫主动出击，可能会变得闷闷不乐，因此系统性的反“你觉得我赢了”策略会导致令人不快的后果。三级“你觉得我赢了”策略的反面应该交给合格的专业人士来处理。

PARTIAL ANALYSIS

部分分析

The aim of this game is vindication. Dynamically the mild form may be related to premature ejaculation, the hard form to rage based on ‘castration’ anxiety. It is easily acquired by children. The external psychological gain (avoidance of responsibility) is prominent, and the game is often precipitated by the threat of impending intimacy, since the ‘justifiable’ anger offers a good excuse for avoiding sexual relations. The existential position is, ‘I am blameless’.

这种游戏的目的是为了寻求补偿。从动态角度来看，轻度形式可能与早泄有关，重度形式则与基于“阉割”焦虑的愤怒有关。儿童很容易习得这种游戏。其外在的心理获益（逃避责任）十分显著，而且这种游戏往往是由即将到来的亲密关系的威胁引发的，因为这种“正当”的愤怒为逃避性关系提供了一个很好的借口。其存在主义立场是：“我无罪。”

笔记

Starrels, Dr Robert Goulding and others with a special interest in this problem, for their continued efforts in the study of ‘Alcoholic’ as a game, and for their contribution to and criticism of the present discussion.

在此，我们要感谢加州奥克兰酒精中毒治疗与教育中心的 Rodney Nurse 博士和 Frances Matson 女士，以及 Kenneth Everts 博士、R. J. Starrels 博士、Robert Goulding 博士和其他对这个问题特别感兴趣的人士，感谢他们持续努力研究“酗酒者”这款游戏，并感谢他们对本次讨论的贡献和批评。

#↩

7 · Marital Games

7. 婚姻游戏

A LMOST any game can form the scaffolding for married life and family living, but some, such as ‘If It Weren’t for You’, flourish better or, like ‘Frigid Woman’, are tolerated longer, under the legal force of contractual intimacy. Marital games, of course, can only be arbitrarily separated from sexual games, which are treated in a separate section. Those games which characteristically evolve into their most full-blown forms in the marital relationship include ‘Corner’, ‘Courtroom’, ‘Frigid Woman’ and ‘Frigid Man’, ‘Harried’, ‘If It Weren’t for You’, ‘Look How Hard I’ve Tried’ and ‘Sweetheart’.

几乎任何游戏都能为婚姻生活和家庭生活搭建框架，但有些游戏，例如“若非有你”，在婚姻关系中发展得更好；或者像“冷淡的女人”，在法律约束下，更容易被容忍。当然，婚姻游戏只能人为地与性游戏区分开来，性游戏将在单独的章节中讨论。那些在婚姻关系中发展到最成熟阶段的游戏包括“角落”、“法庭”、“冷淡的女人”、“冷淡的男人”、“疲惫不堪”、“若非有你”、“看看我有多努力”和“亲爱的”。

1 · CORNER

1 · 角落

Thesis. Corner illustrates more clearly than most games their manipulative aspect and their function as barriers to intimacy. Paradoxically, it consists of a disingenuous refusal to play the game of another.

论点：角落游戏比大多数游戏更清晰地展现了其操控性以及作为亲密关系障碍的功能。矛盾的是，它本身就是一种虚伪地拒绝参与他人游戏的行为。

1. Mrs White suggests to her husband that they go to a movie. Mr White agrees.

1. 怀特太太建议她丈夫去看电影。怀特先生同意了。

2a. Mrs White makes an ‘unconscious’ slip. She mentions quite naturally in the course of conversation that the house needs painting. This is an expensive project, and White has recently told her that their finances are strained; he requested her not to embarrass or annoy him by suggesting unusual expenditures, at least until the beginning of the new month. This is therefore an ill-chosen moment to bring up the condition of the house, and White responds rudely.

2a. 怀特太太无意间说漏了嘴。在谈话中，她很自然地提到房子需要粉刷。这是一项昂贵的工程，而怀特先生最近告诉她，他们的经济状况很紧张；他请求她不要提出任何不寻常的开支，以免让他难堪或恼火，至少在新月份开始之前不要这样做。因此，此时提起房子的状况实在不合时宜，怀特先生的反应也很粗鲁。

2b. Alternatively: White steers the conversation around to the house, making it difficult for Mrs White to resist the temptation to say that it needs painting. As in the previous case, White responds rudely.

2b. 另一种情况是：怀特先生将话题引向房子，使怀特太太难以抑制说出房子需要粉刷的冲动。与前一种情况一样，怀特先生的回应十分粗鲁。

3. Mrs White takes offence and says that if he is in one of his bad moods, she will not go to the movie with him, and he had best go by himself. He says if that is the way she feels about it, he will go alone.

3. 怀特太太很生气，说如果他心情不好，她就不会陪他去看电影，他最好自己去。他说既然她这么想，那他就自己去。

4. White goes to the movie (or out with the boys), leaving Mrs White at home to nurse her injured feelings.

4. 白先生去看电影（或者和朋友们出去玩），留下白太太独自在家疗伤。

There are two possible gimmicks in this game:

这个游戏中可能存在两种噱头：

A. Mrs White knows very well from past experience that she is not supposed to take his annoyance seriously. What he really wants is for her to show some appreciation of how hard he works to earn their living; then they could go off happily together. But she refuses to play, and he feels badly let down. He leaves filled with disappointment and resentment, while she stays at home looking abused, but with a secret feeling of triumph.

A. 怀特太太从过去的经验中很清楚，她不应该把他的恼怒当回事。他真正想要的，是她能对他辛勤工作养家糊口表示一些感激；那样他们就能幸福地一起离开了。但她拒绝配合，他感到非常失望。他满怀失望和怨恨地离开了，而她则留在家里，看起来饱受委屈，但内心却暗自得意。

B. White knows very well from past experience that he is not supposed to take her pique seriously. What she really wants is to be honeyed out of it; then they would go off happily together. But he refuses to play, knowing that his refusal is dishonest: he knows she wants to be coaxed, but pretends he doesn’t. He leaves the house, feeling cheerful and relieved, but looking wronged. She is left feeling disappointed and resentful.

白先生从过去的经验中很清楚，他不该把她的小脾气当回事。她真正想要的只是被哄着消气，然后他们就能幸福地一起离开了。但他拒绝配合，因为他知道自己的拒绝并不真诚：他知道她想被哄，却假装不知道。他离开家时，感觉既高兴又如释重负，但脸上却带着委屈的神情。她则感到失望和怨恨。

In each of these cases the winner’s position is, from a naïve standpoint, irreproachable; all he or she has done is take the other literally. This is clearer in (B), where White takes Mrs White’s refusal to go at face value. They both know that this is cheating, but since she said it, she is cornered.

在这些例子中，从单纯的角度来看，获胜者的立场似乎无可指摘；他或她所做的只是字面理解了对方的话。这一点在(B)中体现得更为明显，怀特完全相信了怀特太太拒绝离开的说法。他们两人都知道这是作弊，但既然她说了出来，她就陷入了困境。

The most obvious gain here is the external psychological. Both of them find movies sexually stimulating, and it is more or less anticipated that after they return from the theatre, they will make love. Hence whichever one of them wants to avoid intimacy sets up the game in move (2a) or (2b). This is a particularly exasperating variety of ‘Uproar’ (see Chapter 9 ). The ‘wronged’ party can, of course, make a good case for not wanting to make love in a state of justifiable indignation, and the cornered spouse has no recourse.

这里最明显的获益在于外部心理层面。两人都觉得电影具有性刺激作用，而且几乎可以肯定的是，看完电影回家后他们会做爱。因此，无论哪一方想要避免亲密行为，都会在（2a）或（2b）步骤中发起博弈。这是一种特别令人恼火的“骚动”策略（参见第九章）。当然，“受委屈”的一方可以理直气壮地提出不想做爱的理由，而处于被动地位的配偶则束手无策。

Antithesis. This is simple for Mrs White. All she has to do is change her mind, take her husband by the arm, smile and go along with him (a shift from Child to Adult ego state). It is more difficult for Mr White, since she now has the initiative; but if he reviews the whole situation, he may be able to coax her into going along with him, either as a sulky Child who has been placated or, better, as an Adult.

对比。这对怀特太太来说很简单。她只需要改变主意，挽起丈夫的胳膊，微笑着顺从他（从孩童自我状态转变为成人自我状态）。这对怀特先生来说就比较困难了，因为现在她掌握了主动权；但如果他仔细审视整个情况，或许可以劝说她顺从，让她像个被安抚的闹别扭的孩子一样，或者更好的是，像个成熟的成年人一样。

‘Corner’ is found in a somewhat different form as a family game involving the children, where it resembles the ‘double-bind’ described by Bateson and his associates. 1 Here the child is cornered, so that whatever he does is wrong. According to the Bateson school this may be an important etiological factor in schizophrenia. In the present language, then, schizophrenia may be a child’s antithesis to ‘Corner’. Experience in treating adult schizophrenics with game analysis bears this out – that is, if the family game of ‘Corner’ is analysed to demonstrate that the schizophrenic behaviour was and is specifically undertaken to counter this game, partial or total remission occurs in a properly prepared patient.

“角落”游戏在儿童参与的家庭游戏中以略有不同的形式出现，它类似于贝特森及其同事描述的“双重束缚”。在这种游戏中，孩子被逼到角落，无论做什么都是错的。根据贝特森学派的观点，这可能是精神分裂症的一个重要病因。因此，用现在的语言来说，精神分裂症可能是儿童版的“角落”游戏的反面。运用游戏分析法治疗成年精神分裂症患者的经验证实了这一点——也就是说，如果分析“角落”游戏，证明精神分裂症患者的行为过去和现在都是为了对抗这个游戏而专门采取的，那么经过适当准备的患者就能获得部分或完全的缓解。

An everyday form of ‘Corner’ which is played by the whole family and is most likely to affect the character development of the younger children occurs with meddlesome ‘Parental’ parents. The little boy or girl is urged to be more helpful around the house, but when he is, the parents find fault with what he does – a homely example of ‘damned if you do and damned if you don’t’. This ‘double-bind’ may be called the Dilemma Type of ‘Corner’.

一种常见的“困境”形式，通常发生在全家参与、且极易影响年幼孩子性格发展的父母身上。这种困境往往发生在爱管闲事的父母身上。父母会敦促小男孩或小女孩多做些家务，但当他们真的去做时，父母却又会挑剔他们的行为——这正是典型的“进退两难”的家庭困境。这种“两难”困境可以被称为“困境”中的“两难型”。

‘Corner’ is sometimes found as an etiological factor in asthmatic children.

“角”有时被认为是儿童哮喘的病因之一。

Little girl: ‘Mummy, do you love me?’

小女孩：“妈妈，你爱我吗？”

Mother: ‘What is love?’

母亲：“什么是爱？”

This answer leaves the child with no direct recourse. She wants to talk about mother, and mother switches the subject to philosophy, which the little girl is not equipped to handle. She begins to breathe hard, mother is irritated, asthma sets in, mother apologizes and the ‘Asthma Game’ now runs its course. This ‘Asthma’ type of ‘Corner’ remains to be studied further.

这个回答让孩子无处可去。她想谈谈妈妈，妈妈却把话题转到了哲学上，而小女孩根本无法理解哲学。她开始喘粗气，妈妈感到烦躁，哮喘发作，妈妈道歉，这场“哮喘游戏”就此结束。这种“哮喘式”的“角落”还有待进一步研究。

An elegant variant, which may be called the ‘Russell-Whitehead Type’ of ‘Corner’, sometimes occurs in therapy groups.

治疗小组中有时会出现一种优雅的变体，可以称之为“罗素-怀特海德型”的“角落”。

Black: ‘Well, anyway, when we’re silent nobody is playing games.’

布莱克：“好吧，反正当我们保持沉默的时候，就没人玩游戏了。”

White: ‘Silence itself may be a game.’

怀特：“沉默本身可能也是一种游戏。”

Red: ‘Nobody was playing games today.’

红：“今天没人玩游戏。”

White: ‘But not playing games may itself be a game.’

怀特：“但是不玩游戏本身可能也是一种游戏。”

The therapeutic antithesis is equally elegant. Logical paradoxes are forbidden. When White is deprived of this manoeuvre, his underlying anxieties come quickly to the fore.

这种治疗上的反面同样精妙。逻辑悖论是被禁止的。当怀特失去这种策略时，他内心深处的焦虑就会迅速浮出水面。

Closely allied to ‘Corner’ on the one hand, and to ‘Threadbare’ on the other, is the marital game of ‘Lunch Bag’. The husband, who can well afford to have lunch at a good restaurant, nevertheless makes himself a few sandwiches every morning, which he takes to the office in a paper bag. In this way he uses up crusts of bread, leftovers from dinner and paper bags which his wife saves for him. This gives him complete control over the family finances, for what wife would dare buy herself a mink stole in the face of such self-sacrifice? The husband reaps numerous other advantages, such as the privilege of eating lunch by himself and of catching up on his work during lunch hour. In many ways this is a constructive game which Benjamin Franklin would have approved of, since it encourages the virtues of thrift, hard work and punctuality.

与“角落”游戏和“破烂”游戏密切相关的，是夫妻间的“午餐袋”游戏。丈夫明明完全有能力去高档餐厅享用午餐，却每天早上都给自己做几个三明治，用纸袋装着带到办公室。这样一来，他就能用掉面包皮、晚餐剩菜和妻子为他攒下的纸袋。这让他完全掌控了家庭财务，毕竟，面对如此巨大的自我牺牲，哪个妻子还敢给自己买貂皮披肩呢？丈夫还能获得其他诸多好处，比如可以独自享用午餐，以及利用午休时间处理工作。从很多方面来看，这都是一个有益的游戏，本杰明·富兰克林也会赞同，因为它鼓励节俭、勤奋和守时等美德。

2 · COURTROOM

2 · 法庭

Thesis. Descriptively this belongs to the class of games which find their most florid expressions in law, and which includes ‘Wooden Leg’ (the plea of insanity) and ‘Debtor’ (the civil suit). Clinically it is most often seen in marital counselling and marital psychotherapy groups. Indeed, some marital counselling and marital groups consist of a perpetual game of ‘Courtroom’ in which nothing is resolved, since the game is never broken up. In such cases it becomes evident that the counsellor or therapist is heavily involved in the game without being aware of it.

论文指出，这种游戏属于法律领域中最为常见的一类，例如“木腿”（精神错乱辩护）和“债务人”（民事诉讼）。临床上，这种游戏最常见于婚姻咨询和婚姻心理治疗小组。事实上，一些婚姻咨询和小组活动实际上就是一场永无休止的“法庭游戏”，由于游戏从未停止，任何问题都无法得到解决。在这种情况下，咨询师或治疗师显然在不知不觉中也深度参与了这场游戏。

‘Courtroom’ can be played by any number, but is essentially three-handed, with a plaintiff, a defendant and a judge, represented by a husband, a wife and the therapist. If it is played in a therapy group or over the radio or TV, the other members of the audience are cast as the jury. The husband begins plaintively, ‘Let me tell you what (wife’s name) did yesterday. She took the …’ etc., etc. The wife then responds defensively, ‘Here is the way it really was … and besides just before that he was … and anyway at the time we were both …’ etc. The husband adds gallantly, ‘Well, I’m glad you people have a chance to hear both sides of the story, I only want to be fair.’ At this point the counsellor says judiciously, ‘It seems to me that if we consider …’ etc., etc. If there is an audience, the therapist may throw it to them with: ‘Well, let’s hear what the others have to say.’ Or, if the group is already trained, they will play the jury without any instruction from him.

《法庭》这个角色扮演游戏可以由任意人数进行，但本质上是三人角色扮演，包括原告、被告和法官，分别由丈夫、妻子和治疗师扮演。如果是在治疗小组中，或者通过广播或电视播放，其他观众则扮演陪审团成员。丈夫以哀怨的语气开始：“让我告诉你（妻子的名字）昨天做了什么。”她拿走了……等等。妻子随即辩解道：“事情的真相是这样的……而且就在那之前他……总之，当时我们俩……”等等。丈夫则略带绅士气地补充道：“好吧，我很高兴你们有机会听到双方的说法，我只是想公平起见。”此时，咨询师会谨慎地说道：“在我看来，如果我们考虑……”等等。如果有旁听者，咨询师可能会把话题抛给他们：“好，让我们听听其他人怎么说。”或者，如果小组成员已经接受过相关培训，他们无需咨询师的任何指示就能扮演陪审团的角色。

Antithesis. The therapist says to the husband, ‘You’re absolutely right!’ If the husband relaxes complacently or triumphantly, the therapist asks: ‘How do you feel about my saying that?’ The husband replies: ‘Fine.’ Then the therapist says, ‘Actually, I feel you’re in the wrong.’ If the husband is honest, he will say: ‘I knew that all along.’ If he is not honest, he will show some reaction that makes it clear a game is in progress. Then it becomes possible to go into the matter further. The game element lies in the fact that while the plaintiff is overtly clamouring for victory, fundamentally he believes that he is wrong.

反面。治疗师对丈夫说：“你说得完全正确！”如果丈夫放松下来，显得沾沾自喜或沾沾自喜，治疗师会问：“你觉得我这么说怎么样？”丈夫回答：“没事。”然后治疗师会说：“其实，我觉得你错了。”如果丈夫诚实，他会说：“我一直都知道。”如果他不诚实，他会表现出一些反应，表明他正在进行一场游戏。这时，就可以进一步探讨这个问题了。游戏的要素在于，虽然原告表面上渴望胜利，但从根本上来说，他认为自己错了。

After sufficient clinical material has been gathered to clarify the situation, the game can be interdicted by a manoeuvre which is one of the most elegant in the whole art of antithetics. The therapist makes a rule prohibiting the use of the (grammatical) third person in the group. Thenceforward the members can only address each other directly as ‘you’ or talk about themselves as ‘I’, but they cannot say, ‘Let me tell you about him ‘or’ Let me tell you about her’. At this point the couple stop playing games in the group altogether, or shift into ‘Sweetheart’ which is some improvement or take up ‘Furthermore’ which is no help at all. ‘Sweetheart’ is described in another section ( page 94 ). In ‘Furthermore’ the plaintiff makes one accusation after the other. The defendant replies to each ‘I can explain’. The plaintiff pays no attention to the explanation, but as soon as the defendant pauses, he launches into his next indictment with another ‘furthermore’, which is followed by another explanation – a typical Parent-Child interchange.

在收集到足够的临床资料以澄清情况后，可以通过一种堪称对立修辞艺术中最精妙的策略来制止这种游戏。治疗师制定一条规则，禁止在小组中使用（语法上的）第三人称。此后，成员之间只能直接称呼为“你”，或用“我”来谈论自己，而不能说“让我告诉你关于他的事”或“让我告诉你关于她的事”。此时，这对伴侣要么完全停止在小组中玩游戏，要么转而使用“亲爱的”游戏（这算是一种进步），要么使用“此外”游戏（这毫无帮助）。“亲爱的”游戏将在另一章节（第94页）中进行描述。在“此外”游戏中，原告会接连提出指控，而被告则对每一项指控都回应“我可以解释”。原告对被告的解释置之不理，但被告一停顿，就立刻以另一个“此外”开始他的下一项指控，随后又进行了另一次解释——典型的父母与子女之间的对话。

‘Furthermore’ is played most intensively by paranoid defendants. Because of their literalness, it is particularly easy for them to frustrate accusers who express themselves in humorous or metaphorical terms. In general, metaphors are the most obvious traps to avoid in a game of ‘Furthermore’.

“此外”这个游戏最常被疑神疑鬼的被告人玩。由于其字面意思，他们很容易让那些用幽默或比喻表达的原告感到恼火。总的来说，在“此外”游戏中，比喻是最容易落入的陷阱。

In its everyday form, ‘Courtroom’ is easily observed in children as a three-handed game between two siblings and a parent. ‘Mummy, she took my candy away.’ ‘Yes, but he took my doll, and before that he was hitting me, and anyway we both promised to share our candy.’

在日常生活中，“法庭游戏”很容易在孩子们身上看到，通常是两个兄弟姐妹和一位家长三人玩的游戏。“妈妈，她把我的糖拿走了。”“是啊，但他拿走了我的娃娃，而且在那之前他还打我，反正我们都答应过要分享糖果的。”

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: They’ve got to say I’m right.

论点：他们不得不承认我是对的。

Aim: Reassurance.

目的：安抚人心。

Roles: Plaintiff, Defendant, Judge (and/or Jury).

角色：原告、被告、法官（和/或陪审团）。

Dynamics: Sibling rivalry.

动态：兄弟姐妹之间的竞争。

Examples: (1) Children quarrelling, parent intervenes. (2) Married couple, seek ‘help’.

例如：（1）孩子吵架，家长介入。（2）夫妻寻求“帮助”。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult: ‘This is what she did to me.’

成人：“她这样对我。”

Adult: ‘The real facts are these.’

成年人：“事实真相是这样的。”

Psychological Paradigm: Child-Parent.

心理范式：儿童-父母。

Child: ‘Tell me I’m right.’

孩子：“告诉我我是对的。”

Parent: ‘This one is right.’ Or: ‘You’re both right.’

家长：“这个是对的。”或者：“你们两个都对。”

Moves: (1) Complaint filed – Defence filed. (2) Plaintiff files rebuttal, concession, or good-will gesture. (3) Decision of judge or instructions to jury. (4) Final decision filed.

诉讼流程：（1）原告提起诉讼——被告提交答辩状。（2）原告提交反驳意见、让步声明或善意姿态声明。（3）法官作出裁决或向陪审团作出指示。（4）作出最终裁决。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – projection of guilt. (2) External Psychological – excused from guilt. (3) Internal Social – ‘Sweetheart’, ‘Furthermore’, ‘Uproar’ and others. (4) External Social – ‘Courtroom’. (5) Biological – stroking from judge and jury. (6) Existential – depressive position, I’m always wrong.

优势：（1）内部心理因素——投射内疚感。（2）外部心理因素——免除内疚感。（3）内部社会因素——“亲爱的”、“此外”、“骚动”等。（4）外部社会因素——“法庭”。（5）生理因素——获得法官和陪审团的安慰。（6）存在主义因素——陷入抑郁，觉得自己总是错的。

3 · FRIGID WOMAN

3 · 冷漠的女人

Thesis . This is almost always a marital game, since it is hardly conceivable that an informal liaison would present the required opportunities and privileges over a sufficient length of time, or that such a liaison would be maintained in the face of it.

论点：这几乎总是婚姻游戏，因为很难想象一段非正式的婚外情能在足够长的时间内提供所需的机会和特权，或者在面临这些情况时还能维持这种关系。

The husband makes advances to his wife and is repulsed. After repeated attempts, he is told that all men are beasts, he doesn’t really love her, or doesn’t love her for herself, that all he is intersted in is sex. He desists for a time, then tries again with the same result. Eventually he resigns himself and makes no further advances. As the weeks or months pass, the wife becomes increasingly informal and sometimes forgetful. She walks through the bedroom half dressed or forgets her clean towel when she takes a bath so that he has to bring it to her. If she plays a hard game or drinks heavily, she may become flirtatious with other men at parties. At length he responds to those provocations and tries again. Once more he is repulsed, and a game of ‘Uproar’ ensues involving their recent behaviour, other couples, their in-laws, their finances and their failures, terminated by a slamming door.

丈夫对妻子示好，却遭到妻子的拒绝。屡次尝试后，妻子指责他都是禽兽，说他根本不爱她，或者说他爱的不是她这个人，只是对她感兴趣。他暂时作罢，但之后又故技重施，结果依然相同。最终，他无奈地放弃了，不再主动示好。几周或几个月过去了，妻子变得越来越随意，有时甚至健忘。她会衣衫不整地走进卧室，或者洗澡时忘记带干净的毛巾，让丈夫不得不给她拿。如果她玩游戏或喝得酩酊大醉，可能会在聚会上与其他男人调情。最终，丈夫对这些挑衅做出了回应，再次尝试。然而，他再次感到厌恶，于是两人开始玩“吵架游戏”，游戏中充斥着他们最近的行为、其他夫妻、他们的姻亲、他们的财务状况以及他们的失败，最终以摔门而告终。

This time the husband makes up his mind that he is really through, that they will find a sexless modus vivendi. Months pass. He declines the negligee parade and the forgotten towel manoeuvre. The wife becomes more provocatively informal and more provocatively forgetful, but he still resists. Then one evening she actually approaches him and kisses him. At first he doesn’t respond, remembering his resolution, but soon nature begins to take its course after the long famine, and now he thinks he surely has it made. His first tentative advances are not repulsed. He becomes bolder and bolder. Just at the critical point, the wife steps back and cries: ‘See, what did I tell you! All men are beasts, all I wanted was affection, but all you are interested in is sex!’ The ensuing game of ‘Uproar’ at this point may skip the preliminary phases of their recent behaviour and their in-laws, and go right to the financial problem.

这一次，丈夫下定决心要彻底结束这段关系，他们要找到一种无性的生活模式。几个月过去了。他拒绝了妻子穿着睡衣的挑逗和用毛巾遮掩身体的举动。妻子变得更加随意，也更加健忘，但他仍然抗拒。然后有一天晚上，她主动接近他，吻了他。起初他没有回应，因为他记得自己之前的决心，但经过漫长的禁欲期，他的本能开始发挥作用，他觉得自己终于成功了。他最初的试探性举动并没有被拒绝。他变得越来越大胆。就在关键时刻，妻子后退一步，哭喊道：“看吧，我早就告诉过你！男人都是禽兽，我想要的只是爱，而你却只对性感兴趣！”接下来的“争吵”游戏可能会跳过他们最近的行为和双方父母的铺垫，直接进入经济问题。

It should be noted that in spite of his protestations, the husband is usually just as afraid of sexual intimacy as his wife is, and had carefully chosen his mate to minimize the danger of overtaxing his disturbed potency, which he can now blame on her.

值得注意的是，尽管丈夫百般辩解，但他通常和妻子一样害怕性亲密，并且会精心挑选伴侣，以尽量减少过度消耗他紊乱的性能力的风险，而现在他可以把这一切归咎于妻子。

In its everyday form this game is played by unmarried ladies of various ages, which soon earns them a common slang epithet. With them it often merges into the game of indignation, or ‘Rapo’.

这种游戏在日常生活中主要由各个年龄段的未婚女性玩，很快她们就因此得了个俚语绰号。在她们中间，这种游戏常常会演变成一种表达愤慨的游戏，或者叫“Rapo”。

Antithesis. This is a dangerous game, and the possible antitheses are equally dangerous. Taking a mistress is a gamble. In the face of such stimulating competition, the wife may give up the game and try to initiate a normal married life, perhaps too late, On the other hand, she may use the affair, often with the help of a lawyer, as ammunition against the husband in a game of ‘Now I’ve Got You, You Son of a Bitch’. The outcome is equally unpredictable if the husband undertakes psychotherapy and she does not. The wife’s game may collapse as the husband grows stronger, leading to healthier adjustment; but if she is a hard player, improvement on his part may result in divorce. The best solution, if available, is for both parties to go into a transactional marital group, where the underlying advantages of the game and the basic sexual pathology can be laid bare. With this preparation both spouses may become interested in intensive individual psychotherapy. That may result in a psychological remarriage. If not, at least each of the parties may make a more sensible readjustment to the situation than they might have otherwise.

对立面。这是一场危险的游戏，而可能的对立面同样危险。婚外情是一场赌博。面对如此刺激的竞争，妻子可能会放弃游戏，试图开始正常的婚姻生活，但或许为时已晚。另一方面，她可能会利用这段婚外情，通常在律师的帮助下，作为攻击丈夫的武器，玩一场“现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋”的游戏。如果丈夫接受心理治疗而妻子没有，结果同样难以预料。随着丈夫的成长，妻子的游戏可能会崩溃，从而带来更健康的调整；但如果她玩得很凶，丈夫的进步反而可能导致离婚。如果条件允许，最好的解决办法是双方参加婚姻咨询小组，在那里，这种游戏的潜在优势和基本的性病态可以被揭露出来。有了这样的准备，夫妻双方都可能对深入的个人心理治疗产生兴趣。这或许会带来心理上的“再婚”。否则，至少各方可能会对现状做出比原本可能做出的更明智的调整。

The decent antithesis for the everyday form is to find another social companion. Some of the shrewder or more brutal antitheses are corrupt and even criminal.

日常生活中体面的反面是寻找另一个社交伴侣。而一些更狡猾或更残酷的反面则是腐败甚至犯罪。

Relatives. The converse game, ‘Frigid Man’, is less common, but it takes much the same general course with some variations in detail. The final outcome depends upon the scripts of the parties involved.

亲戚们。与之相反的游戏“冷漠男”不太常见，但大致流程相同，只是细节上略有不同。最终结果取决于参与者的剧本。

The crucial point of ‘Frigid Woman’ is the terminal phase of ‘Uproar’. Once this has run its course, sexual intimacy is out of the question, since both parties derive a perverse satisfaction from ‘Uproar’ and have no need of further sexual excitement from each other. Hence the most important item in anti- ‘Frigid Woman’ is to decline ‘Uproar’. This leaves the wife in a state of sexual disatisfaction which may be so acute that she will become more compliant. The use made of ‘Uproar’ distinguishes ‘Frigid Woman’ from ‘Beat Me Daddy’, where ‘Uproar’ is part of the foreplay; in ‘Frigid Woman’, ‘Uproar’ substitutes for the sex act itself. Thus in ‘Beat Me Daddy’, ‘Uproar’ is a condition of the sexual act, a kind of fetish which increases the excitement, while in ‘Frigid Woman’, once ‘Uproar’ has taken place, the episode is finished.

《性冷淡的女人》的关键在于“骚动”的终结阶段。一旦骚动结束，性亲密便无从谈起，因为双方都从“骚动”中获得了一种变态的满足感，不再需要彼此提供进一步的性刺激。因此，对抗《性冷淡的女人》最重要的策略就是拒绝“骚动”。这会让妻子陷入性欲不满的状态，这种不满可能非常强烈，以至于她会变得更加顺从。“骚动”的运用使《性冷淡的女人》区别于《打我吧，爸爸》，在《打我吧，爸爸》中，“骚动”是前戏的一部分；而在《性冷淡的女人》中，“骚动”则取代了性行为本身。因此，在《打我吧，爸爸》中，“骚动”是性行为的一种条件，一种增强兴奋感的恋物癖，而在《性冷淡的女人》中，“骚动”一旦发生，整个过程就结束了。

An early analogue of ‘Frigid Woman’ is played by that type of prissy little girl described by Dickens in Great Expectations. She comes out in her starched dress and asks the little boy to make her a mud pie. Then she sneers at his dirty hands and clothing and tells him how clean she is.

早期“冷漠女人”的原型，是由狄更斯在《远大前程》中描写的那种娇滴滴的小女孩扮演的。她穿着浆洗过的裙子出来，让小男孩给她做泥巴派。然后她嘲笑小男孩脏兮兮的手和衣服，告诉他自己有多干净。

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: Now I’ve got you, you son of a bitch.

论点：现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋。

Aim: Vindication.

目的：证明清白。

Roles: Proper Wife, Inconsiderate Husband.

角色：贤惠妻子，不体贴丈夫。

Dynamics: Penis envy.

动态：阴茎嫉妒。

Examples: (1) Thank you for the mud pie, you dirty little boy. (2) Provocative, frigid wife.

例如：（1）谢谢你的泥巴派，你这个脏兮兮的小男孩。（2）挑逗又冷淡的妻子。

Social Paradigm: Parent-Child.

社会范式：亲子关系。

Parent: ‘I give you permission to make me a mud pie (kiss me).’

家长：“我允许你给我做泥巴派（亲我）。”

Child: ‘I’d love to.’

孩子：“我很乐意。”

Parent: ‘Now see how dirty you are.’

家长：“看看你有多脏！”

Psychological Paradigm: Child-Parent.

心理范式：儿童-父母。

Child: ‘See if you can seduce me.’

孩子：“看看你能不能勾引我。”

Parent: ‘I’ll try, if you stop me.’

家长：“如果你阻止我，我就试试。”

Child: ‘See, it was you who started it.’

孩子：“你看，是你先挑起的。”

Moves: (1) Seduction-Response. (2) Rejection-Resignation. (3) Provocation-Response. (4) Rejection-Uproar.

策略：（1）诱惑-回应。（2）拒绝-放弃。（3）挑衅-回应。（4）拒绝-骚动。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – freedom from guilt for sadistic fantasies. (2) External Psychological – avoids feared exhibition and penetration. (3) Internal Social – ‘Uproar’. (4) External Social – What do you do with dirty little boys (husbands)? (5) Biological – inhibited sex play and belligerent exchanges. (6) Existential – I am pure.

优势：（1）内在心理层面——摆脱了因施虐幻想而产生的罪恶感。（2）外在心理层面——避免了恐惧的暴露和性侵犯。（3）内在社会层面——“引起轩然大波”。（4）外在社会层面——如何处置肮脏的小男孩（丈夫）？（5）生理层面——抑制了性游戏和好斗的性行为。（6）存在层面——我是纯洁的。

4 · HARRIED

4 · 疲惫的

Thesis. This is a game played by the harried housewife. Her situation requires that she be proficient in ten or twelve different occupations; or, stated otherwise, that she fill gracefully ten or twelve different roles. From time to time semi-facetious lists of these occupations or roles appear in the Sunday supplements: mistress, mother, nurse, housemaid, etc. Since these roles are usually conflicting and fatiguing, their imposition gives rise in the course of years to the condition symbolically known as ‘Housewife’s Knee’ (since the knee is used for rocking, scrubbing, lifting, driving and so forth), whose symptoms are succinctly summarized in the complaint: ‘I’m tired.’

论文：这是一场由疲惫不堪的家庭主妇玩的游戏。她们的处境要求她们精通十到十二种不同的职业；或者换句话说，她们要优雅地扮演十到十二种不同的角色。这些职业或角色的清单时不时会在周日增刊上出现，但语气略带讽刺：女主人、母亲、护士、女佣等等。由于这些角色通常相互冲突且令人疲惫，多年下来，她们会患上一种被形象地称为“主妇膝”的疾病（因为膝盖要用来摇晃、擦洗、提举、开车等等），其症状可以用一句抱怨来概括：“我累了。”

Now, if the housewife is able to set her own pace and find enough satisfaction in loving her husband and children, she will not merely serve but enjoy her twenty-five years, and see the youngest child off to college with a pang of loneliness. But if on the one hand she is driven by her inner Parent and called to account by the critical husband she has chosen for that purpose, and on the other unable to get sufficient satisfaction from loving her family, she may grow more and more unhappy. At first she may try to console herself with the advantages of ‘If It Weren’t For You’ and ‘Blemish’ (and indeed, any housewife may fall back on these when the going gets rough); but soon these fail to keep her going. Then she has to find another way out, and that is the game of ‘Harried’.
