如果家庭主妇能够按照自己的节奏生活，并在爱丈夫和孩子中获得足够的满足感，她不仅能尽职尽责地完成二十五年的婚姻，还能享受其中，并在送最小的孩子上大学时，带着一丝淡淡的孤独感离开。但如果一方面，她被内心的“父母”角色所驱使，又被她为此选择的、爱挑剔的丈夫所责备；另一方面，她又无法从爱家人中获得足够的满足感，那么她可能会越来越不快乐。起初，她或许会试图用《如果不是你》和《瑕疵》这两首歌来安慰自己（事实上，任何家庭主妇在遇到困难时都可能求助于这些歌）；但很快，这些歌就无法支撑她继续生活下去。这时，她就不得不寻找另一种出路，那就是玩《忙碌》这款游戏。

The thesis of this game is simple. She takes on everything that comes, and even asks for more. She agrees with her husband’s criticisms and accepts all her children’s demands. If she has to entertain at dinner, she not only feels she must function impeccably as a conversationalist, chatelaine over the household and servants, interior decorator, caterer, glamour girl, virgin queen and diplomat ; she will also volunteer that morning to bake a cake and take the children to the dentist. If she already feels harassed, she makes the day even more harried. Then in the middle of the afternoon she justifiably collapses, and nothing gets done. She lets down her husband, the children and their guests, and her self-reproaches add to her misery. After this happens two or three times her marriage is in jeopardy, the children are confused, she loses weight, her hair is untidy, her face is drawn and her shoes are scuffed. Then she appears at the psychiatrist’s office, ready to be hospitalized.

这个游戏的逻辑很简单。她承担一切，甚至还要求更多。她赞同丈夫的批评，接受孩子们的所有要求。如果晚宴要招待客人，她不仅觉得自己必须完美地扮演好健谈者、管家、室内设计师、餐饮策划者、魅力女郎、贞洁女王和外交官的角色，而且当天早上还会主动要求烤蛋糕，带孩子们去看牙医。如果她已经感到疲惫不堪，她还会让这一天更加忙碌。然后到了下午，她理所当然地崩溃了，什么事都做不成。她让丈夫、孩子和客人失望，而她的自责更让她痛苦不堪。这种情况发生两三次后，她的婚姻岌岌可危，孩子们感到困惑，她体重下降，头发蓬乱，面容憔悴，鞋子也磨损了。然后她出现在精神科医生的办公室，准备住院治疗。

Antithesis. The logical antithesis is simple: Mrs White can fill each of her roles in succession during the week, but she must refuse to play two or more of them simultaneously. When she gives a cocktail party, for example, she can play either caterer or nursemaid, but not both. If she is merely suffering from Housewife’s Knee, she may be able to limit herself in this way.

反义词。逻辑上的反义词很简单：怀特太太可以在一周内依次扮演各种角色，但她必须拒绝同时扮演两个或两个以上的角色。例如，当她举办鸡尾酒会时，她可以扮演餐饮服务员或保姆，但不能两者兼顾。如果她只是患上了“主妇膝”，那么她或许能够通过这种方式限制自己。

If she is actually playing a game of ‘Harried’, however, it will be very difficult for her to adhere to this principle. In that case the husband is carefully chosen; he is an otherwise reasonable man who will criticize his wife if she is not as efficient as he thinks his mother was. In effect, she marries his fantasy of his mother as perpetuated in his Parent, which is similar to her fantasy of her mother or grandmother. Having found a suitable partner, her Child can now settle into the harassed role necessary to maintain her psychic balance, and which she will not readily give up. The more occupational responsibility the husband has, the easier it is for both of them to find Adult reasons to preserve the unhealthy aspects of their relationship.

然而，如果她真的在玩“被照顾”的游戏，那么她就很难坚持这个原则。在这种情况下，丈夫是经过精心挑选的；他平时是个通情达理的人，如果妻子不如他想象中的母亲那样能干，他就会批评她。实际上，她嫁给了他从父母身上继承下来的、对母亲的幻想，这与她对母亲或祖母的幻想类似。找到合适的伴侣后，她的孩子就可以安于这种为了维持心理平衡而不得不扮演的“被照顾”的角色，而且她不会轻易放弃这种角色。丈夫的职业责任越大，他们就越容易找到各种“成人”的理由来维持这段不健康的关系。

When the position becomes untenable, often because of official school intervention on behalf of the unhappy offspring, the psychiatrist is called in to make it a three-handed game. Either the husband wants him to do an overhaul job on the wife, or the wife wants him as an ally against the husband. The ensuing proceedings depend on the skill and alertness of the psychiatrist. Usually the first phase, the alleviation of the wife’s depression, will proceed smoothly. The second phase, in which she will give up playing ‘Harried’ in favour of playing ‘Psychiatry’, is the decisive one. It tends to arouse increasing opposition from both spouses. Sometimes this is well concealed and then explodes suddenly, though not unexpectedly. If this stage is weathered, then the real work of game analysis can proceed.

当局面变得难以维系时——通常是由于学校官方介入，代表不满的孩子进行干预——精神科医生就会被请来，使之变成一场三方博弈。要么是丈夫希望他彻底改造妻子，要么是妻子希望他成为对抗丈夫的盟友。接下来的进展取决于精神科医生的技巧和敏锐度。通常，第一阶段，即缓解妻子的抑郁症，会进展顺利。第二阶段，妻子会放弃扮演“疲惫不堪”的角色，转而扮演“精神科医生”的角色，这才是决定性的。这往往会激起夫妻双方日益强烈的反对。有时这种反对被巧妙地隐藏起来，然后突然爆发，虽然并非毫无预兆。如果能顺利度过这个阶段，真正的博弈分析工作才能开始。

It is necessary to recognize that the real culprit is the wife’s Parent, her mother or grandmother; the husband is to some extent only a lay figure chosen to play his role in the game. The therapist has to fight not only this Parent and the husband, who has a heavy investment in playing his end, but also the social environment, which encourages the wife’s compliance. The week after the article appears about the many roles a housewife has to play, there is a How’m I Doing? in the Sunday paper: a ten-item test to determine ‘How Good A Hostess (Wife) (Mother) (Housekeeper) (Budgeteer) Are You?’ For the housewife who plays ‘Harried’, that is the equivalent of the little leaflet that comes with children’s games, stating the rules. It may help to speed up the evolution of ‘Harried’, which, if not checked, may end in a game of ‘State Hospital’ (‘The last thing I want is to be sent to a hospital’).

必须认识到，真正的罪魁祸首是妻子的父母，她的母亲或祖母；丈夫在某种程度上只是一个被选中扮演游戏角色的普通人。治疗师不仅要与这位父母和丈夫作斗争（丈夫在扮演自己的角色上投入了大量精力），还要与鼓励妻子顺从的社会环境作斗争。在关于家庭主妇必须扮演多种角色的文章发表后的一周，周日报纸上刊登了一篇名为“我做得怎么样？”的专栏文章：一个包含十道题的测试，旨在评估“你作为女主人（妻子）（母亲）（管家）（理财者）做得如何？”对于那些扮演“忙碌不堪”角色的家庭主妇来说，这相当于儿童游戏附带的小册子，上面写着游戏规则。这或许有助于加速“忙碌不堪”角色的演变，如果不加以控制，最终可能会演变成一场“被送进医院”的游戏（“我最不想的就是被送进医院”）。

One practical difficulty with such couples is that the husband tends to avoid personal involvement with the treatment beyond playing ‘Look How Hard I’m Trying’, because he is usually more disturbed than he cares to admit. Instead he may send indirect messages to the therapist, through temper outbursts which he knows will be reported by the wife. Hence ‘Harried’ easily progresses to a third-degree life-death-divorce struggle. The psychiatrist is almost alone on the side of life, assisted only by the harried Adult of the patient which is locked in combat that may prove mortal against all three aspects of the husband, allied with her own inner Parent and Child. It is a dramatic battle, with odds of two against five, which tries the skill of the most game-free and professional therapist. If he quails, he can take the easy way out and offer his patient on the altar of the divorce court, which is equivalent to saying ‘I surrender – Let’s you and him fight.’

这类夫妻面临的一个实际难题是，丈夫往往会避免真正参与治疗，只会装出一副“我多么努力”的样子，因为他通常比自己愿意承认的更加痛苦。相反，他可能会通过发脾气来间接地向治疗师传递信息，而他知道妻子会把这些情绪告诉治疗师。因此，“疲惫不堪”很容易演变成一场生死攸关的离婚大战。精神科医生几乎孤军奋战，唯一能帮他的只有病人内心那个疲惫不堪的“成年人”，她要与丈夫的三个方面——包括她内心的“父母”和“孩子”——展开一场可能致命的战斗。这是一场势均力敌的较量，即使是最冷静、最专业的治疗师也会面临严峻的考验。如果他退缩了，他可以选择最简单的办法，把病人送上离婚法庭，这相当于说“我投降了——让你们俩打吧。”

5 · IF IT WEREN’T FOR YOU

5. 如果不是因为你

Thesis. The detailed analysis of this game has already been given in Chapter 5 . It was historically the second game uncovered, after ‘Why Don’t You – Yes But’, which up to that point had been regarded merely as an interesting phenomenon. With the additional discovery of IWFY, it became clear that there must be a whole department of social action based on ulterior transactions. This led to a more active search for such goings-on, and the present collection is one outcome.

论文。第五章已对本博弈进行了详细分析。从历史上看，它是继“Why Don’t You – Yes But”之后发现的第二个博弈，而“Why Don’t You – Yes But”此前一直被视为一种有趣的现象。随着“Why Don’t You – Yes But”的发现，人们逐渐意识到，必然存在一个基于秘密交易的社会行动领域。这促使人们更加积极地寻找此类活动，而本书正是其中一项成果。

Briefly, a woman marries a domineering man so that he will restrict her activities and thus keep her from getting into situations which frighten her. If this were a simple operation, she might express her gratitude when he performed this service for her. In the game of IWFY, however, her reaction is quite the opposite: she takes advantage of the situation to complain about the restrictions, which makes her spouse feel uneasy and gives her all sorts of advantages. This game is the internal social advantage. The external social advantage is the derivative pastime ‘If It Weren’t For Him’, which she plays with her congenial lady friends.

简而言之，一个女人嫁给一个专横的男人，是为了让他限制她的活动，从而避免她陷入令她恐惧的境地。如果这只是一个简单的操作，她或许会在他为她“服务”时表达感激之情。然而，在“如果不是他”（If It Were’t For Him）游戏中，她的反应却截然相反：她会利用这种情况抱怨这些限制，这让她的丈夫感到不安，并给她带来各种好处。这种游戏是内部社交优势。而外部社交优势则是衍生出的消遣游戏“如果不是他”（If It Were’t For Him），她会和她的闺蜜们一起玩这个游戏。

6 · LOOK HOW HARD I’VE TRIED

6 · 看看我有多努力

Thesis . In its common clinical form this is a three-handed game played by a married couple with a psychiatrist. The husband (usually) is bucking for a divorce, despite loud protestations to the contrary, while the spouse is more sincere in wanting to continue the marriage. He comes to the therapist under protest and talks just enough to demonstrate to the wife that he is cooperating; usually he plays a mild game of ‘Psychiatry’ or ‘Courtroom’. As time passes he exhibits either increasingly resentful pseudo-compliance or belligerent argumentativeness towards the therapist. At home he initially shows more ‘understanding’ and restraint, and finally behaves worse than ever. After one, five or ten visits, depending on the skill of the therapist, he refuses to come any longer and goes hunting or fishing instead. The wife is then forced into filing for divorce. The husband is now blameless, since his wife has taken the initiative and he has demonstrated his good faith by going to the therapist. He is in a good position to say to any attorney, judge, friend or relative, ‘Look how hard I’ve tried!’

论点：在常见的临床表现中，这就像一对夫妻与一位精神科医生之间的一场三方博弈。丈夫（通常）极力想要离婚，尽管他极力反对，而妻子则更真诚地希望维持婚姻。他带着怨恨来到治疗师那里，只说一些话来向妻子表明他正在配合；通常他会玩一场温和的“精神病学”或“法庭”游戏。随着时间的推移，他要么表现出越来越怨恨的伪装顺从，要么表现出好斗的争辩。在家，他起初表现得更加“理解”和克制，但最终行为却比以往任何时候都更加恶劣。经过一次、五次或十次治疗后（取决于治疗师的技巧），他拒绝继续治疗，转而去打猎或钓鱼。妻子被迫提出离婚。此时，丈夫已无过错，因为是妻子主动提出的，而他通过去看治疗师表明了自己的诚意。他完全可以对任何律师、法官、朋友或亲戚说：“看看我多么努力！”

Antithesis. The couple is seen together. If one – let us say the husband – is clearly playing this game, the other is taken into individual treatment and the player is sent on his way, on the valid ground that he is less ready for therapy. He can still get a divorce, but only at the expense of abandoning his position that he is really trying. If necessary, the wife can start the divorce, and her position is much improved since she really has tried. The favourable, hoped-for outcome is that the husband, his game broken up, will go into a state of despair and then seek treatment elsewhere with genuine motivation.

对比。夫妻二人一同接受治疗。如果其中一方——比如丈夫——明显在玩弄婚姻游戏，另一方则被安排接受单独治疗，而玩弄婚姻游戏的人则会被送走，理由是他尚未做好接受治疗的准备。他仍然可以离婚，但代价是放弃他“真心努力”的立场。如有必要，妻子可以提出离婚，而且由于她确实努力过，她的处境会好得多。理想的结果是，丈夫的婚姻游戏被打破后，会陷入绝望，然后出于真正的动机去寻求其他治疗。

In its everyday form this is easily observed in children as a two-handed game with one parent. It is played from either of two positions: ‘I am helpless’ or ‘I am blameless’. The child tries, but bungles or is unsuccessful. If he is Helpless, the parent has to do it for him. If he is Blameless, the parent has no reasonable grounds for punishing him. This reveals the elements of the game. The parents should find out two things: which of them taught the child this game; and what they are doing to perpetuate it.

这种游戏在日常生活中很容易观察到，孩子们经常和父母玩这种双人游戏。游戏有两种角色：“我无能为力”或“我无辜”。孩子尝试，但总是搞砸或失败。如果孩子扮演“无能为力”的角色，父母就必须替他完成。如果孩子扮演“无辜”的角色，父母就没有理由惩罚他。这揭示了游戏的本质。父母应该弄清楚两件事：是谁教孩子玩这个游戏的；以及他们正在做什么来延续这个游戏。

An interesting, though sometimes sinister, variant is ‘Look How Hard I Was Trying’, which is usually a harder game of the second or third degree. This can be illustrated by the case of a hardworking man with a gastric ulcer. There are many people with progressive physical disabilities who do the best they can to cope with the situation, and they may enlist the help of their families in a legitimate way. Such conditions, however, can also be exploited for ulterior purposes.

一种有趣但有时也颇为险恶的变体是“看看我有多努力”，这通常是比一般人更难的盘问。一个患有胃溃疡却勤劳的男人就是个很好的例子。许多患有进行性身体残疾的人都在尽力应对困境，他们或许会以正当的方式寻求家人的帮助。然而，这种情况也可能被别有用心的人利用。

First Degree: A man announces to his wife and friends that he has an ulcer. He also lets them know that he is continuing to work. This elicits their admiration. Perhaps a person with a painful and unpleasant condition is entitled to a certain amount of ostentation as a poor recompense for his suffering. He should be given due credit for not playing ‘Wooden Leg’ instead, and deserves some reward for continuing to assume his responsibilities. In such a case, the courteous reply to ‘Look How Hard I’m Trying’ is, ‘Yes, we all admire your fortitude and conscientiousness.’

一级：一个男人告诉妻子和朋友们他得了胃溃疡，还说自己仍在工作。这赢得了他们的钦佩。或许，一个身患重病的人，理应得到一些炫耀，作为对他所受痛苦的微薄补偿。他没有选择“装病”，而是坚持工作，理应得到一些奖励。在这种情况下，对于“你看我多么努力”这种说法，礼貌的回应应该是：“是的，我们都很钦佩你的坚韧和尽责。”

Second Degree: A man is told that he has an ulcer, but keeps it a secret from his wife and friends. He continues working and worrying as hard as ever, and one day he collapses on the job. When his wife is notified, she gets the message instantly: ‘Look How Hard I Was Trying. ‘Now she is supposed to appreciate him as she never has before, and to feel sorry for all the mean things she has said and done in the past. In short, she is now supposed to love him, all previous methods of wooing her having failed. Unfortunately for the husband, her manifestations of affection and solicitude at this point are more apt to be motivated by guilt than by love. Deep down she is likely to be resentful because he is using unfair leverage against her, and has also taken unfair advantage of her by keeping his illness a secret. In short, a diamond bracelet is a much more honest instrument of courtship than a perforated stomach. She has the option of throwing the jewellery back at him, but she cannot decently walk out on the ulcer. A sudden confrontation with a serious illness is more likely to make her feel trapped than won over.

二级情境：一个男人被告知自己得了胃溃疡，但他对妻子和朋友隐瞒了病情。他像往常一样继续努力工作，忧心忡忡，直到有一天在工作中突然晕倒。当妻子得知此事后，她立刻明白了丈夫的意思：“看看我之前有多努力！”现在，她应该像以前从未有过的那样感激他，并为过去说过和做过的所有刻薄事感到愧疚。简而言之，她现在应该爱上他，因为之前所有追求她的手段都失败了。不幸的是，妻子此时表现出的爱意和关心，与其说是出于爱，不如说是出于愧疚。她内心深处很可能心怀怨恨，因为他利用了她的病情，而且隐瞒病情也占了她的便宜。简而言之，一条钻石手链远比一个胃穿孔更真诚地表达爱意。她可以选择把珠宝扔回去，但她无法体面地离开他的胃溃疡。突如其来的重病更可能让她感到无助，而不是被战胜。

This game can often be discovered immediately after the patient first hears that he has a potentially progressive disability. If he is going to play it, the whole plan will very likely flash through his mind at that point, and can be recovered by a careful psychiatric review of the situation. What is recovered is the secret gloating of his Child at learning that he has such a weapon, masked by his Adult concern at the practical problems raised by his illness.

这种游戏往往在患者首次得知自己可能患有进行性残疾后立即被发现。如果他打算玩这个游戏，那么整个计划很可能在那一刻就闪现在他的脑海中，而通过仔细的精神科评估可以将其还原。还原出来的是他内心深处孩童般的得意，得知自己拥有这样一件“武器”后暗自窃喜，而这种得意却被他成人般的担忧所掩盖，后者担忧的是疾病带来的实际问题。

Third Degree: Even more sinister and spiteful is the sudden unheralded suicide because of serious illness. The ulcer progresses to cancer, and one day the wife, who has never been informed that anything serious is amiss, walks into the bathroom and finds her husband lying there dead. The note says clearly enough, ‘Look How Hard I Was Trying.’ If something like this happens twice to the same woman, it is time for her to find out what she has been playing.

第三重：更阴险、更恶毒的是，丈夫因重病突然自杀，事先没有任何征兆。溃疡发展成癌症，妻子从未被告知丈夫有任何严重问题，有一天她走进浴室，发现丈夫躺在那里已经去世。遗书上写着：“看看我有多努力。” 如果这样的事情发生在同一个女人身上两次，她就该好好反思一下自己究竟在玩什么把戏了。

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: They can’t push me around.

论点：他们不能欺负我。

Aim: Vindication.

目的：证明清白。

Roles: Standfast, Persecutor, Authority.

角色：坚定不移者、迫害者、权威。

Dynamics: Anal passivity.

动力学：肛门被动。

Examples: (1) Child dressing. (2) Spouse bucking for divorce.

例如：（1）儿童穿衣。（2）配偶反对离婚。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult: ‘It’s time to (get dressed) (go to a psychiatrist).’

成年人：“该（穿好衣服）（去看精神科医生）了。”

Adult: ‘All right, I’ll try it.’

成人：“好的，我试试。”

Psychological Paradigm: Parent-Child.

心理学范式：亲子关系。

Parent: ‘I’m going to make you (get dressed) (go to a psychiatrist).’

家长：“我要让你（穿好衣服）（去看精神科医生）。”

Child: ‘See, it doesn’t work.’

孩子：“你看，这根本行不通。”

Moves: (1) Suggestion-Resistance. (2) Pressure-Compliance. (3) Approval-Failure.

策略：（1）建议-抵制。（2）压力-顺从。（3）批准-失败。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – freedom from guilt for aggression. (2) External Psychological – evades domestic responsibilities. (3) Internal Social – Look how hard I’ve tried. (4) External Social – same. (5) Biological – belligerent exchanges. (6) Existential – I am helpless (blameless).

优势：（1）内在心理层面——免于因攻击行为而产生的内疚感。（2）外在心理层面——逃避家庭责任。（3）内在社会层面——看看我多么努力。（4）外在社会层面——同上。（5）生理层面——好斗的冲突。（6）存在层面——我无能为力（无罪）。

7 · SWEETHEART

7 · 甜心

Thesis. This is seen in its fullest flower in the early stages of marital group therapy, when the parties feel defensive; it can also be observed on social occasions. White makes a subtly derogatory remark about Mrs White, disguised as an anecdote, and ends: ‘Isn’t that right, sweetheart?’ Mrs White tends to agree for two ostensibly Adult reasons: (a) because the anecdote itself is in the main, accurately reported, and to disagree about what is presented as a peripheral detail (but is really the essential point of the transaction) would seem pedantic; (b) because it would seem surly to disagree with a man who calls one ‘sweetheart’ in public. The psychological reason for her agreement, however, is her depressive position. She married him precisely because she knew he would perform this service for her: exposing her deficiencies and thus saving her from the embarrassment of having to expose them herself. Her parents accommodated her the same way when she was little.

论点。这种现象在婚姻团体治疗的早期阶段表现得最为明显，此时双方都感到防卫；在社交场合也能观察到。怀特先生用一个轶事伪装成对怀特太太的微妙贬损之词，最后说道：“是吧，亲爱的？”怀特太太往往会表示同意，表面上有两个成年人的理由：(a) 因为轶事本身基本准确，而对一个被当作次要细节（但实际上是关键所在）的事情提出异议似乎显得迂腐；(b) 因为反驳一个在公共场合称呼自己“亲爱的”的男人似乎显得很无礼。然而，她同意的心理原因在于她抑郁的状态。她嫁给他正是因为她知道他会为她做这件事：揭露她的缺点，从而让她免于自己暴露这些缺点的尴尬。她小时候，她的父母也用同样的方式迁就她。

Next to ‘Courtroom’, this is the most common game played in marital groups. The more tense the situation, and the closer the game is to exposure, the more bitterly is the word ‘sweetheart’ enunciated, until the underlying resentment becomes obvious. On careful consideration it can be seen that this is a relative of ‘Schlemiel’, since the significant move is Mrs White’s implicit forgiveness for White’s resentment, of which she is trying hard not to be aware. Hence anti-‘Sweetheart’ is played analogously to anti-‘Schlemiel’: ‘You can tell derogatory anecdotes about me, but please don’t call me “sweetheart”.’ This antithesis carries with it the same perils as does anti-‘Schlemiel’. A more sophisticated and less dangerous antithesis is to reply: ‘Yes, honey !’

在夫妻游戏中，除了“法庭”之外，这是最常见的游戏。气氛越紧张，越接近真相大白，对方就越会用苦涩的语气说出“亲爱的”这个词，直到隐藏的怨恨显露出来。仔细想想，这和“笨蛋”游戏有相似之处，因为关键在于怀特太太对怀特心怀怨恨的隐晦原谅，而她自己却极力掩饰。因此，“反‘亲爱的’”游戏的玩法与“反‘笨蛋’”类似：“你可以讲我的坏话，但请不要叫我‘亲爱的’。”这种反讽和“反‘笨蛋’”一样，都存在风险。一个更巧妙、更安全的反讽是回答：“好的，亲爱的！”

In another form the wife, instead of agreeing, responds with a similar ‘Sweetheart’ type anecdote about the husband, saying in effect, ‘You have a dirty face too, dear.’

另一种说法是，妻子不但不表示同意，而是用一个类似的“亲爱的”式轶事来回应丈夫，实际上是说：“亲爱的，你的脸也很脏。”

Sometimes the endearments are not actually pronounced, but a careful listener can hear them even when they are unspoken. This is ‘Sweetheart’, Silent Type.

有时，爱称并没有真正说出口，但细心的倾听者即使没有说出口也能听出来。这就是“甜心”，一种无声的称呼。

REFERENCE

参考

1. Bateson, G., et al., ‘Toward a Theory of Schizophrenia’, Behavioral Science, 1: 251–264, 1956.

1. Bateson, G. 等人，《精神分裂症理论初探》，行为科学，1：251-264，1956 年。

#↩

8 · Party Games

8. 派对游戏

P ARTIES are for pastimes, and pastimes are for parties (including the period before a group meeting officially begins), but as acquaintanceship ripens, games begin to emerge. The Schlemiel and his victim recognize each other, as do Big Daddy and Little Old Me; all the familiar but disregarded processes of selection get under way. In this section four games which are typically played in ordinary social situations are considered: ‘Ain’t It Awful’, ‘Blemish’, ‘Schlemiel’, and ‘Why Don’t You – Yes But’.

聚会是消遣，消遣也是聚会的一部分（包括正式聚会前的这段时间），但随着彼此了解的加深，各种游戏也开始出现。笨蛋和他的受害者彼此认出对方，就像老爸和我一样；所有那些熟悉却常被忽视的选择过程都开始运转。本节将探讨四种通常在日常社交场合中玩的游戏：“真糟糕”、“瑕疵”、“笨蛋”和“你为什么不——是的，但是……”

1 · AIN’T IT AWFUL

1 · 这难道不糟糕吗？

Thesis. This is played in four significant forms: Parental pastime, Adult pastime, Child pastime and game. In the pastimes there is no denouement or payoff, but much unworthy feeling.

论文指出，这种行为主要有四种形式：父母消遣、成人消遣、儿童消遣和游戏。这些消遣没有结局或回报，却充斥着许多不值得的感受。

1. ‘Nowadays’ is the self-righteous, punitive or even vicious Parental pastime. Sociologically it is common among certain types of middle-aged women with small independent incomes. One such woman withdrew from a therapy group when her opening move was met with silence instead of with the excited corroboration she was accustomed to in her social circle. In this more sophisticated group, accustomed to game analysis, there was a conspicuous lack of togetherness when White remarked: ‘Speaking of not trusting people, it’s no wonder you can’t trust anyone nowadays. I was looking through the desk of one of my roomers, and you won’t believe what I found.’ She knew the answers to most of the current community problems: juvenile delinquency (parents too soft nowadays); divorce (wives without enough to do to keep them busy nowadays); crime (foreigners moving into white neighbourhoods nowadays); and rising prices (businessmen too grasping nowadays). She made it clear that she herself was not soft with her delinquent son, nor with her delinquent tenants.

1. “如今”是父母自以为是、惩罚性甚至恶毒的消遣。从社会学角度来看，这种现象在某些收入微薄的中年女性群体中很常见。一位这样的女性在接受治疗小组时，因为开局没有得到她社交圈中惯常的热烈赞同，而是一片沉默，于是退出了小组。在这个更成熟、习惯于博弈分析的小组里，当怀特说道：“说到不信任人，难怪现在谁都不能信任。我翻看了一个室友的桌子，你绝对想不到我发现了什么。”时，小组内部明显缺乏凝聚力。她似乎知道当前大多数社区问题的答案：青少年犯罪（如今的父母太溺爱孩子）；离婚（如今的妻子无所事事）；犯罪（如今的外国人涌入白人社区）；以及物价上涨（如今的商人太贪婪）。她明确表示，她对自己不听话的儿子和拖欠房租的房客都不会心软。

‘Nowadays’ is differentiated from idle gossip by its slogan ‘It’s no wonder’. The opening move may be the same (‘They say that Flossie Murgatroyd’), but in ‘Nowadays’ there is direction and closure; an ‘explanation’ may be offered. Idle gossip merely rambles or trails off.

“Nowadays”与闲言碎语的区别在于它的口号“难怪”。虽然开头可能相同（“据说弗洛西·默格特罗伊德……”），但“Nowadays”更有方向性和结尾，甚至可能提供“解释”。而闲言碎语则只是漫无目的地闲聊或草草收尾。

2. ‘Broken Skin’ is the more benevolent Adult variation, with the slogan ‘What a pity!’ although the underlying motivations are equally morbid. ‘Broken Skin’ deals primarily with the flow of blood; it is essentially an informal clinical colloquium. Anyone is eligible to present a case, the more horrifying the better, and details are eagerly considered. Blows in the face, abdominal operations and difficult childbirths are accepted topics. Here the differentiation from idle gossip lies in the rivalry and surgical sophistication. Pathological anatomy, diagnosis, prognosis and comparative case studies are systematically pursued. A good prognosis is approved in idle gossip, but in ‘Broken Skin’ a consistently hopeful outlook, unless obviously insincere, may invoke a secret meeting of the Credentials Committee because the player is non particeps criminis.

2. “破皮”是成人版的较为温和的变体，其口号是“真可惜！”，尽管其潜在动机同样病态。“破皮”主要讨论血液流动；它本质上是一个非正式的临床研讨会。任何人都可以提交病例，越恐怖越好，细节也会被仔细考虑。面部受伤、腹部手术和难产都是可以接受的话题。这里与闲聊的区别在于竞争和外科手术的精湛技艺。病理解剖、诊断、预后和病例比较研究都会被系统地进行探讨。在闲聊中，良好的预后会被认可，但在“破皮”中，除非明显虚伪，否则一贯乐观的态度可能会引发资格审查委员会的秘密会议，因为参与者属于非犯罪参与者。

3. ‘Water Cooler’, or ‘Coffee Break’, is the Child pastime, with the slogan ‘Look what they’re doing to us now.’ This is an organizational variant. It may be played after dark in the milder political or economic form called ‘Bar Stool’. It is actually three-handed, the ace being held by the often shadowy figure called ‘They’.

3. “饮水机游戏”或“咖啡休息时间游戏”是孩子们的消遣，口号是“看看他们现在对我们做了什么”。这是一种组织上的变体。它也可以在夜幕降临后以较为温和的政治或经济形式出现，称为“酒吧凳子游戏”。实际上，它是三人游戏，王牌由通常被称为“他们”的神秘人物持有。

4. As a game, ‘Ain’t It Awful’ finds its most dramatic expression in polysurgery addicts, and their transactions illustrate its characteristics. These are doctor-shoppers, people who actively seek surgery even in the face of sound medical opposition. The experience itself, the hospitalization and surgery, brings its own advantages. The internal psychological advantage comes from having the body mutilated; the external psychological advantage lies in the avoidance of all intimacies and responsibilities except complete surrender to the surgeon. The biological advantages are typified by nursing care. The internal social advantages come from the medical and nursing staff, and from other patients. After the patient’s discharge the external social advantages are gained by provoking sympathy and awe. In its extreme form this game is played professionally by fraudulent or determined liability and malpractice claimants, who may earn a living by deliberately or opportunistically incurring disabilities. They then demand not only sympathy, as amateur players do, but indemnification. ‘Ain’t It Awful’ becomes a game, then, when the player overtly expresses distress, but is covertly gratified at the prospect of the satisfactions he can wring from his misfortune.

4. 作为一种游戏，“这太可怕了”在过度依赖多次手术的人群中表现得最为极端，他们的行为也充分体现了这种游戏的特征。这些人是“医生购物者”，即使面对合理的医学反对意见，他们仍然积极寻求手术。住院和手术本身就具有其独特的优势。内在的心理优势来自于身体遭受的“残害”；外在的心理优势在于除了完全臣服于外科医生之外，可以避免所有亲密关系和责任。生理上的优势体现在护理服务上。内在的社会优势则来自医护人员和其他患者。患者出院后，他们通过博取同情和敬畏来获得外在的社会优势。在极端情况下，这种游戏被一些职业欺诈者或蓄意索赔者所利用，他们可能通过故意或投机取巧地造成残疾来谋生。然后，他们不仅像业余玩家一样寻求同情，还要求赔偿。因此，“Ain’t It Awful”就变成了一种游戏，玩家表面上表现出痛苦，但实际上却暗自满足于从自己的不幸中获得的满足感。

In general, people who suffer misfortunes may be divided into three classes.

一般来说，遭遇不幸的人可以分为三类。

1. Those in whom the suffering is inadvertent and unwanted. These may or may not exploit the sympathy which is so readily offered to them. Some exploitation is natural enough, and may be treated with common courtesy.

1. 那些遭受苦难并非出于自愿，也并非出于自身意愿的人。这些人可能会利用人们轻易给予的同情，也可能不会。有些利用他人同情的行为是人之常情，可以用基本的礼貌来对待。

2. Those in whom the suffering is inadvertent, but is gratefully received because of the opportunities for exploitation it offers. Here the game is an afterthought, a ‘secondary grain’ in Freud’s sense.

2. 有些人遭受的苦难并非出于本意，而是因为他们乐于接受苦难，因为苦难提供了利用的机会。在这种情况下，游戏只是事后考虑的因素，是弗洛伊德意义上的“次要因素”。

3. Those who seek suffering, like polysurgery addicts who go from one surgeon to another until they find one willing to operate. Here the game is the primary consideration.

3. 有些人寻求痛苦，就像那些沉迷于多次手术的人，他们辗转于各个外科医生之间，直到找到一个愿意为他们动手术的医生。对他们来说，这场游戏才是最重要的。

2 · BLEMISH

2 · 瑕疵

Thesis. This game is the source of a large percentage of petty dissension in everyday life; it is played from the depressive Child position ‘I am no good’, which is protectively transformed into the Parental position ‘They are no good.’ The player’s transactional problem is, then, to prove the latter thesis. Hence ‘Blemish’ players do not feel comfortable with a new person until they have found his blemish. In its hardest form it may become a totalitarian political game played by ‘authoritarian’ personalities, and then it may have serious historical repercussions. Here its close relationship with ‘Nowadays’ is evident. In suburban society positive reassurance is obtained from playing ‘How’m I Doing?’ while ‘Blemish’ provides negative reassurance. A partial analysis will make some of the elements of this game clearer.

论点：这种游戏是日常生活中大量琐碎争执的根源；它始于抑郁的“孩子”角色——“我不好”，这种角色会被保护性地转化为“父母”角色——“他们不好”。因此，玩家的交易问题在于证明后一个论点。所以，“瑕疵”玩家只有在发现对方的瑕疵后，才会对新认识的人感到自在。在最极端的情况下，它可能演变成由“专制”人格者玩的极权政治游戏，并可能造成严重的历史后果。由此可见，它与“当今社会”有着密切的联系。在郊区社会，人们通过玩“我做得怎么样？”游戏获得积极的肯定，而“瑕疵”游戏则提供消极的肯定。部分分析将有助于我们更清晰地理解这种游戏的某些要素。

The premise may range from the most trivial and extraneous (‘Last year’s hat’), to the most cynical (‘Hasn’t got $7,000 in the bank’), sinister (‘Not 100 % Aryan’), esoteric (‘Hasn’t read Rilke’) intimate (‘Can’t hold his erection’) or sophisticated (‘What’s he trying to prove?’). Psychodynamically it is usually based on sexual insecurity, and its aim is reassurance. Transactionally there is prying, morbid curiosity or watchfulness, sometimes with Parental or Adult concern charitably masking the Child’s relish. It has the internal psychological advantage of warding off depression, and the external psychological advantage of avoiding the intimacy which might expose White’s own blemishes. White feels justified in turning away an unfashionable woman, a man without financial backing, a non-Aryan, an illiterate, an impotent man or an insecure personality. At the same time the prying offers some internal social action with biological gain. The external social advantage is of the ‘Ain’t It Awful’ family – Neighbourly Type.

这种假设的范畴很广，从最琐碎无关紧要的（“去年的帽子”）到最愤世嫉俗的（“银行里没7000美元”）、最阴险的（“不是百分之百的雅利安人”）、最深奥的（“没读过里尔克”）、最私密的（“勃起困难”）或最老练的（“他想证明什么？”）。从心理动力学的角度来看，它通常基于性方面的不安全感，其目的是为了获得安慰。从交易的角度来看，它包含窥探、病态的好奇心或监视，有时父母或成年人的关心会出于善意掩盖孩子内心的快感。它具有内在的心理优势，可以预防抑郁；也具有外在的心理优势，可以避免可能暴露自身缺陷的亲密关系。白人觉得有理由拒绝一个不时髦的女人、一个没有经济来源的男人、一个非雅利安人、一个文盲、一个阳痿的男人或一个缺乏安全感的人。与此同时，这种窥探行为也带来了一些内在的社会互动和生理上的益处。而外在的社会优势则体现在“真糟糕”式的家庭——那种邻里关系融洽的类型。

An interesting sidelight is that White’s choice of premise is independent of his intellectual capacity or apparent sophistication. Thus a man who had held some responsible positions in the foreign service of his country told an audience that another country was inferior because, among other things, the men wore jackets with sleeves that were too long. In his Adult ego state this man was quite competent. Only when playing a Parental game like ‘Blemish’ would he mention such irrelevancies.

一个有趣的旁支是，怀特选择的前提与他的智力水平或表面上的世故程度无关。因此，一位曾在本国外交部门担任要职的人士告诉听众，另一个国家不如他，原因之一是那里的男士穿着袖子过长的夹克。在他“成人自我”状态下，这个人相当称职。只有在玩“瑕疵”这类“父母自我”游戏时，他才会提及这些无关紧要的细节。

3 · SCHLEMIEL

3 · 施莱米尔

Tliesis. The term ‘schlemiel’ does not refer to the hero of Chamisso’s novel, 1 who was a man without a shadow, but to a popular Yiddish word allied to the German and Dutch words for cunning. The Schlemiel’s victim, who is something like the ‘Good-Natured Fellow’ of Paul de Kock, 2 is colloquially called the Schlemazl. The moves in a typical game of ‘Schlemiel’ are as follows:

特列西斯。“schlemiel”一词并非指沙米索小说中那个没有影子的主人公，而是指一个流行的意第绪语词汇，与德语和荷兰语中表示狡猾的词汇相关。“Schlemiel”的受害者，类似于保罗·德·科克笔下的“善良的家伙”，俗称“Schlemazl”。典型的“Schlemiel”游戏步骤如下：

1W. White spills a highball on the hostess’s evening gown.

1W. White 不小心把一杯高球酒洒在了女主人的晚礼服上。

1B. Black (the host) responds initially with rage, but he senses (often only vaguely) that if he shows it, White wins. Black therefore pulls himself together, and this gives him the illusion that he wins.

1B. 黑方（东道主）起初怒不可遏，但他隐约感觉到（通常只是模糊地感觉到）如果表现出来，白方就会获胜。因此，黑方强忍怒火，这让他产生了自己获胜的错觉。

2W. White says: ‘I’m sorry.’

2W. White 说：“对不起。”

2B. Black mutters or cries forgiveness, strengthening his illusion that he wins.

2B. 黑魔王低声或哭着请求原谅，这更加强化了他获胜的错觉。

3W. White then proceeds to inflict other damage on Black’s property. He breaks things, spills things and makes messes of various kinds. After the cigarette burn in the tablecloth, the chair leg through the lace curtain and the gravy on the rug, White’s Child is exhilarated because he has enjoyed himself in carrying out these procedures, for all of which he has been forgiven, while Black has made a gratifying display of suffering self-control. Thus both of them profit from an unfortunate situation, and Black is not necessarily anxious to terminate the friendship.

3W. 随后，怀特继续破坏布莱克的财物。他摔东西、洒东西，弄得一团糟。桌布上被烟头烫了个洞，椅子腿戳破了蕾丝窗帘，地毯上沾满了肉汁，怀特的孩子却因此兴奋不已，因为他乐在其中，而且这一切都得到了原谅。与此同时，布莱克则表现出了令人欣慰的克制。就这样，两人都从这场不幸的事件中获益，而布莱克也未必急于结束这段友谊。

As in most games, White, who makes the first move, wins either way. If Black shows his anger, White can feel justified in returning the resentment. If Black restrains himself, White can go on enjoying his opportunities. The real payoff in this game, however, is not the pleasure of destructiveness, which is merely an added bonus for White, but the fact that he obtains forgiveness. * This leads directly into the antithesis.

如同大多数棋局一样，白方先手，无论结果如何都能获胜。如果黑方表现出愤怒，白方可以理直气壮地予以回击。如果黑方克制，白方则可以继续享受胜利的喜悦。然而，这盘棋的真正意义并非在于破坏带来的快感（这仅仅是白方的额外收获），而在于他最终获得了对方的宽恕。这直接引出了反面。

Antithesis. Anti-‘Schlemiel’ is played by not offering the demanded absolution. After White says ‘I’m sorry’, Black, instead of muttering ‘It’s okay’, says, ‘Tonight you can embarrass my wife, ruin the furniture and wreck the rug, but please don’t say “I’m sorry”.’ Here Black switches from being a forgiving Parent to being an objective Adult who takes the full responsibility for having invited White in the first place.

反面。反“笨蛋”的体现是拒绝给予对方所要求的宽恕。在怀特说了“对不起”之后，布莱克没有低声说“没关系”，而是说：“今晚你可以让我妻子难堪，弄坏家具，弄脏地毯，但请不要再说‘对不起’。” 在这里，布莱克从一个宽容的家长转变为一个客观的成年人，他承担了当初邀请怀特来访的全部责任。

The intensity of White’s game will be revealed by his reaction, which may be quite explosive. One who plays anti-‘Schlemiel’ runs the risk of immediate reprisals or, at any rate, of making an enemy.

白方的棋艺强度将从他的反应中体现出来，而他的反应可能相当激烈。采取反“笨棋”策略的人，要么会面临立即遭到报复的风险，要么至少会树敌。

Children play ‘Schlemiel’ in an abortive form in which they are not always sure of forgiveness but at least have the pleasure of making messes; as they learn to comport themselves socially, however, they may take advantage of their increasing sophistication to obtain the forgiveness which is the chief goal of the game as played in polite, grown-up social circles.

孩子们玩“Schlemiel”游戏时，虽然不确定是否会被原谅，但至少可以享受制造混乱的乐趣；然而，随着他们学会如何与人相处，他们可能会利用自己日益增长的成熟度来获得原谅，而这正是该游戏在有礼貌的成人社交圈中的主要目标。

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: I can be destructive and still get forgiveness.

论点：我可以做出破坏性的事情，但仍然可以得到原谅。

Aim: Absolution.

目的：赦免。

Roles: Aggressor, Victim (colloquially, Schlemiel and Schlemazl).

角色：攻击者、受害者（通俗地讲，Schlemiel 和 Schlemazl）。

Dynamics: Anal aggression.

动态：肛门攻击。

Examples: (1) Messily destructive children. (2) Clumsy guest. Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

例如：（1）邋遢又破坏力强的孩子。（2）笨手笨脚的客人。社交模式：成人-成人。

Adult: ‘Since I’m polite, you have to be polite, too.’

成年人：“既然我讲礼貌，你也得讲礼貌。”

Adult: ‘That’s fine. I forgive you.’

成人：“没关系，我原谅你。”

Psychological Paradigm: Child-Parent.

心理范式：儿童-父母。

Child: ‘You have to forgive things which appear accidental.’

孩子：“你必须原谅那些看似偶然的事情。”

Parent: ‘You are right. I have to show you what good manners are.’

家长：“你说得对。我得教你什么是礼貌。”

Moves: (1) Provocation-resentment. (2) Apology-forgiveness.

策略：（1）挑衅-怨恨。（2）道歉-原谅。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – pleasure of messing. (2) External Psychological – Avoids punishment. (3) Internal Social – ‘Schlemiel.’ (4) External Social – ‘Schlemiel.’ (5) Biological – provocative and gentle stroking. (6) Existential – I am blameless.

优势：（1）内在心理——享受捣乱的快感。（2）外在心理——避免惩罚。（3）内在社会——“笨蛋”。（4）外在社会——“笨蛋”。（5）生理——挑逗而温柔的抚摸。（6）存在主义——我无辜。

4 · WHY DON’T YOU – YES BUT

4. 为什么你不——是的，但是

Thesis. ‘Why Don’t You – Yes But’ occupies a special place in game analysis, because it was the original stimulus for the concept of games. It was the first game to be dissected out of its social context, and since it is the oldest subject of game analysis, it is one of the best understood. It is also the game most commonly played at parties and in groups of all kinds, including psychotherapy groups. The following example will serve to illustrate its main characteristics:

论文指出，《你为什么不——是的，但是》在游戏分析中占据着特殊的地位，因为它是游戏概念的最初灵感来源。它是第一个被从社会语境中剥离出来的游戏，并且由于它是游戏分析中最古老的研究对象之一，因此也是最容易理解的游戏之一。它也是聚会和各种团体（包括心理治疗小组）中最常见的游戏。以下示例将阐明其主要特征：

White: ‘My husband always insists on doing our own repairs, and he never builds anything right.’

怀特说：“我丈夫总是坚持自己动手修理，但他从来没把什么东西修好过。”

Black: ‘Why doesn’t he take a course in carpentry?’

布莱克：“他为什么不去学木工呢？”

White: ‘Yes, but he doesn’t have time.’

怀特：“是的，但他没时间。”

Blue: ‘Why don’t you buy him some good tools?’

布鲁：“你为什么不给他买些好工具呢？”

White: ‘Yes, but he doesn’t know how to use them.’

怀特：“是的，但他不知道如何使用它们。”

Red: ‘Why don’t you have your building done by a carpenter?’

红：‘为什么不请木匠来盖房子呢？’

White: ‘Yes, but that would cost too much.’

怀特：“是的，但是那样成本太高了。”

Brown: ‘Why don’t you just accept what he does the way he does it?’

布朗：“你为什么不接受他做事的方式呢？”

White: ‘Yes, but the whole thing might fall down.’

怀特：“是的，但整个结构可能会倒塌。”

Such an exchange is typically followed by a silence. It is eventually broken by Green, who may say something like, ‘That’s men for you, aways trying to show how efficient they are.’

这样的对话之后通常会陷入沉默。最终，格林会打破沉默，说些类似这样的话：“男人就是这样，总是想方设法证明自己有多高效。”

YDYB can be played by any number. The agent presents a problem. The others start to present solutions, each beginning with ‘Why don’t you …?’ To each of these White objects with a ‘Yes, but …’ A good player can stand off the others indefinitely until they all give up, whereupon White wins. In many situations she might have to handle a dozen or more solutions to engineer the crestfallen silence which signifies her victory, and which leaves the field open for the next game in the above paradigm, Green switching into ‘PTA’, Delinquent Husband Type.

YDYB游戏可以由任意数量的玩家进行。玩家提出一个问题。其他玩家开始提出解决方案，每个方案都以“你为什么不……？”开头。白方对每个方案都提出反驳：“是的，但是……”。高手可以无限期地拖延时间，直到其他玩家全部放弃，此时白方获胜。在很多情况下，她可能需要应对十几个甚至更多的解决方案，才能营造出一种令人沮丧的沉默——这象征着她的胜利，也为下一局游戏打开了局面。在这种模式下，绿方可以切换到“PTA”（不良丈夫类型）角色。

Since the solutions are, with rare exceptions, rejected, it is apparent that this game must serve some ulterior purpose. YDYB is not played for its ostensible purpose (an Adult quest for information or solutions), but to reassure and gratify the Child. A bare transcript may sound Adult, but in the living tissue it can be observed that White presents herself as a Child inadequate to meet the situation; whereupon the others become transformed into sage Parents anxious to dispense their wisdom for her benefit.

既然这些解决方案几乎都被拒绝了，显然这个游戏必定另有所图。YDYB 的目的并非其表面所宣称的（成人寻求信息或解决方案），而是为了安抚和取悦孩子。单从文字描述来看，这或许显得成人化，但在实际游戏中，我们可以发现，怀特把自己塑造成一个无法应对当前情况的孩子；于是，其他人便化身为睿智的父母，急于将他们的智慧传授给她。

Figure 8. Why Don’t You – Yes But

图 8. 你为什么不——是的，但是

This is illustrated in Figure 8. The game can proceed because at the social level both stimulus and response are Adult to Adult, and at the psychological level they are also complementary, with Parent to Child stimulus (‘Why don’t you …’) eliciting Child to Parent response (‘Yes, but …’). The psychological level is usually unconscious on both sides, but the shifts in ego state (Adult to ‘inadequate’ Child on White’s part, Adult to ‘wise’ Parent by the others) can often be detected by an alert observer from changes in posture, muscular tone, voice and vocabulary.

如图 8 所示，游戏得以进行，是因为在社会层面，刺激和反应都是成人对成人的互动；在心理层面，二者也互为补充，父母对孩子的刺激（“你为什么不……”）引发孩子对父母的反应（“是的，但是……”）。心理层面的转变通常是双方无意识的，但敏锐的观察者往往能从姿势、肌肉张力、声音和词汇的变化中察觉到自我状态的转变（白人从成人转变为“不称职”的孩子，其他人则转变为“睿智”的父母）。

In order to illustrate the implications, it is instructive to follow through on the example given above.

为了说明其含义，不妨继续研究上面给出的例子。

Therapist: ‘Did anyone suggest anything you hadn’t thought of yourself?’

治疗师：“有没有人提出过你没想到的建议？”

White: ‘No, they didn’t. As a matter of fact, I’ve actually tried almost everything they suggested. I did buy my husband some tools, and he did take a course in carpentry.’

怀特：“不，他们没有。事实上，他们建议的我几乎都试过了。我给我丈夫买了一些工具，他也去上了木工课。”

Here White demonstrates two of the reasons why the proceedings should not be taken at face value. First, in the majority of cases White is as intelligent as anyone else in the company, and it is very unlikely that others will suggest any solution that she has not thought of herself. If someone does happen to come up with an original suggestion, White will accept it gratefully if she is playing fair; that is, her ‘inadequate’ Child will give way if anyone present has an idea ingenious enough to stimulate her Adult. But habitual YDYB players, such as White above, seldom play fair. On the other hand, a too ready acceptance of suggestions raises the question of whether the YDYB is not masking an underlying game of ‘Stupid’.

怀特在此阐述了不应轻信表面现象的两个原因。首先，在大多数情况下，怀特的智力与公司里的其他人不相上下，其他人不太可能提出她自己没想到的解决方案。如果有人真的提出了原创建议，只要怀特秉持公平原则，她就会欣然接受；也就是说，如果在场的任何人提出了足够巧妙的想法来激发她的“成人”思维，她“不称职”的“孩子”思维就会让步。但像怀特这样的惯常“装傻充愣”玩家很少会秉持公平原则。另一方面，过于轻易地接受建议也会引发疑问：这种“装傻充愣”的玩家是否在掩盖其潜在的“愚蠢”游戏策略？

The example given is particularly dramatic, because it clearly illustrates the second point. Even if White has actually tried some of the solutions presented, she will still object to them. The purpose of the game is not to get suggestions, but to reject them.

举的例子尤其引人注目，因为它清楚地说明了第二点。即使怀特确实尝试过一些提出的解决方案，她仍然会反对。这个游戏的目的不是为了获得建议，而是为了拒绝它们。

While almost anyone will play this game under proper circumstances because of its time-structuring value, careful study of individuals who particularly favour it reveals several interesting features. First, they characteristically can and will play either side of the game with equal facility. This switchability of roles is true of all games. Players may habitually prefer one role to another, but they are capable of trading, and they are willing to play any other role in the same game if for some reason that is indicated. (Compare, for example, the switch from Drinker to Rescuer in the game of ‘Alcoholic’.)

虽然几乎所有人都会在合适的条件下玩这个游戏，因为它具有时间管理价值，但仔细研究那些特别喜欢玩这个游戏的人，会发现一些有趣的特征。首先，他们通常能够并且愿意同样轻松地扮演游戏中的双方角色。这种角色转换能力在所有游戏中都存在。玩家可能习惯性地偏爱某个角色，但他们能够转换角色，并且如果出于某种原因需要，他们也愿意在同一局游戏中扮演任何其他角色。（例如，比较一下在“酗酒者”游戏中从“饮酒者”到“救援者”的转换。）

Second, in clinical practice it is found that people who favour YDYB belong to that class of patients who eventually request hypnosis or some sort of hypnotic injection as a method of speeding up their treatment. When they are playing the game, their object is to demonstrate that no one can give them an acceptable suggestion – that is, they will never surrender; whereas with the therapist, they request a procedure which will put them in a state of complete surrender. It is thus apparent that YDYB represents a social solution to a conflict about surrender.

其次，临床实践发现，那些偏好“YDYB”游戏的人，往往属于最终会要求接受催眠或某种催眠注射疗法以加速治疗的那一类患者。他们在玩这个游戏时，目的是为了证明没有人能给他们一个可以接受的暗示——也就是说，他们永远不会屈服；而面对治疗师时，他们却要求接受某种能让他们完全屈服的疗法。由此可见，“YDYB”代表了一种解决关于屈服冲突的社会方案。

Even more specifically, this game is common among people who have a fear of blushing, as the following therapeutic exchange demonstrates:

更具体地说，这种游戏在害怕脸红的人群中很常见，如下面的治疗性对话所示：

Therapist: ‘Why do you play “Why Don’t You – Yes But” if you know it’s a con?’

治疗师：“如果你知道‘Why Don’t You – Yes But’是骗局，为什么还要玩这个游戏呢？”

White: ‘If I’m talking to somebody I have to keep thinking of things to say. If I don’t, I’ll blush. Except in the dark. I can’t stand a lull. I know it, and my husband knows it, too. He’s always told me that.’

怀特说：“如果我和别人说话，我就得不停地想该说什么。不然我会脸红。除非是在黑暗中。我受不了冷场。我知道，我丈夫也知道。他总是这么跟我说。”

Therapist: ‘You mean if your Adult doesn’t keep busy, your Child takes the chance to pop up and make you feel embarrassed?’

治疗师：“你的意思是，如果你的成年人无所事事，你的孩子就会趁机冒出来，让你感到尴尬吗？”

White: ‘That’s it. So if I can keep making suggestions to somebody, or get him to make suggestions to me, then I’m all right, I’m protected. As long as I can keep my Adult in control, I can postpone the embarrassment.’

怀特：“就是这样。所以，如果我能继续给别人提建议，或者让他给我提建议，那我就没事了，我就安全了。只要我能让我的成年人控制我，我就能推迟尴尬的局面。”

Here White indicates clearly that she fears unstructured time. Her Child is prevented from advertising as long as the Adult can be kept busy in a social situation, and a game offers a suitable structure for Adult functioning. But the game must be suitably motivated in order to maintain her interest. Her choice of YDYB is influenced by the principle of economy: it yields the maximum internal and external advantages to her Child’s conflicts about physical passivity. She could play with equal zest either the shrewd Child who cannot be dominated or the sage Parent who tries to dominate the Child in someone else, but fails. Since the basic principle of YDYB is that no suggestion is ever accepted, the Parent is never successful. The motto of the game is: ‘Don’t get panicky, the Parent never succeeds.’

怀特在此明确指出她害怕无序的时间。只要成年人能在社交场合保持忙碌，她的孩子就不会到处宣扬自己的意愿，而游戏恰好为成年人的活动提供了一个合适的结构。但游戏必须有足够的动机才能保持她的兴趣。她选择“YDYB”（一种游戏）是出于经济原则：它能最大限度地满足孩子在身体被动性方面的冲突，并带来最大的内外益处。她既可以兴致勃勃地扮演那个精明强干、无法被支配的孩子，也可以扮演那个试图支配他人身上孩子特质却最终失败的睿智父母。由于“YDYB”的基本原则是任何建议都不会被接受，所以父母永远不会成功。这个游戏的座右铭是：“别慌，父母永远不会成功。”

In summary, then: while each move is amusing, so to speak, to White, and brings its own little pleasure in rejecting the suggestion, the real payoff is the silence or masked silence which ensues when all the others have racked their brains and grown tired of trying to think of acceptable solutions. This signifies to White and to them that she has won by demonstrating it is they who are inadequate. If the silence is not masked, it may persist for several minutes. In the paradigm, Green cut White’s triumph short because of her eagerness to start a game of her own, and that was what kept her from participating in White’s game. Later on in the session, White demonstrated her resentment against Green for having abridged her moment of victory.

总而言之：虽然白方每一步棋都颇为有趣，拒绝对方的提议也让她感到些许快感，但真正的收获在于当其他棋手绞尽脑汁、疲惫不堪地试图找到可接受的解决方案时，随之而来的沉默或隐隐的沉默。这向白方和他们表明，她已经通过证明他们的不足而获胜。如果这种沉默没有被掩饰，它可能会持续数分钟。在这个例子中，绿方因为急于开始自己的棋局而打断了白方的胜利，也正是因为如此，她才没有参与到白方的对局中。之后，白方对绿方打断她的胜利时刻表达了不满。

Another curious feature of YDYB is that the external and internal games are played exactly the same way, with the roles reversed. In the external form, the one observed clinically, White’s Child comes out to play the role of the inadequate help-seeker in a many-handed situation. In the internal form, the more intimate two-handed game played at home with her husband, her Parent comes out as the wise, efficient suggestion-giver. This reversal is usually secondary, however, since during the courtship she plays the helpless Child side, and only after the honeymoon is over does her bossy Parent begin to emerge into the open. There may have been slips as the wedding approached, but her fiancé will overlook these in his eagerness to settle down with his carefully chosen bride. If he does not overlook them, the engagement may be called off for ‘good reasons’, and White, sadder but no wiser, will resume her search for a suitable mate.

YDYB的另一个奇特之处在于，外部游戏和内部游戏的玩法完全相同，只是角色互换。在临床观察到的外部游戏中，怀特的“孩子”扮演着在多方博弈中无能为力的求助者角色。而在与丈夫在家中进行的更私密的“父母”游戏中，她则扮演着睿智高效的建议提供者角色。然而，这种角色互换通常是次要的，因为在恋爱期间，她扮演的是无助的“孩子”角色，只有在蜜月结束后，她强势的“父母”角色才会逐渐显露出来。婚礼临近时，她可能会出现一些小失误，但她的未婚夫会因为急于与精心挑选的新娘安定下来而忽略这些。如果他无法忽略这些失误，婚约可能会以“正当理由”取消，而怀特则会更加悲伤，却依然没有从中吸取教训，继续寻找合适的伴侣。

Antithesis. It is evident that those who respond to White’s first move, the presentation of her ‘problem’, are playing a form of ‘I’m Only Trying to Help You’ (ITHY). In fact YDYB is the inverse of ITHY. In ITHY there is one therapist and many clients; in YDYB one client and many ‘therapists’. The clinical antithesis to YDYB, therefore, is not to play ITHY. If the opening is of the form: ‘What do you do if …’ (WYDI), a suggested response is: ‘That is a difficult problem. What are you going to do about it?’ If it is of the form: ‘X didn’t work out properly’, the response then should be ‘That is too bad.’ Both of these are polite enough to leave White at a loss, or at least to elicit a crossed transaction, so that his frustration becomes manifest and can then be explored. In a therapy group it is good practice for susceptible patients to refrain from playing ITHY when invited. Then not only White, but the other members as well, can learn from anti-YDYB, which is merely the other side of anti-ITHY.

反面。显然，那些回应怀特第一步——提出她的“问题”——的人，都在玩一种“我只是想帮你”（ITHY）的游戏。事实上，“我只是想帮你”（YDYB）是ITHY的反面。在ITHY中，有一个治疗师和许多来访者；在YDYB中，有一个来访者和许多“治疗师”。因此，YDYB的临床反面就是不要玩ITHY。如果开场白是“如果……你会怎么做”（WYDI），建议的回应是：“这确实是个难题。你打算怎么做？”如果是“X没有成功”，那么回应应该是“那太遗憾了”。这两种回应都足够礼貌，足以让怀特感到不知所措，或者至少会引发一次交锋，从而使他的挫败感显露出来，以便进行深入探讨。在治疗小组中，对于易受影响的患者来说，当被邀请玩ITHY时，最好不要玩，这是一种良好的做法。这样一来，不仅是怀特，其他成员也可以从反YDYB中学习，而反YDYB只不过是反ITHY的另一面。

In a social situation, if the game is friendly and harmless, there is no reason not to participate. If it is an attempt to exploit professional knowledge, an antithetical move may be required; but in such situations this arouses resentment because of the exposure of White’s Child. The best policy under those circumstances is to flee from the opening move and look for a stimulating game of first-degree ‘Rapo’.

在社交场合，如果棋局友好无害，没有理由不参与。但如果对方试图利用你的专业知识，或许需要采取反制措施；然而，在这种情况下，反制会因为暴露白方的弱点而引起反感。此时，最佳策略是避开开局，寻找一盘刺激的初级“拉波”对局。

Relatives. ‘Why Don’t You – Yes But’ must be distinguished from its obverse, ‘Why Did You – No But’ (YDNB), in which it is the Parent who wins and the defensive Child who eventually retires in confusion, although again the bare transcript may sound factual, rational and Adult to Adult. YDNB is closely related to ‘Furthermore’.

亲属关系。“Why Don’t You – Yes But”必须与它的反面“Why Did You – No But”（YDNB）区分开来。在YDNB中，是父母一方获胜，而处于防御状态的孩子最终困惑地退缩，尽管单看文字描述可能听起来像是事实陈述、理性分析，并且是成人之间的交流。YDNB与“Furthermore”密切相关。

The reverse of YDYB at first resembles ‘Peasant’. Here White seduces the therapist into giving her suggestions which she immediately accepts, rather than rejects. Only after he is deeply involved does he perceive that White is turning on him. What looked like ‘Peasant’ ends up as a game of intellectual ‘Rapo’. The classical version of this is the switch from positive to negative transference in the course of orthodox psychoanalysis.

YDYB 的反向模式起初类似于“农民”模式。在这种模式下，白先生引诱治疗师向她提出建议，而治疗师立即接受而非拒绝。只有在治疗师深陷其中之后，他才意识到白先生正在对他进行反击。原本看似“农民”的模式最终演变成一场智力上的“拉波”游戏。这种模式的经典版本是正统精神分析过程中从正向移情到负向移情的转变。

YDYB may also be played in a second-degree hard form as ‘Do Me Something’. The patient refuses to do the housework, for example, and there is a game of YDYB every evening, when the husband returns home. But no matter what he says, she sullenly refuses to change her ways. In some cases the sullenness may be malignant and require careful psychiatric evaluation. The game aspect must be considered as well, however, since it raises the question of why the husband selected such a spouse, and how he contributes to maintaining the situation.

YDYB 也可能以更严重的形式出现，称为“做点什么”（Do Me Something）。例如，患者拒绝做家务，于是每天晚上丈夫回家后，她都会玩 YDYB 游戏。但无论丈夫说什么，她都闷闷不乐地拒绝改变。在某些情况下，这种闷闷不乐可能是恶性的，需要进行仔细的精神评估。然而，游戏本身也必须考虑在内，因为它引出了一个问题：丈夫为什么会选择这样的妻子，以及他是如何促成这种情况的？

ANALYSIS

分析

Thesis: See if you can present a solution I can’t find fault with.

论文题目：看看你能不能提出一个我无法挑出毛病的解决方案。

Aim: Reassurance.

目的：安抚人心。

Roles: Helpless person, Advisers.

角色：无助者、顾问。

Dynamics: Surrender conflict (oral).

动态：投降冲突（口头）。

Examples: (1) Yes, but I can’t do my homework now because … (2) Helpless wife.

例如：（1）是的，但我现在不能做作业，因为……（2）无助的妻子。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult: ‘What do you do if …’

成人：“如果……你会怎么办？”

Adult: ‘Why don’t you …’

成人：“你为什么不……”

Adult: ‘Yes, but …’

成人：“是的，但是……”

Psychological Paradigm: Parent-Child.

心理学范式：亲子关系。

Parent: ‘I can make you grateful for my help.’

家长：“我可以让你感激我的帮助。”

Child: ‘Go ahead and try.’

孩子：“你试试吧。”

Moves: (1) Problem-Solution. (2) Objection-Solution. (3) Objection-Disconcertion.

策略：（1）问题-解决方案。（2）反对意见-解决方案。（3）反对意见-消除疑虑。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – reassurance. (2) External Psychological – avoids surrender. (3) Internal Social –YDYB, Parental role. (4) External Social – YDYB, Child role. (5) Biological – rational discussion. (6) Existential – Everybody wants to dominate me.

优势：（1）内部心理因素——获得安慰。（2）外部心理因素——避免屈服。（3）内部社会因素——父母角色。（4）外部社会因素——孩子角色。（5）生物因素——理性讨论。（6）存在主义因素——每个人都想支配我。

REFERENCES

参考

1. von Chamisso, Adelbert, Peter Schlemiel, Calder, 1957.

1. Chamisso, Adelbert, Peter Schlemiel, Calder, 1957.

2. de Kock, Paul. One of the most popular works of this nineteenth-century librettist and novelist is A Good-Natured Fellow, about a man who gives away too much.

2. 德·科克，保罗。这位十九世纪的剧作家兼小说家最受欢迎的作品之一是《一个善良的人》，讲述了一个慷慨大方的人的故事。

#↩

9 · Sexual Games

9. 性游戏

S OME games are played to exploit or fight off sexual impulses These are all, in effect, perversions of the sexual instincts in which the satisfaction is displaced from the sexual act to the crucial transactions which constitute the payoff of the game. This cannot always be demonstrated convincingly, because such games are usually played in privacy, so that clinical information about them has to be obtained secondhand, and the informant’s bias cannot always be satisfactorily evaluated. The psychiatric conception of homosexuality, for example, is heavily skewed, because the more aggressive and successful ‘players’ do not often come for psychiatric treatment, and the available material mostly concerns the passive partners.

有些游戏是为了利用或抑制性冲动而进行的。实际上，这些都是性本能的扭曲，其满足感从性行为本身转移到了构成游戏回报的关键交易上。这一点并非总能得到令人信服的证实，因为这类游戏通常在私下进行，因此相关的临床信息只能通过二手资料获得，而信息提供者的偏见也难以得到令人满意的评估。例如，精神病学对同性恋的理解就存在严重的偏差，因为那些更积极主动、更成功的“玩家”往往不会寻求精神治疗，而现有的资料大多只涉及被动的一方。

The games included here are: ‘Let’s You and Him Fight’, ‘Perversion’, ‘Rapo’, ‘Stocking Game’ and ‘Uproar’. In most cases the agent is a woman. This is because the hard forms of sexual games in which the man is the agent verge on or constitute criminality, and properly belong in the Underworld section. On the other side, sexual games and marital games overlap, but the ones described here are readily available to unmarried people as well as to spouses.

这里收录的游戏包括：“你和他打架”、“变态”、“强奸”、“丝袜游戏”和“骚动”。大多数情况下，扮演者是女性。这是因为，如果男性是扮演者，那么那些更激烈的性游戏就接近或构成犯罪，应该归入“地下世界”类别。另一方面，性游戏和婚姻游戏有所重叠，但这里描述的游戏未婚人士和已婚人士都可以轻松参与。

1 · LET’S YOU AND HIM FIGHT

1. 让你和他打一架吧

Thesis. This may be a manoeuvre, a ritual or a game. In each case the psychology is essentially feminine. Because of its dramatic qualities, LYAHF is the basis of much of the world’s literature, both good and bad.

论点。这可能是一种策略、一种仪式或一场游戏。无论哪种情况，其心理本质上都是女性化的。由于其戏剧性的特质，《爱，你好 ...

1. As a manoeuvre it is romantic. The woman manoeuvres or challenges two men into fighting, with the implication or promise that she will surrender herself to the winner. After the competition is decided, she fulfils her bargain. This is an honest transaction, and the presumption is that she and her mate live happily ever after.

1. 作为一种策略，这很浪漫。女人挑拨两个男人之间的关系，让他们打架，并暗示或承诺她会把自己献给胜者。比赛结束后，她履行了约定。这是一笔诚实的交易，人们普遍认为她和她的伴侣从此过上了幸福的生活。

2. As a ritual, it tends to be tragic. Custom demands that the two men fight for her, even if she does not want them to, and even if she has already made her choice. If the wrong man wins, she must nevertheless take him. In this case it is society and not the woman who sets up LYAHF. If she is unwilling, the transaction is an honest one. If she is unwilling or disappointed, the outcome may offer her considerable scope for playing games, such as ‘Let’s Pull A Fast One on Joey’.

2. 作为一种仪式，它往往是悲剧性的。习俗要求两个男人为她争风吃醋，即使她并不情愿，即使她已经做出了选择。如果错的人赢了，她也必须接受他。在这种情况下，是社会而非女人自己设定了“求婚”的规则。如果她不情愿，这笔交易是公平的。如果她不情愿或失望，结果可能会给她提供很大的空间去玩弄权术，比如“我们来耍耍乔伊”。

3. As a game it is comic. The woman sets up the competition, and while the two men are fighting, she decamps with a third. The internal and external psychological advantages for her and her mate are derived from the position that honest competition is for suckers, and the comic story they have lived through forms the basis for the internal and external social advantages.

3. 作为一场游戏，它颇具喜剧效果。女人策划了这场竞争，趁着两个男人争斗不休时，她带着第三个男人溜走了。她和她的伴侣之所以能获得内在和外在的心理优势，是因为他们觉得公平竞争是傻瓜才会做的事；而他们经历的这场滑稽闹剧，则构成了他们内在和外在社会优势的基础。

2 · PERVERSION

2 · 变态

Thesis. Heterosexual perversions such as fetishism, sadism and masochism are symptomatic of a confused Child and are treated accordingly. Their transactional aspects, however, as manifested in actual sexual situations, can be dealt with by means of game analysis. This may lead to social control, so that even if the warped sexual impulses remain unchanged, they are neutralized as far as actual indulgence is concerned.

论点：诸如恋物癖、施虐癖和受虐癖等异性恋性变态行为是儿童期困惑的表现，应据此进行治疗。然而，这些行为在实际性行为中的交易层面，可以通过博弈分析来处理。这或许能起到社会控制的作用，即使扭曲的性冲动本身没有改变，也能在实际的放纵行为方面将其消除。

People who are suffering from mild sadistic or masochistic distortions tend to take a primitive kind of ‘Mental Health’ position. They feel that they are strongly sexed, and that prolonged abstinence will lead to serious consequences. Neither of these conclusions is necessarily true, but they form the basis for a game of ‘Wooden Leg’ with the plea: ‘What do you expect from someone as strongly sexed as I am?’

患有轻度施虐或受虐倾向的人往往会采取一种原始的“心理健康”观念。他们觉得自己性欲旺盛，长期禁欲会导致严重后果。这两种结论都不一定正确，但它们却构成了一种“木腿游戏”的基础，玩家会辩解说：“你还能指望像我这样性欲旺盛的人做什么呢？”

Antithesis. To extend ordinary courtesy to oneself and one’s partner; that is, to refrain from verbal or physical flagellation and confine oneself to more conventional forms of coitus. If White is a true pervert, this will lay bare the second element of the game, which is often clearly expressed in his dreams: that coitus itself has little interest for him, and that his real satisfaction is derived from the humiliating foreplay. This is something that he may not have cared to admit to himself. But it will now become clear to him that his complaint is: ‘After all this work, I have to have intercourse, yet!’ At this point the position is much more favourable for specific psychotherapy, and much of the pleading and evasiveness has been nullified. This applies to ordinary ‘sexual psychopaths’ as seen in practice, and not to malignant schizophrenic or criminal perversions, nor to those who confine their sexual activities to fantasy.

反义词。对自身和伴侣保持基本的礼貌；也就是说，避免言语或肢体上的鞭笞，并将性交方式限制在更传统的范围内。如果怀特真是个变态，这将揭示游戏的第二个要素，这要素常常在他的梦境中清晰地表达出来：性交本身对他来说毫无吸引力，他真正的满足感来源于屈辱的前戏。这或许是他不愿承认的。但现在他会明白，他的抱怨是：“费了这么大劲，我居然还要做爱！”此时，情况更有利于进行特定的心理治疗，许多恳求和回避的手段都已失效。这适用于实践中常见的“性变态者”，但不适用于恶性精神分裂症或犯罪性变态者，也不适用于那些将性活动局限于幻想的人。

The game of ‘Homosexuality’ has become elaborated into a subculture in many countries, just as it is ritualized in others. Many of the disabilities which result from homosexuality arise from making it into a game. The provocative behaviour which gives rise to ‘Cops and Robbers’, ‘Why Does This Always Happen to Us’, ‘It’s the Society We Live In’, ‘All Great Men Were’ and so forth, is often amenable to social control, which reduces the handicaps to a minimum. The ‘professional homosexual’ wastes a large amount of time and energy which could be applied to other ends. Analysis of his games may help him establish a quiet ménage which will leave him free to enjoy the benefits that bourgeois society offers, instead of devoting himself to playing his own variation of ‘Ain’t It Awful’.

在许多国家，“同性恋”游戏已经发展成一种亚文化，正如它在另一些国家被仪式化一样。许多由同性恋引起的弊端都源于将其游戏化。诸如“警察抓小偷”、“为什么这种事总是发生在我们身上”、“这就是我们生活的社会”、“所有伟人都是……”等等挑衅行为，往往容易受到社会控制，从而将弊端降至最低。“职业同性恋”浪费了大量本可以用于其他方面的时间和精力。分析他们的游戏或许能帮助他们建立一段平静的三人关系，使他们能够自由地享受资产阶级社会提供的种种好处，而不是沉迷于玩弄他们自己版本的“真糟糕”。

3 · RAPO

3. 报告

Thesis. This is a game played between a man and a woman which might more politely be called, in the milder forms at least, ‘Kiss Off’ or ‘Indignation’. It may be played with varying degrees of intensity.

论文。这是一种男女之间玩的游戏，至少在比较温和的版本中，或许可以更礼貌地称为“吻别”或“愤慨”。游戏的激烈程度可以有所不同。

1. First-Degree ‘Rapo’, or ‘Kiss Off’, is popular at social gatherings and consists essentially of mild flirtation. White signals that she is available and gets her pleasure from the man’s pursuit. As soon as he has committed himself, the game is over. If she is polite, she may say quite frankly ‘I appreciate your compliments and thank you very much’, and move on to the next conquest. If she is less generous, she may simply leave him. A skilful player can make this game last for a long time at a large social gathering by moving around frequently, so that the man has to carry out complicated manoeuvres in order to follow her without being too obvious.

一级“告别”（Rapo）或“拒绝”（Kiss Off）游戏在社交聚会中很流行，其本质是一种轻微的调情。白衣女子暗示自己单身，并享受男士的追求。一旦男士做出承诺，游戏就结束了。如果她比较礼貌，可能会坦率地说“谢谢你的赞美”，然后继续寻找下一个目标。如果她不那么慷慨，则可能直接离开。高手可以通过频繁走动，让男士为了不显得太过明显地跟随她，不得不进行复杂的操作，从而在大型社交聚会中长时间地玩这个游戏。

2. In Second-Degree ‘Rapo’, or ‘Indignation’, White gets only secondary satisfaction from Black’s advances. Her primary gratification comes from rejecting him, so that this game is also colloquially known as ‘Buzz Off, Buster’. She leads Black into a much more serious commitment than the mild flirtation of First-Degree ‘Rapo’ and enjoys watching his discomfiture when she repulses him. Black, of course, is not as helpless as he seems, and may have gone to considerable trouble to get himself involved. Usually he is playing some variation of ‘Kick Me’.

2. 在二级“拒绝”（Rapo）或“愤慨”（Indignation）游戏中，白方从黑方的追求中获得的满足感微乎其微。她的主要满足感来自于拒绝黑方，因此这种游戏也被俗称为“滚开，混蛋”（Buzz Off, Buster）。与一级“拒绝”游戏中的轻佻调情相比，白方会将黑方引向更为严肃的局面，并乐于看到黑方被拒绝时的窘迫。当然，黑方并非表面看起来那么无助，他可能费尽心思才让自己卷入其中。通常情况下，他是在玩某种“踢我”（Kick Me）的变体游戏。

3. Third-Degree ‘Rapo’ is a vicious game which ends in murder, suicide or the courtroom. Here White leads Black into compromising physical contact and then claims that he has made a criminal assault or has done her irreparable damage. In its most cynical form White may actually allow him to complete the sexual act so that she gets that enjoyment before confronting him. The confrontation may be immediate, as in the illegitimate cry of rape, or it may be long delayed, as in suicide or homicide following a prolonged love affair. If she chooses to play it as a criminal assault, she may have no difficulty in finding mercenary or morbidly interested allies, such as the press, the police, counsellors and relatives. Sometimes, however, these outsiders may cynically turn on her, so that she loses the initiative and becomes a tool in their games.

3. 三级“强奸”是一种恶性游戏，最终以谋杀、自杀或法庭审判告终。在这种游戏中，白方诱骗黑方进行有损隐私的身体接触，然后声称黑方犯有刑事袭击罪或对她造成了无法弥补的伤害。在最阴险的情况下，白方甚至可能允许黑方完成性行为，以便她在与黑方对质之前享受到快感。对质可能立即发生，例如诬告强奸；也可能拖延很久，例如在一段长期的婚外情后自杀或他杀。如果她选择以刑事袭击罪来应对，她可能很容易找到唯利是图或病态的盟友，例如媒体、警察、咨询师和亲戚。然而，有时这些局外人可能会阴险地反噬她，使她失去主动权，沦为他们游戏中的工具。

In some cases outsiders perform a different function. They force the game on an unwilling White because they want to play ‘Let’s You and Him Fight’. They put her in such a position that in order to save her face or her reputation she has to cry rape. This is particularly apt to happen with girls under the legal age of consent; they may be quite willing to continue a liaison, but because it is discovered or made an issue of, they feel constrained to turn the romance into a game of Third-Degree ‘Rapo’.

在某些情况下，外人扮演着不同的角色。他们强迫不情愿的白人女性参与游戏，因为他们想玩“你和他打一架”的游戏。他们把她逼到这种境地：为了保全颜面或名誉，她不得不谎称自己被强奸。这种情况尤其容易发生在未成年少女身上；她们可能很乐意继续这段关系，但一旦被发现或被公开，她们就被迫将这段恋情变成一场极其残酷的“强奸”游戏。

In one well-known situation, the wary Joseph refused to be inveigled into a game of ‘Rapo’, whereupon Potiphar’s wife made the classical switch into ‘Let’s You and Him Fight’, an excellent example of the way a hard player reacts to antithesis, and of the dangers that beset people who refuse to play games. These two games are combined in the well-known ‘Badger Game’, in which the woman seduces Black and then cries rape, at which point her husband takes charge and abuses Black for purposes of blackmail.

在一个著名的例子中，谨慎的约瑟拒绝被诱骗玩“拉波”（Rapo）游戏，于是波提乏的妻子立刻转而玩起了“你和他打一架”（Let’s You and Him Fight）游戏。这完美地展现了强硬玩家如何应对反面，以及拒绝参与游戏的人所面临的危险。这两个游戏在著名的“獾游戏”（Badger Game）中被结合了起来：女人引诱黑獾（Black），然后谎称被强奸，这时她的丈夫便会接管一切，并虐待黑獾以勒索钱财。

One of the most unfortunate and acute forms of Third-Degree ‘Rapo’ occurs relatively frequently between homosexual strangers, who in a matter of an hour or so may bring the game to a point of homicide. The cynical and criminal variations of this game contribute a large volume to sensational newspaper copy.

三级性侵中最不幸、最严重的形式之一，相对频繁地发生在同性恋陌生人之间，他们可能在短短一小时左右的时间里，将这种游戏演变成谋杀。这种游戏的种种冷酷无情和犯罪变种，为耸人听闻的报纸报道提供了大量素材。

The childhood prototype of ‘Rapo’ is the same as that of ‘Frigid Woman’, in which the little girl induces the boy to humiliate himself or get dirty and then sneers at him, as classically described by Maugham in Of Human Bondage and, as already noted, by Dickens in Great Expectations. This is Second Degree. A harder form, approaching Third Degree, may be played in tough neighbourhoods.

“拉波”这种游戏的童年原型与“冷漠女人”相同，都是小女孩诱使男孩出丑或弄脏自己，然后嘲笑他，毛姆在《人性的枷锁》中有经典描写，狄更斯在《远大前程》中也有提及（如前所述）。这是第二级。更严重的版本，接近第三级，可能会在治安较差的社区里上演。

Antithesis. The man’s ability to avoid becoming involved in this game or to keep it under control depends on his capacity to distinguish genuine expressions of feeling from moves in the game. If he is thus able to exert social control, he may obtain a great deal of pleasure from the mild flirtations of ‘Kiss Off’. On the other hand it is difficult to conceive of a safe antithesis for the Potiphar’s Wife manoeuvre, other than checking out before closing time with no forwarding address. In 1938 the writer met an ageing Joseph in Aleppo who had checked out of Constantinople thirty-two years previously, after one of the Sultan’s ladies had cornered him during a business visit to the Yildiz harem. He had to abandon his shop, but took time to pick up his hoard of gold francs, and had never returned.

反面。一个人能否避免卷入这场游戏或将其掌控在手，取决于他能否区分真情流露与游戏中的举动。如果他能够如此有效地控制社交，他或许能从“滚开”这种温和的调情中获得极大的乐趣。另一方面，除了在关门前退房且不留下任何新地址之外，很难想象还有什么安全的反面来应对“波提乏之妻”的策略。1938年，笔者在阿勒颇遇到了一位年迈的约瑟夫，他三十二年前离开君士坦丁堡。当时，他去耶尔德兹后宫做生意，被苏丹的一位侍女堵住了嘴。他不得不放弃自己的店铺，但还是抽出时间取回了他积攒的金法郎，从此再也没有回来。

Relatives. The male versions of ‘Rapo’ are notoriously found in commercial situations: ‘Casting Couch’ (and then she didn’t get the part) and ‘Cuddle Up’ (and then she got fired).

亲戚们。男性版的“Rapo”经常出现在商业广告中，例如“Casting Couch”（结果她没得到角色）和“Cuddle Up”（结果她被解雇了）。

ANALYSIS

分析

The following analysis refers to Third-Degree ‘Rapo’ because there the elements of the game are more dramatically illustrated.

以下分析指的是三级“拉波”，因为那里的游戏元素得到了更生动的展现。

Aim: Malicious revenge.

目的：恶意报复。

Roles: Seductress , Wolf.

角色：魅惑者，狼。

Dynamics (Third Degree): Penis envy, oral violence. ‘Kiss Off’ is phallic, while ‘Indignation’ has strong anal elements.

动态（三级）：阴茎嫉妒，口交暴力。“Kiss Off”是阳具象征，而“Indignation”则有强烈的肛门元素。

Examples: (1) I’ll tell on you, you dirty little boy. (2) Wronged woman.

例如：（1）我会告发你，你这个肮脏的小男孩。（2）受委屈的女人。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult (male): ‘I’m sorry if I went further than you intended me to.’

成年男性：“如果我做得太过分，我很抱歉。”

Adult (female): ‘You have violated me and must pay the full penalty.’

成年女性：“你侵犯了我，必须承担全部惩罚。”

Psychological Paradigm: Child-Child.

心理学范式：儿童-儿童。

Child (male): ‘See how irresistible I am.’

男孩（男）：“看看我多么令人无法抗拒。”

Child (female): ‘Now I’ve got you, you son of a bitch.’

女童：“现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋。”

Moves: (1) Female: seduction; Male: counter-seduction. (2) Female: surrender; Male: victory. (3) Female: confrontation; Male: collapse.

策略：（1）女方：诱惑；男方：反诱惑。（2）女方：投降；男方：胜利。（3）女方：对抗；男方：崩溃。

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – expression of hatred and projection of guilt. (2) External Psychological – avoidance of emotional sexual intimacy. (3) Internal Social – ‘Now I’ve Got You, You Son of a Bitch’. (4) External Social – ‘Ain’t It Awful’, ‘Courtroom’, ‘Let’s You and Him Fight’. (5) Biological – sexual and belligerent exchanges. (6) Existential – I am blameless.

优势：（1）内在心理层面——表达仇恨和投射罪恶感。（2）外在心理层面——回避情感上的性亲密。（3）内在社会层面——“现在我抓到你了，你这个混蛋！”。（4）外在社会层面——“太糟糕了”、“法庭”、“让你和他打一架”。（5）生理层面——性欲和好斗的交流。（6）存在层面——我是无辜的。

4 · THE STOCKING GAME

4. 长袜游戏

Thesis. This is a game of the ‘Rapo’ family; in it the most obvious characteristic is the exhibitionism, which is hysterical in nature. A woman comes into a strange group and after a very short time raises her leg, exposing herself in a provocative way, and remarks, ‘Oh my, I have a run in my stocking.’ This is calculated to arouse the men sexually and to make the other women angry. Any confrontation of White is met, of course, with protestations of innocence or counter-accusations, hence the resemblance to classical ‘Rapo’. What is significant is White’s lack of adaptation. She seldom waits to find out what kind of people she is dealing with or how to time her manoeuvre. Hence it stands out as inappropriate and affects her relationships with her associates. In spite of some superficial ‘sophistication’, she fails to understand what happens to her in life because her judgement of human nature is too cynical. The aim is to prove that other people have lascivious minds, and her Adult is conned by her Child and her Parent (usually a lascivious mother) into ignoring both her own provocativeness and the good sense of many of the people she meets. Thus the game tends to be self-destructive.

论文：这是一种“拉波”式的游戏；其最显著的特征是歇斯底里的暴露癖。一个女人进入一群陌生人中，没过多久就抬起腿，以一种挑衅的方式暴露自己，并说道：“哎呀，我的丝袜破了。” 这样做是为了挑逗男人的性欲，并激怒其他女人。当然，任何对怀特的质疑都会遭到辩解或反驳，因此与经典的“拉波”游戏相似。值得注意的是怀特缺乏适应能力。她很少会先弄清楚自己面对的是什么样的人，或者如何把握时机。因此，她的行为显得很不合时宜，并影响了她与同伴的关系。尽管表面上有些“世故”，但她无法理解自己在生活中遭遇的一切，因为她对人性的判断过于愤世嫉俗。其目的是为了证明其他人也心怀淫念，而她的成年角色则被她的幼年角色和父母角色（通常是淫荡的母亲）所蒙蔽，从而忽略了自身的挑衅行为以及她所遇到的许多人的理智。因此，这种游戏往往会走向自我毁灭。

This is probably a phallic variant of a game whose content depends on the underlying disturbance. An ‘oral’ variant may be exhibited by women with deeper pathology and well-developed breasts. Such women often sit with their hands behind their heads so as to thrust their breasts forward; they may draw additional attention to them by remarking about their size or some pathology such as an operation or a lump. Some types of squirming probably constitute an anal variant. The implication of this game is that the woman is sexually available. Thus it may be played in a more symbolic form by bereaved women who ‘exhibit’ their widowhood insincerely.

这或许是一种性暗示游戏，其内容取决于潜在的心理障碍。“口交”变体可能出现在病理较重、乳房发育良好的女性身上。这类女性常常双手抱头，使乳房向前挺起；她们可能会通过谈论乳房的大小或某些病理情况（例如手术或肿块）来吸引更多人的注意。某些扭动动作可能构成肛门变体。这种游戏的隐含意义是暗示女性处于性开放状态。因此，丧夫的女性可能会以更具象征意义的形式玩这种游戏，虚伪地“展示”她们的寡妇身份。

Antithesis. Along with the poor adaptation, these women show little tolerance for antithesis. If the game is ignored or countered by a sophisticated therapy group, for example, they may not return. Antithesis must be carefully distinguished in this game from reprisal, since the latter signifies that White has won. Women are more skilful at counter-moves in ‘Stocking Game’ than men, who indeed have little incentive to break up this game. Antithesis, therefore, is best left to the discretion of the other women present.

对立。除了适应能力差之外，这些女性对对立的容忍度也很低。例如，如果游戏被忽略或被一个老练的治疗小组反制，她们可能就不会再来了。在这个游戏中，对立必须与报复区分开来，因为后者意味着白方获胜。在“囤积游戏”中，女性比男性更擅长反制，而男性也确实没有多少动力去破坏这个游戏。因此，对立最好由在场的其他女性自行决定。

5 · UPROAR

5 · 骚动

Thesis. The classical game is played between domineering fathers and teen-age daughters, where there is a sexually inhibited mother. Father comes home from work and finds fault with daughter, who answers impudently, or daughter may make the first move by being impudent, whereupon father finds fault. Their voices rise, and the clash becomes more acute. The outcome depends on who has the initiative. There are three possibilities: (a) father retires to his bedroom and slams the door; (b) daughter retires to her bedroom and slams the door; (c) both retire to their respective bedrooms and slam the doors. In any case, the end of a game of ‘Uproar’ is marked by a slamming door. ‘Uproar’ offers a distressing but effective solution to the sexual problems that arise between fathers and teen-age daughters in certain households. Often they can only live in the same house together if they are angry at each other, and the slamming doors emphasize for each of them the fact that they have separate bedrooms.

论点：经典的“争吵游戏”发生在专横的父亲和青春期女儿之间，母亲则性压抑。父亲下班回家后会指责女儿，女儿则以无礼回应；或者女儿也可能先出言不逊，父亲随即指责。双方的音量逐渐增大，冲突也愈发激烈。最终结果取决于谁先发制人。有三种可能：（a）父亲回到卧室摔门而去；（b）女儿回到卧室摔门而去；（c）双方都回到各自的卧室摔门而去。无论如何，“争吵游戏”的结束都以摔门告终。“争吵游戏”为某些家庭中父亲和青春期女儿之间出现的性问题提供了一种令人痛苦但却有效的解决方案。他们往往只有在彼此生气的时候才会住在一起，而砰砰的关门声也向他们每个人强调了他们各自拥有独立卧室的事实。

In degenerate households this game may be played in a sinister and repellent form in which father waits up for daughter whenever she goes out on a date, and examines her and her clothing carefully on her return to make sure that she has not had intercourse. The slightest suspicious circumstance may give rise to the most violent altercation, which may end with the daughter being expelled from the house in the middle of the night. In the long run nature will take its course – if not that night then the next, or the one after. Then the father’s suspicions are ‘justified’, as he makes plain to the mother, who has stood by ‘helplessly’ while all this went on.

在一些堕落的家庭里，这种游戏可能会以一种阴险可憎的形式上演：父亲会在女儿每次外出约会后守候在她家，并在她回来后仔细检查她和她的衣着，以确保她没有发生性关系。哪怕是最轻微的可疑情况都可能引发激烈的争吵，最终导致女儿在半夜被赶出家门。从长远来看，自然规律终会发挥作用——如果不是当晚，那就是第二天，或者下下天。然后，父亲的怀疑就会“得到证实”，他会向在一旁“无助”地看着这一切发生的母亲解释清楚。

In general, however, ‘Uproar’ may be played between any two people who are trying to avoid sexual intimacy. For example, it is a common terminal phase of ‘Frigid Woman’. It is relatively rare between teen-age boys and their female relatives, because it is easier for teen-age boys to escape from the house in the evening than for other members of the family. At an earlier age brothers and sisters can set up effective barriers and partial satisfactions through physical combat, a pattern which has various motivations at different ages, and which in America is a semi-ritualistic form of ‘Uproar’ sanctioned by television, pedagogic and pediatric authorities. In upper-class England it is (or was) considered bad form, and the corresponding energies are channelled into the well-regulated ‘Uproar’ of the playing fields.

然而，一般来说，“争吵”这种行为可能发生在任何试图避免性亲密关系的两个人之间。例如，它是“冷淡女人”游戏的一个常见终末阶段。青少年男孩和他们的女性亲属之间发生这种行为相对较少，因为青少年男孩比其他家庭成员更容易在晚上离家出走。在更小的年纪，兄弟姐妹可以通过肢体冲突来设置有效的障碍并获得部分满足感，这种模式在不同年龄段有着不同的动机，在美国，这是一种半仪式化的“争吵”形式，并得到了电视、教育和儿科权威机构的认可。在英国上流社会，这种行为（或曾经）被认为是不雅的，相应的能量会被引导到运动场上规范的“争吵”中。

Antithesis. The game is not as distasteful to the father as he might like to think, and it is generally the daughter who makes the antithetical move through an early, often premature or forced marriage. If it is psychologically possible, the mother can make the antithetical move by relinquishing her relative or absolute frigidity. The game may subside if the father finds an outside sexual interest, but that may lead to other complications. In the case of married couples, the antitheses are the same as for ‘Frigid Woman’ or ‘Frigid Man’.

反面。这种游戏对父亲来说可能并不像他想象的那样令人厌恶，通常是女儿通过早婚（往往是过早的婚姻或被迫的婚姻）来采取反面行动。如果心理上可行，母亲也可以通过放弃相对或绝对的性冷淡来采取反面行动。如果父亲找到了婚外情，这种游戏可能会逐渐平息，但这可能会引发其他问题。对于已婚夫妇来说，反面与“性冷淡的女人”或“性冷淡的男人”的情况相同。

Under appropriate circumstances ‘Uproar’ leads quite naturally into ‘Courtroom’.

在适当的情况下，“骚动”很自然地过渡到“法庭”。

#↩

10 · Underworld Games

10 · 地下世界游戏

W ITH the infiltration of the ‘helping’ professions into the courts, probation departments and correctional facilities, and with the increasing sophistication of criminologists and law enforcement officers, those concerned should be aware of the more common games prevalent in the underworld, both in prison and out of it. These include ‘Cops and Robbers’, ‘How Do You Get Out of Here’ and ‘Let’s Pull a Fast One on Joey’.

随着“助人”行业的从业人员渗透到法院、缓刑部门和惩教机构，以及犯罪学家和执法人员的技能日益精湛，相关人士应该意识到黑社会（无论是在监狱内外）普遍存在的一些常见伎俩。这些伎俩包括“警察抓小偷”、“如何才能离开这里”和“我们来捉弄一下乔伊”。

1 · COPS AND ROBBERS

1. 警察与强盗

Thesis. Because many criminals are cop-haters, they seem to get as much satisfaction from outwitting the police as from their criminal gains, often more. Their crimes, at the Adult level, are games played for the material rewards, the take; but at the Child level it is the thrill of the chase: the getaway and the cool-off.

论点：由于许多罪犯憎恨警察，他们似乎从智胜警察中获得的满足感与犯罪所得不相上下，甚至往往更高。成年人的犯罪是为了物质利益，为了赃物；而儿童的犯罪则是为了追逐的刺激：逃脱和冷静下来的感觉。

Curiously enough, the childhood prototype of ‘Cops and Robbers’ is not cops and robbers but hide-and-seek, in which the essential element is the chagrin at being found. Younger children readily betray this. If father finds them too easily, the chagrin is there without much fun. But father, if he is a good player, knows what to do: he holds off, whereupon the little boy gives him a clue by calling out, dropping something or banging. Thus he forces father to find him, but still shows chagrin; this time he has had more fun because of the increased suspense. If father gives up, the boy usually feels disappointed rather than victorious. Since the fun of being hidden was there, evidently that is not where the trouble lies. What he is disappointed about is not being caught. When his turn comes to hide, father knows he is not supposed to outwit the little boy for very long, just long enough to make it fun; and he is wise enough to look chagrined when he is caught. It soon becomes clear that being found is the necessary payoff.

有趣的是，儿童时期“警察抓小偷”游戏的原型并非真正的警察抓小偷，而是捉迷藏，其中最关键的要素是被发现时的懊恼。年幼的孩子很容易流露出这种懊恼。如果父亲轻易就找到了他们，孩子只会感到懊恼，而无趣可言。但如果父亲玩得好，他知道该怎么做：他会故意拖延时间，让小男孩通过喊叫、掉落物品或敲打等方式给出线索。这样，小男孩就不得不费力寻找，但仍然会表现出懊恼；这一次，由于悬念的增加，小男孩反而获得了更多乐趣。如果父亲放弃，小男孩通常会感到失望而不是胜利。既然躲藏的乐趣已经存在，显然问题不在于此。他失望的不是被抓住。轮到父亲躲藏时，父亲知道自己不应该长时间智胜小男孩，只需足够让游戏充满乐趣即可；而且他足够聪明，在被抓住时会表现出懊恼的神情。很快人们就明白，被找到是必要的回报。

Hence hide-and-seek is not a mere pastime but a true game. At the social level it is a battle of wits, and is most satisfying when the Adult of each player does his best; at the psychological level, however, it is set up like compulsive gambling, in which White’s Adult has to lose in order for his Child to win. Not being caught is actually the antithesis. Among older children, one who finds an insoluble hiding place is regarded as not being a good sport, since he has spoiled the game. He has eliminated the Child element and turned the whole thing into an Adult procedure. He is no longer playing for fun. He is in the same class as the owner of a casino, or some professional criminals, who are really out for money rather than sport.

因此，捉迷藏并非简单的消遣，而是一种真正的游戏。在社交层面，它是一场智力较量，当双方的“成人”都竭尽全力时，游戏最为精彩；然而，在心理层面，它却像是一种强迫性赌博，白方的“成人”必须输，其“儿童”才能赢。不被抓住恰恰是其反面。在年龄较大的孩子中，如果有人找到了一个无法破解的藏身之处，就会被认为缺乏体育精神，因为他破坏了游戏。他抹杀了“儿童”的元素，将整个游戏变成了“成人”的游戏。他不再是为了乐趣而玩，而是和赌场老板或某些职业罪犯一样，他们真正追求的是金钱而非游戏本身。

There seem to be two distinctive types of habitual criminals: those who are in crime primarily for profit, and those who are in it primarily for the game – with a large group in between who can handle it either way. The ‘compulsive winner’, the big moneymaker whose Child really does not want to be caught, rarely is, according to reports; he is an untouchable, for whom the fix is always in. The ‘compulsive loser’, on the other hand, who is playing ‘Cops and Robbers’ (C & R), seldom does very well financially. The exceptions to this often seem to be due to luck rather than skill; in the long run even the lucky ones usually end up as their Child requires, squawking rather than riding high.

惯犯似乎可以分为两大类：一类主要为了牟利而犯罪，另一类则纯粹为了享受犯罪的乐趣——当然，还有一大批人介于两者之间，他们两种目的都能接受。“惯性赢家”，也就是那些赚得盆满钵满、其子女极力避免被抓的罪犯，据报道很少会落网；他们是“法外之徒”，对他们来说，一切都已安排妥当。而“惯性输家”，就像玩“警察抓小偷”游戏一样，很少能赚到多少钱。少数例外往往是运气而非技巧；从长远来看，即使是那些幸运儿，最终也往往如其子女所愿，怨天尤人，而非风光无限。

The C & R player, with whom we are concerned here, in some ways resembles the Alcoholic. He can shift roles from Robber to Cop and from Cop to Robber. In some cases he may play the Parental Cop during the day and the Child Robber after dark. There is a Cop in many Robbers, and a Robber in many Cops. If the criminal ‘reforms’, he may play the role of Rescuer, becoming a social worker or a mission worker; but the Rescuer is far less important in this game than in ‘Alcoholic’. Ordinarily, however, the player’s role as Robber is his destiny, and each has his own modus operandi for getting caught. He may make it tough or easy for the Cops.

我们这里讨论的“C&R”玩家，在某些方面与“酗酒者”相似。他可以随时在劫匪和警察之间切换角色。有时，他白天扮演家长警察的角色，晚上则化身为儿童劫匪。许多劫匪身上都有警察的影子，许多警察身上也有劫匪的影子。如果罪犯“改过自新”，他可能会扮演“拯救者”的角色，成为社工或慈善工作者；但在这个游戏中，“拯救者”的重要性远不及“酗酒者”游戏中的角色。通常情况下，玩家扮演劫匪是他的宿命，每个人都有自己独特的落网方式。他可能会让警察抓捕他变得困难重重，也可能让他轻而易举。

The situation is similar with gamblers. At the social or sociological level a ‘professional’ gambler is one whose chief interest in life is gambling. But at the psychological level there are two different kinds of people who are professional gamblers. There are those who spend their time gaming, i.e., playing with Fate, in whom the strength of the Adult’s desire to win is exceeded only by the strength of the Child’s need to lose. Then there are those who run gambling houses and actually do earn a living, usually a very good one, by providing opportunities for gamesters to play; they themselves are not playing, and try to avoid playing, although occasionally under certain conditions they will indulge themselves and enjoy it, just as a straight criminal may occasionally play a game of C & R.

赌徒的情况也类似。从社会学层面来看，“职业”赌徒是指那些将赌博作为人生主要兴趣的人。但从心理层面来看，职业赌徒可以分为两种。一种是把时间花在赌博上，也就是与命运博弈，他们内心深处渴望胜利的欲望，仅次于渴望失败的孩童本能。另一种是经营赌场并以此为生的人，他们通常收入颇丰，为赌徒提供赌博的机会；他们自己并不参与赌博，并且尽量避免参与，尽管在某些情况下，他们也会偶尔放纵自己，享受赌博的乐趣，就像一个惯犯偶尔也会玩玩“C&R”（一种纸牌游戏）一样。

This throws light on why sociological and psychological studies of criminals have been generally ambiguous and unproductive: they are dealing with two different kinds of people who cannot be adequately differentiated in the ordinary theoretical or empirical frameworks. The same is true in studying gamblers. Transactional and game analyses offer an immediate solution for this. They remove the ambiguity by distinguishing transactionally, below the social level, between ‘players’ and ‘straight professionals’.
