亲戚们。“骑士游戏”是一种游戏，必须将其与正式求爱过程中的种种行为和程序区分开来，后者只是没有其他目的的简单交易。女性版的“骑士游戏”可以方便地称为“花言巧语”，因为它常常是风度翩翩的爱尔兰女士在晚年玩的游戏。

PARTIAL ANALYSIS

部分分析

Aim: Mutual admiration.

目的：相互欣赏。

Roles: Poet, Appreciative subject.

角色：诗人，欣赏者。

Social Paradigm: Adult-Adult.

社会范式：成人-成人。

Adult (male): ‘See how good I can make you feel.’

成年男性：“看看我能让你有多么舒服。”

Adult (female): ‘My, but you make me feel good.’

成年女性：“哎呀，你让我感觉真好。”

Psychological Paradigm:

心理学范式：

Child (male): ‘See what phrases I can create.’

儿童（男）：“看看我能创造出什么短语。”

Child (female): ‘My, but you’re creative.’

女童：“哇，你真有创意。”

Advantages: (1) Internal Psychological – creativity and reassurance of attractiveness. (2) External Psychological – avoids rejection for unnecessary sexual advances. (3) Internal Social – ‘Cavalier’. (4) External Social – these may be resigned. (5) Biological – mutual stroking. (6) Existential – I can live gracefully.

优势：（1）内在心理层面——创造力和吸引力的提升。（2）外在心理层面——避免因不必要的性骚扰而被拒绝。（3）内在社交层面——“潇洒不羁”。（4）外在社交层面——这些都可以接受。（5）生理层面——相互爱抚。（6）存在层面——我可以优雅地生活。

3 · HAPPY TO HELP

3. 乐于助人

Thesis. White is consistently helpful to other people, with some ulterior motive. He may be doing penance for past wickedness, covering up for present wickedness, making friends in order to exploit them later or seeking prestige. But whoever questions his motives must also give him credit for his actions. After all, people can cover up for past wickedness by becoming more wicked, exploit people by fear rather than generosity and seek prestige for evil ways instead of good ones. Some philanthropists are more interested in competition than in benevolence: ‘I gave more money (works of art, acres of land) than you did.’ Again, if their motives are questioned, they must nevertheless be given credit for competing in a constructive way, since there are so many people who compete destructively. Most people (or peoples) who play ‘Happy to Help’ have both friends and enemies, both perhaps justified in their feelings. Their enemies attack their motives and minimize their actions, while their friends are grateful for their actions and minimize their motives. Therefore so-called ‘objective’ discussions of this game are practically nonexistent. People who claim to be neutral soon show which side they are neutral on.

论点：怀特先生一贯乐于助人，但背后可能另有图谋。他或许是在为过去的罪恶赎罪，掩盖当下的罪恶，结交朋友以便日后利用，或是追求声望。然而，无论谁质疑他的动机，都必须承认他行为的合理性。毕竟，人们可以通过变得更加邪恶来掩盖过去的罪恶，通过恐惧而非慷慨来剥削他人，并通过作恶而非行善来追求声望。有些慈善家更热衷于竞争而非行善：“我捐的钱（艺术品、土地）比你多。” 同样，即便他们的动机受到质疑，也必须承认他们以建设性的方式参与竞争，因为有太多人以破坏性的方式进行竞争。大多数乐于助人的人（或群体）都有朋友和敌人，双方的感受或许都有道理。敌人会攻击他们的动机，贬低他们的行为；而朋友则会感激他们的行为，并淡化他们的动机。因此，所谓对这款游戏的“客观”讨论实际上并不存在。那些声称自己保持中立的人很快就会暴露他们究竟站在哪一边。

This game, as an exploitative manoeuvre, is the basis for a large proportion of ‘public relations’ in America. But the customers are glad to become involved, and it is perhaps the most pleasant and constructive of the commercial games. In another connection, one of its most reprehensible forms is a three-handed family game in which the mother and father compete for the affection of their offspring. But even here, it should be noted, the choice of ‘Happy to Help’ removes some of the discredit, since there are so many unpleasant ways of competing available – for example, ‘Mummy is sicker than daddy,’ or ‘Why do you love him more than you love me?’

这种游戏，作为一种剥削手段，是美国很大一部分“公共关系”的基础。但顾客乐于参与其中，它或许是商业游戏中最为愉快且富有建设性的一种。另一方面，它最令人反感的形式之一是三人家庭游戏，父母在其中争夺子女的爱。但即便如此，值得注意的是，“乐于助人”这一选项也减轻了部分负面影响，因为还有许多令人不快的竞争方式可供选择——例如，“妈妈比爸爸病得重”或“你为什么更爱他而不是我？”

4 · HOMELY SAGE

4 · 家常鼠尾草

Thesis. This is properly a script rather than a game, but it has gamelike aspects. A well-educated and sophisticated man learns as much as he can about all sorts of things besides his own business. When he reaches retirement age, he moves from the big city where he held a responsible position to a small town. There it soon becomes known that people can go to him with their problems of whatever kind, from a knock in the engine to a senile relative, and that he will help them himself if he is competent or else refer them to qualified experts. Thus he soon finds his place in his new environment as a ‘Homely Sage’, making no pretences, but always willing to listen. In its best form it is played by people who have taken the trouble to go to a psychiatrist to examine their motives, and to learn what errors to avoid before setting themselves up in this role.

主题：与其说这是一场游戏，不如说这是一部剧本，但它确实包含一些游戏元素。一位受过良好教育、见多识广的男士，除了自己的职业之外，尽可能地学习各种知识。退休后，他从担任要职的大城市搬到了一个小镇。很快，人们便知道无论遇到什么问题，从汽车引擎故障到老年痴呆的亲戚，都可以来找他。如果他有能力，他会亲自帮忙；否则，他会将他们转介给合格的专家。就这样，他很快在新环境中找到了自己的位置，成为了一位“居家智者”，他从不摆架子，总是乐于倾听。最好的演绎方式是，由那些认真咨询过心理医生，审视过自己的动机，并在扮演这个角色之前了解应该避免哪些错误的人来演绎。

5 · THEY’LL BE GLAD THEY KNEW ME

5. 他们会很高兴认识我

Thesis. This is a more worthy variant of ‘I’ll Show Them’. There are two forms of Til Show Them’. In the destructive form White ‘shows them’ by inflicting damage on them. Thus he may manoeuvre himself into a superior position, not for the prestige or the material rewards but because it gives him power to exercise his spite. In the constructive form White works hard and exerts every effort to gain prestige, not for the sake of craftsmanship or legitimate accomplishment (although those may play a secondary role), nor to inflict direct damage on his enemies, but so that they will be eaten with envy and with regret for not having treated him better.

论点：这是“我要让他们看看”的一种更有价值的变体。“我要让他们看看”有两种形式。在破坏性形式中，怀特通过伤害他们来“让他们看看”。这样，他就能巧妙地让自己处于优势地位，并非为了声望或物质回报，而是因为这种地位赋予他发泄怨恨的力量。在建设性形式中，怀特努力工作，竭尽全力去赢得声望，并非为了技艺或正当的成就（尽管这些可能起到次要作用），也不是为了直接伤害他的敌人，而是为了让他们嫉妒得发狂，后悔当初没有善待他。

In ‘They’ll Be Glad They Knew Me’, White is working not against but for the interests of his former associates. He wants to show them that they were justified in treating him with friendliness and respect and to demonstrate to them, for their own gratification, that their judgement was sound. In order for him to have a secure win in this game, his means as well as his ends must be honourable, and that is its superiority over ‘I’ll Show Them’. Both ‘I’ll Show Them’ and ‘They’ll Be Glad’ can be merely secondary advantages of success, rather than games. They become games when White is more interested in the effects on his enemies or friends than he is in the success itself.

在《他们会庆幸认识我》中，怀特并非与他以前的同伴作对，而是为他们谋利。他想向他们证明，他们之前对他友好和尊重是理所应当的，并为了让他们自己感到欣慰，也想证明他们的判断是正确的。为了确保他在这场博弈中获胜，他的手段和目的都必须是高尚的，这正是它优于《我会让他们见识见识》的原因。《我会让他们见识见识》和《他们会庆幸认识我》都可能仅仅是成功的次要好处，而非博弈本身。只有当怀特更关注对敌人或朋友的影响，而非成功本身时，它们才真正变成了博弈。

#↩

PART THREE

第三部分

#↩

BEYOND GAMES

超越游戏

#↩

13 · The Significance of Games

13. 游戏的意义

1. G AMES are passed on from generation to generation. The favoured game of any individual can be traced back to his parents and grandparents, and forward to his children; they in turn, unless there is a successful intervention, will teach them to his grandchildren. Thus game analysis takes place in a grand historical matrix, demonstrably extending back as far as one hundred years and reliably projected into the future for at least fifty years. Breaking this chain which involves five or more generations may have geometrically progressive effects. There are many living individuals who have more than two hundred descendants. Games may be diluted or altered from one generation to another, but there seems to be a strong tendency to inbreed with people who play a game of the same family, if not of the same genus. That is the historical significance of games.

1. 游戏代代相传。任何人喜爱的游戏都可以追溯到他的父母和祖父母，并传给他的孩子；而他们，除非有人成功干预，否则又会将游戏传给他们的孙辈。因此，游戏分析是在一个宏大的历史框架中进行的，其历史可以追溯到一百年前，并能可靠地预测未来至少五十年。打破这条涉及五代或更多代的链条可能会产生几何级数递增的影响。许多在世的人拥有超过两百个后代。游戏可能会在一代又一代之间被稀释或改变，但似乎存在一种强烈的近亲繁殖倾向，即玩同一家族（如果不是同一类别）游戏的人之间会进行近亲繁殖。这就是游戏的历史意义。

2. ‘Raising’ children is primarily a matter of teaching them what games to play. Different cultures and different social classes favour different types of games, and various tribes and families favour different variations of these. That is the cultural significance of games.

2. “养育”孩子主要就是教他们玩什么游戏。不同的文化和社会阶层偏爱不同类型的游戏，不同的部落和家庭也偏爱这些游戏的不同变体。这就是游戏的文化意义。

3. Games are sandwiched, as it were, between pastimes and intimacy. Pastimes grow boring with repetition, as do promotional cocktail parties. Intimacy requires stringent circumspection, and is discriminated against by Parent, Adult and Child. Society frowns upon candidness, except in privacy; good sense knows that it can always be abused; and the Child fears it because of the unmasking which it involves. Hence in order to get away from the ennui of pastimes without exposing themselves to the dangers of intimacy, most people compromise for games when they are available, and these fill the major part of the more interesting hours of social intercourse. That is the social significance of games.

3. 游戏仿佛夹在消遣和亲密关系之间。消遣和促销鸡尾酒会一样，重复多了就会变得乏味。亲密关系需要谨慎，因此受到父母、成人和孩子的排斥。社会不赞成坦诚，除非是在私下场合；常识告诉我们坦诚总是会被滥用；而孩子则因为坦诚意味着袒露心扉而感到恐惧。因此，为了摆脱消遣的乏味，又不想让自己陷入亲密关系的风险，大多数人会在有游戏的时候选择玩游戏，而这些游戏也占据了社交互动中大部分更有趣的时间。这就是游戏的社会意义。

4. People pick as friends, associates and intimates other people who play the same games. Hence ‘everybody who is anybody’ in a given social circle (aristocracy, juvenile gang, social club, college campus, etc.) behaves in a way which may seem quite foreign to members of a different social circle. Conversely, any member of a social circle who changes his games will tend to be extruded, but he will find himself welcome at some other social circle. That is the personal significance of games.

4. 人们倾向于选择那些和自己玩相同游戏的人作为朋友、伙伴和亲密伙伴。因此，在某个社交圈（例如贵族阶层、青少年团伙、社交俱乐部、大学校园等）中，“举足轻重”的人物的行为方式，在其他社交圈中可能显得格格不入。反之，任何改变游戏规则的社交圈成员都可能被排斥，但他会在其他社交圈中受到欢迎。这就是游戏对个人的意义所在。

NOTE

笔记

The reader should now be in a position to appreciate the basic difference between mathematical and transactional game analysis. Mathematical game analysis postulates players who are completely rational. Transactional game analysis deals with games which are un-rational, or even irrational, and hence more real.

读者现在应该能够理解数学博弈分析和交易博弈分析之间的基本区别。数学博弈分析假定参与者完全理性。而交易博弈分析处理的是非理性甚至无理性的博弈，因此更贴近现实。

#↩

14 · The Players

14 · 球员

M ANY games are played most intensely by disturbed people; generally speaking, the more disturbed they are, the harder they play. Curiously enough, however, some schizophrenics seem to refuse to play games, and demand candidness from the beginning. In everyday life games are played with the greatest conviction by two classes of individuals: the Sulks, and the Jerks or Squares.

许多游戏在精神障碍患者中玩得最为投入；一般来说，精神障碍越严重，他们玩得就越投入。然而，奇怪的是，一些精神分裂症患者似乎拒绝玩游戏，并且从一开始就要求坦诚相待。在日常生活中，最投入游戏的人分为两类：爱抱怨的人和傻瓜或古板。

The Sulk is a man who is angry at his mother. On investigation it emerges that he has been angry at her since early childhood. He often has good ‘Child’ reasons for his anger: she may have ‘deserted’ him during a critical period in his boyhood by getting sick and going to the hospital, or she may have given birth to too many siblings. Sometimes the desertion is more deliberate; she may have farmed him out in order to remarry. In any case, he has been sulking ever since. He does not like women, although he may be a Don Juan. Since sulking is deliberate at its inception, the decision to sulk can be reversed at any period of life, just as it can be during childhood when it comes time for dinner. The requirements for reversing the decision are the same for the grown-up Sulk as for the little boy. He must be able to save face, and he must be offered something worthwhile in exchange for the privilege of sulking. Sometimes a game of ‘Psychiatry’ which might otherwise last several years can be aborted by reversing a decision to sulk. This requires careful preparation of the patient and proper timing and approach. Clumsiness or bullying on the part of the therapist will have no better result than it does with a sulky little boy; in the long run, the patient will pay the therapist back for his mishandling just as the little boy will eventually repay clumsy parents.

“生闷气”的人通常对母亲怀恨在心。经调查发现，他从孩提时代就开始生母亲的气。他常常能找到一些“孩子气”的理由来解释自己的愤怒：比如，母亲可能在他童年的关键时期生病住院，从而“抛弃”了他；又或者，母亲可能生了太多弟妹。有时，母亲的抛弃是蓄意的，比如为了再婚而把他送走。无论如何，他从那时起就一直闷闷不乐。他不喜欢女人，尽管他可能是一个风流成性的花花公子。由于生闷气是蓄意的，因此，无论在人生的哪个阶段，生闷气的决定都可以改变，就像孩提时代到了吃饭时间一样。改变生闷气的决定，对于成年后的“生闷气者”和幼年时的“生闷气者”来说，需要满足的条件是一样的：他必须能够保住面子，并且必须得到一些有价值的东西来换取他生闷气的权利。有时，一场可能持续数年的“心理治疗”游戏，可以通过改变患者生闷气的决定而终止。这需要对患者进行周密的准备，并把握好时机和方法。治疗师的笨拙或霸道，其效果不会比对待一个生闷气的小男孩更好；从长远来看，患者会以其人之道还治其人之身，就像小男孩最终会惩罚笨拙的父母一样。

With female Sulks the situation is the same, mutatis mutandis, if they are angry at father. Their Wooden Leg (‘What do you expect of a woman who had a father like that?’) must be handled with even more diplomacy by a male therapist. Otherwise he risks being thrown into the wastebasket of ‘men who are like father’.

如果女性因为父亲而生气，那么她们的情绪低落情况也大同小异，只是略有不同。男性治疗师必须更加委婉地处理她们的抱怨（“你还能指望一个有这样父亲的女人怎么样？”）。否则，他很可能被归入“像父亲一样的男人”的行列。

There is a bit of Jerk in everyone, but the object of game analysis is to keep it at a minimum. A Jerk is someone who is overly sensitive to Parental influences. Hence his Adult data processing and his Child’s spontaneity are likely to be interfered with at critical moments, resulting in inappropriate or clumsy behaviour. In extreme cases the Jerk merges with the Toady, the Show-off, and the Cling. The Jerk is not to be confused with the bewildered schizophrenic, who has no functioning Parent and very little functioning Adult, so that he has to cope with the world in the ego state of a confused Child. It is interesting that in common usage ‘jerk’ is an epithet applied to men only, or in rare cases to masculine women. A Prig is even more of a Square than a Jerk; Prig is a word usually reserved for women, but occasionally it is said of men of somewhat feminine tendencies.

每个人身上都或多或少有些“混蛋”的特质，但游戏分析的目的在于将其控制在最低限度。“混蛋”指的是对父母角色影响过度敏感的人。因此，在关键时刻，他/她成人角色的信息处理能力和孩童角色的自发性都可能受到干扰，导致行为不当或笨拙。在极端情况下，“混蛋”会与阿谀奉承者、爱炫耀者和粘人者融为一体。“混蛋”不应与迷茫的精神分裂症患者混淆，后者缺乏有效的父母角色，成人角色也几乎无法正常运作，因此他/她只能以迷茫孩童的自我状态来应对这个世界。有趣的是，在日常用语中，“混蛋”一词通常仅用于形容男性，极少数情况下也用于形容具有男性气质的女性。“伪君子”比“混蛋”更像个老古板；“伪君子”一词通常用于形容女性，但偶尔也用来形容一些略带女性气质的男性。

#↩

15 · A Paradigm

15 · 范式

C ONSIDER the following exchange between a patient (P) and a therapist (T):

请考虑以下患者（P）和治疗师（T）之间的对话：

P. ‘I have a new project – being on time.’

P：“我有一个新项目——准时。”

T. ‘I’ll try to cooperate.’

T：“我会尽量配合。”

P. ‘I don’t care about you. I’m doing it for myself…. Guess what grade I got on my history test!’

P：“我不在乎你。我是为了我自己……猜猜我历史考试得了多少分！”

T. ‘B+.’

T. ‘B+。’

P. ‘How did you know?’

问：“你怎么知道的？”

T. ‘Because you’re afraid to get an A.’

T：“因为你害怕得A。”

P. ‘Yes, I had an A, and I went over my paper and crossed out three correct answers and put in three wrong ones.’

P：“是的，我得了A，然后我检查了我的试卷，划掉了三个正确的答案，换成了三个错误的答案。”

T. ‘I like this conversation. It’s Jerk-free.’

T：“我喜欢这种对话。没有混蛋。”

P. ‘You know, last night I was thinking how much progress I’ve made. I figured I was only 17 per cent Jerk now.’

P：“你知道吗，昨晚我一直在想我取得了多大的进步。我算了一下，我现在只剩下17%的混蛋成分了。”

T. ‘Well, so far this morning it’s zero, so you’re entitled to 34 per cent discount on the next round.’

T：“嗯，今天早上到目前为止是零，所以你下一轮可以享受 34% 的折扣。”

P. ‘It all began six months ago, that time I was looking at my coffeepot and for the first time I really saw it. And you know how it is now, how I hear the birds sing, and I look at people and they’re really there as people, and best of all, I’m really there. And I’m not only there, but right now I’m here. The other day I was standing in the art gallery looking at a picture, and a man came up and said, “Gauguin is very nice, isn’t he?” So I said: “I like you too.” So we went out and had a drink and he’s a very nice guy.’

P：“一切都始于六个月前，那时我看着我的咖啡壶，第一次真正地看到了它。你知道现在是什么感觉吗？我能听到鸟儿歌唱，我能看着人们，他们真的就在那里，像个人一样，最重要的是，我感觉自己也真的在那里。我不但感觉自己在那里，而且此刻我就在这里。前几天我站在美术馆里看画，一个男人走过来对我说：‘高更真不错，对吧？’我说：‘我也很喜欢你。’于是我们出去喝了杯酒，他真是个很友善的人。”

This is presented as a Jerk-free, game-free conversation between two autonomous Adults, with the following annotations:

本文以两个自主成年人之间不带任何恶意和游戏元素的对话形式呈现，并附有以下注释：

‘I have a new project – being on time.’ This announcement was made after the fact. The patient was nearly always late. This time she wasn’t. If punctuality had been a resolution, an act of ‘will power’, an imposition of the Parent on the Child, made only to be broken, it would have been announced before the fact: ‘This is the last time I’ll be late.’ That would have been an attempt to set up a game. Her announcement was not. It was an Adult decision, a project, not a resolution. The patient continued to be punctual.

“我有个新计划——准时。” 这句话是事后宣布的。这位病人几乎总是迟到。但这次她没有。如果守时是一种决心，一种“意志力”的体现，一种父母强加于孩子的、注定会被打破的规则，那么她应该在事前就宣布：“这是我最后一次迟到了。” 那会是一种试图和孩子玩的游戏。但她的宣布并非如此。这是一个成年人的决定，一个计划，而不是一个决心。这位病人继续保持着准时。

‘I’ll try to cooperate.’ This was not a ‘supportive’ statement, nor the first move in a new game of ‘I’m Only Trying to Help You.’ The patient’s hour came after the therapist’s coffee break. Since she was habitually late, he had fallen into the habit of taking his time and getting back late himself. When she made her declaration, he knew she meant it, and made his. The transaction was an Adult contract which both of them kept, and not a Child teasing a Parental figure who because of his position felt forced to be a ‘good daddy’ and say he would cooperate.

“我会尽量配合。” 这句话并非一句“支持”之言，也不是一场“我只是想帮你”游戏的开端。病人的治疗时间是在治疗师的咖啡休息时间之后。由于治疗师经常迟到，他也养成了拖延时间、迟到的习惯。当治疗师做出承诺时，他知道她是认真的，于是也做出了自己的承诺。这是一份双方都遵守的成人契约，而不是孩子戏弄长辈，长辈因为身份而被迫扮演“好爸爸”的角色，并说自己会配合。

‘I don’t care about you.’ This emphasizes that her punctuality is a decision, and not a resolution to be exploited as part of a pseudo-compliant game.

“我不在乎你。” 这句话强调，她的守时是一种选择，而不是一种可以被利用来玩弄伪顺从游戏的决心。

‘Guess what grade I got.’ This is a pastime which both were aware of and felt free to indulge in. There was no need for him to demonstrate how alert he was by telling her it was a pastime, some thing she already knew, and there was no need for her to refrain from playing it just because it was called a pastime.

“猜猜我考了多少分。”这是他们俩都知道的消遣，而且都乐于参与。他没必要特意告诉她这是消遣，以此来证明自己有多机敏，因为她早就知道了；而她也没必要因为这叫消遣就阻止自己玩。

‘B+.’ The therapist reckoned that in her case this was the only possible grade, and there was no reason not to say so. False modesty or a fear of being wrong might have led him to pretend that he did not know.

“B+。”治疗师认为，就她的情况而言，这是唯一可能的成绩，没有理由不这么说。虚伪的谦虚或害怕犯错可能会让他假装不知道。

‘How did you know?’ This was an Adult question, not a game of ‘Gee You’re Wonderful’, and it deserved a pertinent answer.

“你怎么知道的？”这是一个成年人的问题，而不是“哇，你真棒”之类的吹捧游戏，它需要一个恰当的回答。

‘Yes, I had an A.’ This was the real test. The patient did not sulk with rationalizations or pleas, but faced her Child squarely.

“是的，我得了A。”这才是真正的考验。病人没有找借口或哀求，而是直面她的孩子。

‘I like this conversation.’ This and the following semi-facetious remarks were expressions of mutual Adult respect, with perhaps a little Parent-Child pastime, which again was optional with both of them, and of which they were both aware.

“我喜欢这种谈话。”这句话以及接下来半开玩笑的话语，都表达了成年人之间的相互尊重，或许还带有一丝亲子间的玩笑意味，当然，这对于他们两人来说都是可选项，而且他们也都心知肚明。

‘For the first time I really saw it.’ She is now entitled to her own kind of awareness and is no longer obliged to see coffeepots and people the way her parents told her to. ‘Right now I’m here.’ She no longer lives in the future or the past, but can discuss them briefly if it serves a useful purpose.

“我第一次真正看清了这一切。”她现在有权拥有自己的感知，不再需要像父母教导的那样去看待咖啡壶和人。“此刻，我就在这里。”她不再活在未来或过去，但如果有必要，她也可以简要地谈论它们。

‘I said: “I like you too.” She is not obliged to waste time playing ‘Art Gallery’ with the newcomer, although she could if she chose to.

我说：“我也喜欢你。”她没有义务浪费时间陪这位新来者玩“艺术画廊”游戏，尽管她如果愿意也可以这么做。

The therapist, on his part, does not feel obliged to play ‘Psychiatry’. There were several opportunities to bring up questions of defence, transference and symbolic interpretation, but he was able to let these go by without feeling any anxiety. It did seem worthwhile, however, to ascertain for future reference which answers she crossed out on her examination. During the rest of the hour, unfortunately, the 17 per cent of Jerk left in the patient and the 18 per cent left in the therapist showed from time to time. In summary, the proceedings given constitute an activity enlightened with some pastime.

治疗师本人并不觉得有义务扮演“精神病学家”的角色。他曾多次有机会提出关于防御机制、移情和象征性解释的问题，但他都能坦然面对，没有感到任何焦虑。不过，记录下她在答题卡上划掉的答案，以备将来参考，似乎还是很有必要的。不幸的是，在接下来的一个小时里，患者身上残留的17%的“混蛋”和治疗师身上残留的18%的“混蛋”时不时地显露出来。总而言之，整个过程构成了一场略带娱乐性的活动。

#↩

16 · Autonomy

16. 自主性

T HE attainment of autonomy is manifested by the release or recovery of three capacities: awareness, spontaneity and intimacy.

获得自主性表现为三种能力的释放或恢复：意识、自发性和亲密性。

Awareness. Awareness means the capacity to see a coffeepot and hear the birds sing in one’s own way, and not the way one was taught. It may be assumed on good grounds that seeing and hearing have a different quality for infants than for grownups, 1 and that they are more aesthetic and less intellectual in the first years of life. A little boy sees and hears birds with delight. Then the ‘good father’ comes along and feels he should ‘share’ the experience and help his son ‘develop’. He says: ‘That’s a jay, and this is a sparrow.’ The moment the little boy is concerned with which is a jay and which is a sparrow, he can no longer see the birds or hear them sing. He has to see and hear them the way his father wants him to. Father has good reasons on his side, since few people can afford to go through life listening to the birds sing, and the sooner the little boy starts his ‘education’ the better. Maybe he will be an ornithologist when he grows up. A few people, however, can still see and hear in the old way. But most of the members of the human race have lost the capacity to be painters, poets or musicians, and are not left the option of seeing and hearing directly even if they can afford to; they must get it secondhand. The recovery of this ability is called here ‘awareness’. Physiologically awareness is eidetic perception, allied to eidetic imagery. 2 Perhaps there is also eidetic perception, at least in certain individuals, in the spheres of taste, smell and kinesthesia, giving us the artists in those fields: chefs, perfumers and dancers, whose eternal problem is to find audiences capable of appreciating their products.

觉察力。觉察力意味着能够以自己的方式去观察咖啡壶、聆听鸟儿的歌唱，而不是按照别人教给他的方式去理解。我们可以合理地假设，对于婴儿来说，视觉和听觉的特质与成人不同，在生命最初的几年里，视觉和听觉更多地体现在审美层面而非理性层面。一个小男孩兴高采烈地观察和聆听鸟儿。这时，“好父亲”出现了，觉得他应该“分享”这种体验，帮助儿子“成长”。他说：“那是只松鸦，那是只麻雀。” 小男孩一旦开始纠结于哪个是松鸦哪个是麻雀，他就再也无法观察和聆听鸟儿了。他必须按照父亲希望的方式去观察和聆听。父亲的做法不无道理，因为很少有人能一生都沉浸在聆听鸟儿歌唱的乐趣中，小男孩越早开始接受“教育”越好。也许他长大后会成为一名鸟类学家。然而，少数人仍然能够像过去那样看和听。但大多数人已经丧失了成为画家、诗人或音乐家的能力，即使他们有能力，也无法直接去看和去听；他们只能通过间接的方式获得。这种能力的恢复在这里被称为“意识”。从生理学角度来看，意识是图像感知，与图像记忆密切相关。或许在某些人身上，味觉、嗅觉和动觉领域也存在图像感知，这造就了这些领域的艺术家：厨师、调香师和舞蹈家，他们永恒的难题是如何找到能够欣赏他们作品的观众。

Awareness requires living in the here and now, and not in the elsewhere, the past or the future. A good illustration of possibilities in American life, is driving to work in the morning in a hurry. The decisive question is: ‘Where is the mind when the body is here? and there are three common cases.

觉察需要活在当下，而不是活在别处、过去或未来。美国生活中一个很好的例子就是早上匆匆开车上班。关键问题是：“当身体在这里时，心在哪里？” 这种情况通常有三种。

1. The man whose chief preoccupation is being on time is the one who is furthest out. With his body at the wheel of his car, his mind is at the door of his office, and he is oblivious to his immediate surroundings except insofar as they are obstacles to the moment when his soma will catch up with his psyche. This is the Jerk, whose chief concern is how it will look to the boss. If he is late, he will take pains to arrive out of breath. The compliant Child is in command, and his game is ‘Look How Hard I’ve Tried’. While he is driving, he is almost completely lacking in autonomy, and as a human being he is in essence more dead than alive. It is quite possible that this is the most favourable condition for the development of hypertension or coronary disease.

1. 那些一心只想准时的人，往往最不专注。他的身体坐在方向盘后，心思却早已飞到了办公室门口，对周围的一切都漠不关心，除非它们会阻碍他的身体追上他的精神。这种人就是个混蛋，他最关心的是如何给老板留下好印象。如果他迟到了，他会故意气喘吁吁地赶到。顺从的孩子掌控着一切，他的游戏规则是“看我多么努力”。当他开车时，他几乎完全丧失了自主性，作为一个人，他实际上更像是行尸走肉。这很可能是高血压或冠心病最容易发生的条件。

2. The Sulk, on the other hand, is not so much concerned with arriving on time as in collecting excuses for being late. Mishaps, badly timed lights and poor driving or stupidity on the part of others fit well into his scheme and are secretly welcomed as contributions to his rebellious Child or righteous Parent game of ‘Look What They Made Me Do’. He, too, is oblivious to his surroundings except as they subscribe to his game, so that he is only half alive. His body is in his car, but his mind is out searching for blemishes and injustices.

2. 而“闷闷不乐”的人则不然，他更关心的不是准时到达，而是收集迟到的借口。意外事故、糟糕的红绿灯、驾驶技术差劲或他人的愚蠢行为，都正合他意，被他暗中视为“看他们都逼我干了些什么”游戏中的素材，让他得以扮演叛逆的孩子或自以为是的家长。他也对周围环境漠不关心，除非周围的一切都符合他的游戏规则，所以他只是半死不活。他的身体在车里，但他的心思却在外面寻找瑕疵和不公。

3. Less common is the ‘natural driver’, the man to whom driving a car is a congenial science and art. As he makes his way swiftly and skilfully through the traffic, he is at one with his vehicle. He, too, is oblivious of his surroundings except as they offer scope for the craftsmanship which is its own reward, but he is very much aware of himself and the machine which he controls so well, and to that extent he is alive. Such driving is formally an Adult pastime from which his Child and Parent may also derive satisfaction.

3. 较为少见的是“天生驾驶者”，对他们而言，驾驶汽车既是一门技艺精湛的科学，也是一门艺术。当他们娴熟地穿梭于车流之中时，仿佛人车合一。他们也对周围环境浑然不觉，除非周围环境为他们提供了施展技艺的舞台——而这本身就是一种享受。但他们对自身以及自己操控自如的车辆却有着清醒的认知，正是这种认知让他们感到鲜活。这种驾驶方式传统上是成年人的消遣，但他们的孩子和父母也能从中获得乐趣。

4. The fourth case is the person who is aware, and who will not hurry because he is living in the present moment with the environment which is here: the sky and the trees as well as the feeling of motion. To hurry is to neglect that environment and to be conscious only of something that is still out of sight down the road, or of mere obstacles, or solely of oneself. A Chinese man started to get into a local subway train, when his Caucasian companion pointed out that they could save twenty minutes by taking an express, which they did. When they got off at Central Park, the Chinese man sat down on a bench, much to his friend’s surprise. ‘Well,’ explained the former, ‘since we saved twenty minutes, we can afford to sit here that long and enjoy our surroundings.’

第四种情况是，一个人如果能够觉察当下，就不会匆忙行事，因为他活在当下，感受着周围的环境：天空、树木，以及运动的感觉。匆忙意味着忽略周围的环境，只关注前方看不见的东西、路障，或者仅仅是自己。一位中国男子正要登上地铁，他的白人同伴指出，他们可以乘坐快车节省二十分钟，于是他们就这么做了。当他们在中央公园下车时，中国男子坐在长椅上，这让他的朋友颇感意外。“嗯，”他解释说，“既然我们节省了二十分钟，我们就可以在这里坐这么久，好好欣赏一下周围的景色。”

The aware person is alive because he knows how he feels, where he is and when it is. He knows that after he dies the trees will still be there, but he will not be there to look at them again, so he wants to see them now with as much poignancy as possible.

有觉知的人之所以活着，是因为他知道自己的感受，知道自己身处何地，以及何时发生。他知道死后树木依然会在那里，但他将无法再亲眼目睹，所以他想尽可能深刻地感受当下，好好欣赏它们。

Spontaneity. Spontaneity means option, the freedom to choose and express one’s feelings from the assortment available (Parent feelings, Adult feelings and Child feelings). It means liberation, liberation from the compulsion to play games and have only the feelings one was taught to have.

自发性。自发性意味着选择，意味着能够自由地从各种情感（父母的情感、成人的情感和孩童的情感）中选择并表达自己的情感。它意味着解放，从被迫玩弄游戏、只能拥有被教导拥有的情感中解放出来。

Intimacy. Intimacy means the spontaneous, game-free candidness of an aware person, the liberation of the eidetically perceptive, uncorrupted Child in all its naïveté living in the here and now. It can be shown experimentally 3 that eidetic perception evokes affection, and that candidness mobilizes positive feelings, so that there is even such a thing as ‘one-sided intimacy’ – a phenomenon well known, although not by that name, to professional seducers who are able to capture their partners without becoming involved themselves. This they do by encouraging the other person to look at them directly and to talk freely, while the male or female seducer makes only a well-guarded pretence of reciprocating.

亲密。亲密意味着一个觉察之人自发的、不加掩饰的坦诚，意味着那个拥有超凡感知力、纯真无邪的孩童，在此时此地释放出所有的天真。实验可以证明，超凡的感知力能够唤起爱意，坦诚能够激发积极的情感，因此甚至存在“单向亲密”这种现象——这种现象虽然不被称为“单向亲密”，但职业诱惑者对此却十分熟悉。他们能够俘获伴侣的心，却不必真正投入其中。他们通过鼓励对方直视自己、畅所欲言来达到目的，而男性或女性诱惑者则只是小心翼翼地假装回应。

Because intimacy is essentially a function of the natural Child (although expressed in a matrix of psychological and social complications), it tends to turn out well if not disturbed by the intervention of games. Usually the adaptation to Parental influences is what spoils it, and most unfortunately this is almost a universal occurrence. But before, unless and until they are corrupted, most infants seem to be loving, 4 and that is the essential nature of intimacy, as shown experimentally.

因为亲密关系本质上是儿童天性（尽管它表现为一系列心理和社会因素的复杂交织）的一种功能，所以如果不受到游戏的干扰，它往往会发展良好。通常，对父母影响的适应会破坏这种亲密关系，而不幸的是，这种情况几乎普遍存在。但在被“腐蚀”之前，大多数婴儿似乎都充满爱意，而这正是亲密关系的本质，实验也证实了这一点。

#↩

17 · The Attainment of Autonomy

17. 获得自主权

P ARENTS , deliberately or unaware, teach their children from birth how to behave, think, feel and perceive. Liberation from these influences is no easy matter, since they are deeply ingrained and are necessary during the first two or three decades of life for biological and social survival. Indeed, such liberation is only possible at all because the individual starts off in an autonomous state, that is, capable of awareness, spontaneity and intimacy, and he has some discretion as to which parts of his parents’ teachings he will accept. At certain specific moments early in life he decides how he is going to adapt to them. It is because his adaptation is in the nature of a series of decisions that it can be undone, since decisions are reversible under favourable circumstances.

父母有意或无意地从孩子出生起就教导他们如何行事、思考、感受和感知。摆脱这些影响并非易事，因为它们根深蒂固，并且在生命的前二三十年对于生物和社会生存至关重要。事实上，这种摆脱之所以成为可能，是因为个体最初处于一种自主状态，也就是说，他们拥有意识、自发性和亲密感，并且能够自主选择接受父母教诲的哪些部分。在生命早期的某些特定时刻，他们会决定如何适应这些教诲。正因为这种适应本质上是一系列选择的结果，所以它才有可能被逆转，因为在有利的情况下，这些选择是可以改变的。

The attainment of autonomy, then, consists of the overthrow of all those irrelevancies discussed in Chapters 13 , 14 and 15 . And such overthrow is never final: there is a continual battle against sinking back into the old ways.

因此，获得自主权意味着推翻第 13、14 和 15 章中讨论的所有无关紧要的事情。而且这种推翻永远不会是最终的：要不断地与退回到旧方式作斗争。

First, as discussed in Chapter 13 , the weight of a whole tribal or family historical tradition has to be lifted, as in the case of Margaret Mead’s villagers in New Guinea; 1 then the influence of the individual parental, social and cultural background has to be thrown off. The same must be done with the demands of contemporary society at large, and finally the advantages derived from one’s immediate social circle have to be partly or wholly sacrificed. Then all the easy indulgences and rewards of being a Sulk or a Jerk, as described in Chapter 14 , have to be given up. Following this, the individual must attain personal and social control, so that all the classes of behaviour described in the Appendix, except perhaps dreams, become free choices subject only to his will. He is then ready for game-free relationships such as that illustrated in the paradigm in Chapter 15 . At this point he may be able to develop his capacities for autonomy. In essence, this whole preparation consists of obtaining a friendly divorce from one’s parents (and from other Parental influences) so that they may be agreeably visited on occasion, but are no longer dominant.

首先，正如第十三章所述，必须卸下整个部落或家族历史传统的重担，就像玛格丽特·米德在新几内亚的村民那样；其次，必须摆脱个人父母、社会和文化背景的影响。同样，也必须摆脱当代社会的各种要求，最后，必须部分或全部放弃从个人社交圈中获得的利益。然后，正如第十四章所述，必须放弃所有因耍脾气或做混蛋而获得的轻松放纵和好处。之后，个人必须获得自我控制和社会控制，这样，附录中描述的所有行为类型（也许除了梦境之外）都将成为完全受其意志支配的自由选择。这时，他就可以建立像第十五章范例中所示的无游戏式的人际关系。此时，他或许能够发展出自主能力。从本质上讲，整个准备过程包括与父母（以及其他父母的影响）友好地断绝关系，以便偶尔可以愉快地拜访他们，但不再拥有支配权。

REFERENCE

参考

1. Mead, M., New Lives for Old, Gollancz, 1956.

1. Mead, M.，《老年人的新生活》，Gollancz，1956 年。

#↩

18 · After Games, What?

18. 比赛结束后，做什么？

T HE sombre picture presented in Parts I and II of this book, in which human life is mainly a process of filling in time until the arrival of death, or Santa Claus, with very little choice, if any, of what kind of business one is going to transact during the long wait, is a commonplace but not the final answer. For certain fortunate people there is something which transcends all classifications of behaviour, and that is awareness; something which rises above the programming of the past, and that is spontaneity; and something that is more rewarding than games, and that is intimacy. But all three of these may be frightening and even perilous to the unprepared. Perhaps they are better off as they are, seeking their solutions in popular techniques of social action, such as ‘togetherness’. This may mean that there is no hope for the human race, but there is hope for individual members of it.

本书第一部分和第二部分描绘的这幅阴郁图景——人类生活主要就是在等待死亡或圣诞老人到来之前，虚度光阴，而对于在漫长的等待中究竟要处理什么事情，几乎没有选择余地——虽然老生常谈，但并非最终答案。对于某些幸运儿而言，有一种东西超越了所有行为的分类，那就是觉察；有一种东西超越了过往的束缚，那就是自发性；有一种东西比游戏更有意义，那就是亲密关系。然而，对于毫无准备的人来说，这三者都可能令人恐惧，甚至充满危险。或许他们最好还是保持现状，在诸如“团结”之类的社会行动中寻求解决之道。这或许意味着人类整体已无希望，但对于个体而言，希望犹存。

The Classification of Behaviour

行为分类

A T any given moment a human being is engaged in one or more of the following classes of behaviour:

在任何特定时刻，人类都可能从事以下一种或多种行为：

C LASS I. Internally programmed (archaeopsychic). Autistic behaviour.

第一类：内在程序（古心理）。自闭症行为。

Orders :

订单：

( a ) Dreams.

（a）梦。

( b ) Fantasies.

（b）幻想。

Families:

家庭：

i. Extraneous fantasies (wish fulfilment).

i. 无关的幻想（愿望实现）。

ii. Autistic transactions, Unadapted.

ii. 自闭症交易，未经改编。

iii. Autistic transactions, Adapted (with neopsychic programming).

iii. 自闭症交易，改编版（采用新心理编程）。

( c ) Fugues.

（c）赋格曲。

( d ) Delusional behaviour.

（d）妄想行为。

( e ) Involuntary actions.

（e）非自愿行为。

( e ) Involuntary actions.

（e）非自愿行为。

Families:

家庭：

i. Tics.

i. 抽动症。

ii. Mannerisms.

二、矫饰主义。

iii. Parapraxes.

iii. 语无伦次。

( f ) Others.

（f）其他。

C LASS II. Probability programmed (neopsychic). Reality-tested behaviour.

第二类。概率编程（新心理学）。经现实检验的行为。

Orders :

订单：

( a ) Activities.

（a）活动。

Families:

家庭：

i. Professions, trades, etc.

一、职业、行业等

二、运动、爱好等。

（b）程序。

（c）其他。

第三类：社会程序化（部分外在心理因素）。社会行为。

订单：

( a ) Rituals and ceremonies.

（a）仪式和庆典。

（b）消遣。

（c）作战和演习。

（d）游戏。

Suborders: A. Professional games (angular transactions).

子订单：A. 专业游戏（Angular 交易）。

B. Social games (duplex transactions).

B. 社交游戏（双重交易）。

( e ) Intimacy.

（e）亲密关系。

In this scheme the social games previously discussed would be classified as follows: Class III, Socially programmed; Order ( d ), Games; Suborder B, Social Games

在此方案中，先前讨论的社交游戏将按以下方式分类：第三类，社会程序化游戏；（d）类，游戏；B子类，社交游戏

Intimacy, ‘the end of the line’, is the final classification, and is part of game-free living.

亲密关系，作为“终点”，是最终的分类，也是无游戏生活的一部分。

The reader should feel free to carp (but not to gleek or fleer) at the above classification. It is included not because the writer is in love with it, but because it is more functional, real and practical than other systems now in use and can be helpful to those who like or need taxonomy.

读者可以随意对上述分类提出批评意见（但请勿幸灾乐祸或轻蔑对待）。之所以列出此分类，并非因为作者对其情有独钟，而是因为它比目前使用的其他系统更实用、更真实、更易于理解，并且对那些喜欢或需要分类学的人有所帮助。
